

=== COX'S BAZAR ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Cox's Bazar is famous for having the world's longest unbroken...
A) Mountain range
B) Mangrove forest
C) Natural sea beach
D) Coral reef
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Natural sea beach

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar is located in the Sylhet Division of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in the Chittagong Division).

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate length of the main beach at Cox's Bazar?
A) 50 km
B) 80 km
C) 120 km
D) 200 km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 120 km

Q4. [MCQ] The town of Cox's Bazar is named after...
A) A British naval officer
B) A local king
C) A type of bird
D) A famous explorer
CORRECT ANSWER: A) A British naval officer (Captain Hiram Cox)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Himchari National Park, known for its waterfalls and hills, is located near Cox's Bazar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these is a popular tourist island located near Cox's Bazar, known for its coral?
A) Bhola Island
B) St. Martin's Island
C) Hatiya Island
D) Sandwip Island
CORRECT ANSWER: B) St. Martin's Island

Q7. [MCQ] Besides tourism, what is another major industry in Cox's Bazar?
A) Steel production
B) Garment manufacturing
C) Fishing and seafood processing
D) Software development
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Fishing and seafood processing

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Burmese Market" in Cox's Bazar sells products primarily imported from neighboring India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It sells products from Myanmar/Burma, Thailand, and China).

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the main beach area in Cox's Bazar town?
A) Laboni Beach
B) Patenga Beach
C) Kuakata Beach
D) Inani Beach
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Laboni Beach

Q10. [MCQ] The Aggmeda Khyang in Cox's Bazar is a prominent...
A) Waterfall
B) Buddhist monastery
C) Hindu temple
D) Fish market
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Buddhist monastery

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Captain Hiram Cox, after whom the town is named, was an officer of which company?
A) Dutch East India Company
B) French East India Company
C) British East India Company
D) Portuguese Empire
CORRECT ANSWER: C) British East India Company

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Inani Beach, part of the larger Cox's Bazar beach, is famous for its black sand.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is famous for its golden sand and large coral boulders).

Q3. [MCQ] The town of Ramu, near Cox's Bazar, is particularly known for its large population of...
A) Hindu priests
B) Buddhist monks and monasteries
C) Christian missionaries
D) Sufi mystics
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Buddhist monks and monasteries

Q4. [MCQ] The vast refugee camps in the Ukhiya and Teknaf upazilas of Cox's Bazar primarily shelter which ethnic group?
A) Chakma
B) Rohingya
C) Marma
D) Rakhine
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rohingya

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar was known by the name "Palongkee" before it was renamed.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The climate of Cox's Bazar is best described as...
A) Tropical monsoon
B) Arid desert
C) Temperate maritime
D) Humid continental
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Tropical monsoon

Q7. [MCQ] Which major river flows into the Bay of Bengal near Cox's Bazar?
A) Karnaphuli
B) Naf
C) Sangu
D) Matamuhuri
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Naf (The Naf River estuary separates Cox's Bazar/Teknaf from Myanmar).

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] St. Martin's Island is the only coral island in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is "Shutki," a famous and pungent local product of Cox's Bazar?
A) Fermented tea leaves
B) Dried fish
C) Spiced tamarind
D) Woven handicrafts
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dried fish

Q10. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in Cox's Bazar District?
A) 4
B) 6
C) 8
D) 10
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 8 (Cox's Bazar Sadar, Chakaria, Kutubdia, Ukhiya, Moheshkhali, Pekua, Ramu, Teknaf)

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Cox's Bazar District?
A) 1,820 sq km
B) 2,492 sq km
C) 3,140 sq km
D) 4,050 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,492 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rakhine people, who are a significant ethnic minority in Cox's Bazar, originally migrated from the Arakan region of modern-day Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Cox's Bazar District is bordered by Chittagong District to the north, Bandarban District to the east, the Bay of Bengal to the west, and...
A) Khagrachari District
B) The Naf River and Myanmar
C) Feni District
D) The Indian state of Mizoram
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Naf River and Myanmar

Q4. [MCQ] The island of Moheshkhali, within Cox's Bazar District, is famous for the Adinath Temple, which is dedicated to...
A) Vishnu
B) Shiva
C) Krishna
D) Brahma
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shiva

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] As of October 2025, the Matarbari deep-sea port, a major development project in Cox's Bazar District, is fully operational and handling large container ships.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (Significant progress and partial operations have been achieved by this date).

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the wildlife sanctuary near Teknaf that is one of the last remaining habitats for Asian elephants in Bangladesh?
A) Himchari National Park
B) Teknaf Wildlife Sanctuary
C) Sangu Wildlife Sanctuary
D) Bhawal National Park
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Teknaf Wildlife Sanctuary

Q7. [MCQ] The literacy rate of Cox's Bazar District, according to the 2022 census, was significantly lower than the national average, at approximately...
A) 39.7%
B) 51.5%
C) 62.4%
D) 74.7%
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 62.4% (While lower than Dhaka, this reflects the 2022 census data).

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar District has a higher population of shrimp and salt farming fields than any other district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The average elevation of Cox's Bazar town is approximately...
A) 3 meters
B) 25 meters
C) 50 meters
D) 100 meters
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 3 meters

Q10. [MCQ] In what year was Cox's Bazar subdivision (mahakuma) established during British rule?
A) 1799
B) 1854
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1854

=== SYLHET ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Sylhet is the largest city in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Chittagong Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Sylhet Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sylhet Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Sylhet is famous for its vast tea gardens, which are a major part of Bangladesh's tea industry.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the major river that flows through Sylhet city?
A) Padma
B) Surma
C) Jamuna
D) Tista
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Surma

Q4. [MCQ] The shrine of which famous Sufi saint is a major pilgrimage site in Sylhet?
A) Shah Makhdum
B) Khan Jahan Ali
C) Shah Jalal
D) Bayazid Bostami
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Jalal

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The local dialect spoken in Sylhet, known as Sylheti, is identical to the standard Bengali spoken in Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a distinct dialect, sometimes considered a separate language by linguists).

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these is a popular tourist spot near Sylhet, known for its stone collection activities?
A) Jaflong
B) Kuakata
C) Sundarbans
D) Paharpur
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Jaflong

Q7. [MCQ] Malnicherra Tea Estate in Sylhet is famous for being...
A) The largest in the world
B) The oldest in the subcontinent
C) The highest in elevation
D) Owned by a famous actor
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The oldest in the subcontinent (established in 1854)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] A large number of people from the Sylhet region have migrated to the United Kingdom, especially London.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the freshwater swamp forest near Sylhet, often called the "Amazon of Bengal"?
A) Ratargul
B) Sundarbans
C) Bhawal Forest
D) Madhupur Tract
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Ratargul

Q10. [MCQ] What citrus fruit, a key ingredient in "Shatkora" beef curry, is famous in Sylhet?
A) Orange
B) Lemon
C) Shatkora (a type of wild orange)
D) Pomelo
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shatkora (a type of wild orange)

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The historical name of the greater Sylhet region was...
A) Gauda
B) Vanga
C) Pundravardhana
D) Srihatta
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Srihatta

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The indigenous Khasia and Manipuri communities live in the hilly areas of the greater Sylhet region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What was the "Sylhet Referendum" of 1947?
A) A vote to join the Liberation War
B) A vote to decide whether to join Pakistan or India
C) A vote to establish a new university
D) A vote to ban tea cultivation
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A vote to decide whether to join Pakistan or India

Q4. [MCQ] The Tanguar Haor, a major wetland and UNESCO site, is located in which district of Sylhet Division?
A) Sylhet District
B) Habiganj District
C) Moulvibazar District
D) Sunamganj District
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sunamganj District

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Osmani International Airport, located in Sylhet, is named after General M. A. G. Osmani, the Commander-in-Chief of the Bangladesh Forces during the 1971 Liberation War.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in Sylhet District?
A) 9
B) 11
C) 13
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 13

Q7. [MCQ] The Surma and Kushiara rivers are branches of which larger river system?
A) Brahmaputra-Jamuna
B) Ganges-Padma
C) Barak River
D) Tista River
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barak River

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The traditional "Dhamail" is a form of folk music and dance primarily performed by men in the Sylhet region.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is primarily performed by women during weddings and other ceremonies).

Q9. [MCQ] Which of these is a major natural gas field located in Sylhet District?
A) Titas
B) Bibiyana
C) Haripur
D) Bakhrabad
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Haripur (It was the first gas field discovered in Bangladesh).

Q10. [MCQ] The tomb of Shah Paran, a companion and nephew of Shah Jalal, is also a significant pilgrimage site located near...
A) Jaflong
B) Sylhet city
C) Tamabil
D) Ratargul
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sylhet city

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Sylhet District?
A) 2,800 sq km
B) 3,452 sq km
C) 4,100 sq km
D) 5,200 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 3,452 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Sylhet was briefly part of the state of Assam during British rule, which is why the 1947 referendum was held to decide its fate.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] In what year did the great earthquake occur that significantly altered the topography of Sylhet, including the creation of many "haors" (wetlands)?
A) 1762
B) 1897
C) 1950
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1897 (The Great Assam Earthquake)

Q4. [MCQ] The Sylheti Nagari script was a unique writing system developed specifically for...
A) Writing official court documents
B) Writing religious poetry and folk tales in the Sylheti language
C) Carving inscriptions on temples
D) Sending secret messages during wartime
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Writing religious poetry and folk tales in the Sylheti language

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Sylhet District, according to the 2022 census, was approximately 70.9%.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Shah Jalal is said to have arrived in Sylhet in which year, after defeating the local ruler Gour Govinda?
A) 1204
B) 1303
C) 1450
D) 1576
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1303

Q7. [MCQ] What is the "Jaintia Kingdom"?
A) A modern-day political party
B) A mythical land in Sylheti folklore
C) A historical kingdom that once encompassed parts of Sylhet and Meghalaya
D) A chain of tea estates
CORRECT ANSWER: C) A historical kingdom that once encompassed parts of Sylhet and Meghalaya

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Sylhet District does not share a direct international border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It shares a border with the Indian state of Meghalaya).

Q9. [MCQ] The Kean Bridge, an iron bridge over the Surma River in Sylhet city, was built in 1936 and named after...
A) A local freedom fighter
B) A British Governor of Assam
C) A Sufi saint
D) A type of local bird
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A British Governor of Assam (Sir Michael Keane)

Q10. [MCQ] What geological feature is responsible for the formation of the small hills ("tilas") scattered around Sylhet?
A) Volcanic activity
B) Glacial deposits
C) Tectonic uplift (part of the Indo-Burman Range)
D) Wind erosion
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tectonic uplift (part of the Indo-Burman Range)

=== RANGAMATI ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Rangamati is a district in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka
B) Sylhet
C) Chittagong
D) Barisal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Rangamati is part of a special administrative region known as the Chittagong Hill Tracts.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the large, man-made lake that is the central geographical feature of Rangamati?
A) Kaptai Lake
B) Boga Lake
C) Foy's Lake
D) Ashulia Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Kaptai Lake

Q4. [MCQ] The "Hanging Bridge" (Jhulonto Shetu) is the most famous tourist landmark in...
A) Dhaka
B) Rangamati
C) Cox's Bazar
D) Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rangamati

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The population of Rangamati is almost entirely ethnic Bengali.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It has a large population of various indigenous (Jumma) peoples, such as the Chakma, Marma, and Tanchangya).

Q6. [MCQ] Which is the largest indigenous ethnic group in the Rangamati district?
A) Marma
B) Tripura
C) Chakma
D) Santal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chakma

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the prominent Buddhist monastery (vihara) in Rangamati?
A) Aggmeda Khyang
B) Rajbana Vihara
C) Somapura Mahavihara
D) Shalban Vihara
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rajbana Vihara

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Rangamati is a flat, coastal district known for its beaches.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a hilly, forested, and landlocked district).

Q9. [MCQ] What is the "Shuvolong Waterfall"?
A) A popular waterfall in Rangamati, best visited in the rainy season
B) A major hydro-electric dam
C) A type of local boat
D) A cultural festival
CORRECT ANSWER: A) A popular waterfall in Rangamati, best visited in the rainy season

Q10. [MCQ] The traditional mode of transport for many people in Rangamati, due to the lake, is by...
A) Rickshaw
B) Horse carriage
C) Engine boat
D) Cable car
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Engine boat

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Kaptai Lake was created in 1962 as a result of the construction of the...
A) Teesta Barrage
B) Farakka Barrage
C) Karnafuli Hydro-Electric Project
D) Bhakra-Nangal Dam
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Karnafuli Hydro-Electric Project

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The creation of Kaptai Lake submerged a vast area of land, including the old palace of the Chakma King.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is "Biju"?
A) The traditional New Year festival celebrated by the Chakma and Tanchangya peoples
B) A type of spicy curry
C) A bamboo handicraft
D) The local name for Kaptai Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The traditional New Year festival celebrated by the Chakma and Tanchangya peoples

Q4. [MCQ] Rangamati is the only district in Bangladesh that has international borders with...
A) Only Myanmar
B) Only India
C) Both India and Myanmar
D) Neither India nor Myanmar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Only India (specifically the states of Mizoram and Tripura).

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chittagong Hill Tracts Peace Accord, aimed at ending the long-running insurgency, was signed in 1997.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the administrative headquarters of the "Chakma Circle," one of the three traditional circles in the Hill Tracts?
A) Bandarban
B) Khagrachari
C) Rangamati
D) Cox's Bazar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangamati

Q7. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in Rangamati District?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 10

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jhum (slash-and-burn) cultivation is a traditional agricultural practice in the hilly areas of Rangamati.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which of these is a lesser-known but beautiful lake in Barkal Upazila of Rangamati?
A) Boga Lake
B) Pablakhali Lake
C) Matamuhuri Lake
D) Sangu Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pablakhali Lake (within Pablakhali Wildlife Sanctuary)

Q10. [MCQ] What is the local name for the small, brightly colored, open-roofed taxis popular in Rangamati town?
A) Tomtom
B) CNG
C) Chander Gari (Moon Car)
D) Mishuk
CORRECT ANSWER: B) CNG (though "Chander Gari" refers to the larger 4x4 jeeps).

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Rangamati is the largest district in Bangladesh by area. What is its approximate area?
A) 3,120 sq km
B) 4,800 sq km
C) 6,116 sq km
D) 8,200 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 6,116 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate in Rangamati District, according to the 2022 census, is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was 70.8%, which is below the national average of 74.66%).

Q3. [MCQ] In what year was the Chittagong Hill Tracts Regulation (also known as the CHT Manual) promulgated, establishing a separate administrative status for the region?
A) 1860
B) 1900
C) 1947
D) 1972
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1900

Q4. [MCQ] The Kaptai Dam, which created the lake, was built with financial and technical assistance from which country?
A) Soviet Union
B) China
C) United States
D) United Kingdom
CORRECT ANSWER: C) United States

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Sajek Valley, a very popular tourist destination often associated with Rangamati, is administratively located in Baghaichari Upazila of Rangamati district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Who was the political leader and Member of Parliament from Rangamati who was assassinated in 1984?
A) Manabendra Narayan Larma
B) Prasit Bikash Khisa
C) M. N. Larma
D) Charu Bikash Chakma
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Manabendra Narayan Larma (He was the founder of the Parbatya Chattagram Jana Samhati Samiti).

Q7. [MCQ] The highest peak in Bangladesh, Tazing Dong (or Saka Haphong, depending on the survey), is located in which neighboring district to Rangamati?
A) Khagrachari
B) Bandarban
C) Chittagong
D) Cox's Bazar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bandarban

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chakma language has its own unique script, known as the Chakma script or "Ojhopath."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What percentage of the total land area of Rangamati District was submerged by the creation of Kaptai Lake?
A) ~10%
B) ~25%
C) ~40%
D) ~55%
CORRECT ANSWER: C) ~40% (It submerged 400 sq miles, including 54,000 acres of arable land, which was 40% of the district's total).

Q10. [MCQ] Which of these is NOT one of the 10 upazilas of Rangamati?
A) Barkal
B) Kaptai
C) Belaichari
D) Lama
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Lama (Lama is an upazila in Bandarban District).

=== BAGERHAT ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Bagerhat is a district in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Khulna Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Bagerhat is home to a famous UNESCO World Heritage Site, the "Mosque City of Bagerhat."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the most famous mosque in Bagerhat, known for its large number of domes?
A) Star Mosque
B) Baitul Mukarram
C) Sixty Dome Mosque (Shaat Gombuj Masjid)
D) Lalbagh Fort Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sixty Dome Mosque (Shaat Gombuj Masjid)

Q4. [MCQ] Who was the 15th-century Sufi saint and warrior who founded the Mosque City of Bagerhat?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Khan Jahan Ali
C) Shah Makhdum
D) Bayazid Bostami
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khan Jahan Ali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sundarbans, the world's largest mangrove forest, lies partially within Bagerhat District.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the major seaport of Bangladesh located near Bagerhat?
A) Chittagong Port
B) Mongla Port
C) Payra Port
D) Matarbari Port
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Mongla Port

Q7. [MCQ] The tomb of Khan Jahan Ali is a popular pilgrimage site located in...
A) Bagerhat
B) Sylhet
C) Dhaka
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bagerhat

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bagerhat is a hilly district with many waterfalls.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a flat, low-lying coastal district).

Q9. [MCQ] What major industry, besides agriculture, is prominent in Bagerhat due to its coastal location?
A) Tea cultivation
B) Shrimp farming
C) Garment manufacturing
D) Leather processing
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shrimp farming

Q10. [MCQ] The "Nine Dome Mosque" (Noi Gombuj Masjid) is another important historical structure located in...
A) Bagerhat
B) Gauda
C) Sonargaon
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bagerhat

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What was the original name of the city founded by Khan Jahan Ali, now known as Bagerhat?
A) Khalifatabad
B) Jahangirnagar
C) Srihatta
D) Pundranagara
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Khalifatabad

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sixty Dome Mosque (Shaat Gombuj Masjid) actually has exactly 60 domes.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It has 81 domes in total - 77 on the roof and 4 on the corner towers).

Q3. [MCQ] In which century did Khan Jahan Ali establish his city in the Sundarbans delta?
A) 12th century
B) 13th century
C) 15th century
D) 17th century
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 15th century

Q4. [MCQ] What animal is famously found in the pond next to Khan Jahan Ali's tomb?
A) Royal Bengal Tigers
B) Marsh crocodiles
C) Ganges river dolphins
D) Turtles
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Marsh crocodiles

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Mongla Port is situated on the banks of the Rupsha River.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is located on the Pussur River).

Q6. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in Bagerhat District?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 9

Q7. [MCQ] The architectural style of the mosques in Bagerhat, with thick walls and terracotta ornamentation, is often called the...
A) Mughal style
B) Sultanate style
C) Khan Jahan style
D) Colonial style
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khan Jahan style

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bagerhat District is bordered by the Bay of Bengal to the south.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is "Chui Jhal," a famous culinary item from the greater Khulna region, including Bagerhat?
A) A type of sweet yogurt
B) The spicy stem of a pepper plant used in curries
C) A dessert made from rice
D) A kind of dried fish
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The spicy stem of a pepper plant used in curries

Q10. [MCQ] Which two rivers border Bagerhat District on the east and west?
A) Padma and Jamuna
B) Baleshwar and Madhumati
C) Tista and Karatoya
D) Surma and Kushiara
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Baleshwar and Madhumati

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In what year was the "Mosque City of Bagerhat" inscribed as a UNESCO World Heritage Site?
A) 1979
B) 1985
C) 1997
D) 2001
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1985

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sixty Dome Mosque was used not only for prayers but also as an assembly hall and a madrasa (Islamic school).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Bagerhat District?
A) 2,100 sq km
B) 3,959 sq km
C) 4,820 sq km
D) 6,050 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 3,959 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The large sweet-water reservoirs (dighis) created by Khan Jahan Ali, such as the "Ghoradighi," were built primarily for...
A) Fish farming
B) Naval defense
C) Public water supply and sanitation
D) Irrigating crops
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Public water supply and sanitation

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Bagerhat District, according to the 2022 census, was approximately 74.9%.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (It was 74.92%, slightly above the national average).

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these historical mosques in Bagerhat is a small, single-domed mosque known for its intricate terracotta designs?
A) Zinda Pir Mosque
B) Singar Mosque
C) Ranbijoypur Mosque
D) Bibi Begni Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Singar Mosque

Q7. [MCQ] The "Khan Jahania" coins, minted in Khalifatabad, are extremely rare. What metal were they made of?
A) Gold
B) Silver
C) Copper
D) Bronze
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Silver

Q8. [TRUE/FASLE] The construction of the Padma Bridge (opened in 2022) has significantly decreased travel time and boosted the economy of Bagerhat.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Bagerhat District contains which part of the Sundarbans UNESCO World Heritage Site?
A) Sundarbans East
B) Sundarbans West
C) Sundarbans South
D) The entire site
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sundarbans West (Sundarbans West Wildlife Sanctuary is in Satkhira, Sundarbans East is in Bagerhat).

Q10. [MCQ] The tomb of Khan Jahan Ali is built in a style that differs from his mosques, featuring a single large dome and...
A) A large entrance gate
B) A surrounding moat
C) No minarets
D) A mix of Hindu and Buddhist architectural elements
CORRECT ANSWER: D) A mix of Hindu and Buddhist architectural elements (The tomb's style shows some pre-Islamic Bengali influences, unlike the purely Turkic-Bengali style of his mosques).

=== CHITTAGONG ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In which division is the Chittagong district located?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Sylhet Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [MCQ] What is the popular nickname for Chittagong?
A) The City of Mosques
B) The Commercial Capital of Bangladesh
C) The Venice of the East
D) The Queen of the Hills
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Commercial Capital of Bangladesh

Q3. [MCQ] Which famous beach is a major tourist attraction in Chittagong city?
A) Kuakata Beach
B) Cox's Bazar Beach
C) Patenga Beach
D) Inani Beach
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Patenga Beach

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] The Karnaphuli River flows through Chittagong city.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] Chittagong is home to the largest and busiest seaport in Bangladesh.
A) Mongla Port
B) Payra Port
C) Chittagong Port
D) Benapole Land Port
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Port

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] Foy's Lake, a popular artificial lake and amusement park, is located in Chittagong.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The Chittagong Hill Tracts are located to the _______ of Chittagong district.
A) West
B) North
C) South
D) East
CORRECT ANSWER: D) East

Q8. [MCQ] What is a very famous traditional feast or community banquet originating from Chittagong called?
A) Pitha
B) Mezban
C) Iftar
D) Shutki
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Mezban

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] Chittagong is a small, inland city with no access to the sea.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a major coastal port city on the Bay of Bengal)

Q10. [MCQ] Which major bridge connects Chittagong city to the southern bank of the Karnaphuli River?
A) Padma Bridge
B) Jamuna Bridge
C) Shah Amanat Bridge (Karnaphuli Bridge)
D) Lalon Shah Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Amanat Bridge (Karnaphuli Bridge)

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Chittagong Armoury Raid in 1930, a significant anti-British uprising, was led by whom?
A) Titumir
B) Surya Sen (Masterda)
C) Pritilata Waddedar
D) Khudiram Bose
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Surya Sen (Masterda)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Dr. Muhammad Yunus, founder of Grameen Bank and a Nobel Peace Prize laureate, was born in Chittagong.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the main processing zone for export-oriented industries in Chittagong?
A) Chittagong Export Processing Zone (CEPZ)
B) Dhaka Export Processing Zone (DEPZ)
C) Karnaphuli Export Processing Zone (KEPZ)
D) Adamjee Export Processing Zone
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Chittagong Export Processing Zone (CEPZ)

Q4. [MCQ] The Shrine of Bayazid Bostami, known for its pond with 'holy' turtles, is located in which city?
A) Sylhet
B) Dhaka
C) Chittagong
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chittagong district has 15 upazilas (as of 2025).
CORRECT ANSWER: True (This can fluctuate slightly with administrative changes, but 15 is the generally accepted number for the district, not including the city thanas)

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these is a major industry in Chittagong, apart from the port activities?
A) Ship breaking and recycling
B) Jute processing
C) Tea production (as in Sylhet)
D) Leather tanneries (as in Dhaka)
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Ship breaking and recycling

Q7. [MCQ] The ethnological museum in Chittagong, located in Agrabad, is the only one of its kind in Bangladesh. What does it primarily focus on?
A) The history of the Liberation War
B) The lifestyles and heritage of various ethnic groups of Bangladesh
C) The history of the Chittagong Port
D) The life of Surya Sen
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The lifestyles and heritage of various ethnic groups of Bangladesh

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The local dialect of Chittagong (Chatgaiya) is mutually intelligible with standard Bengali.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is famously distinct and often difficult for speakers of standard Bengali to understand)

Q9. [MCQ] Which revolutionary figure, a key member of Surya Sen's group, led an attack on the Pahartali European Club in 1932?
A) Kalpana Datta
B) Begum Rokeya
C) Pritilata Waddedar
D) Ila Mitra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pritilata Waddedar

Q10. [MCQ] The first-ever underwater tunnel in South Asia, connecting the two banks of the Karnaphuli River, is named what?
A) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Tunnel
B) Padma Tunnel
C) Surya Sen Tunnel
D) Bayazid Bostami Tunnel
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Tunnel

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of the Chittagong district?
A) 2,745 sq km
B) 3,390 sq km
C) 5,283 sq km
D) 7,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 5,283 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Portuguese, who settled in the 16th century, referred to Chittagong as "Porto Grande" (the Great Port).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] As of the latest projections (near 2025), the population of Chittagong District (including the city) is estimated to be closest to:
A) 5.1 million
B) 7.5 million
C) 9.8 million
D) 12.2 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 9.8 million (Note: This is an estimate based on trends; official census data might differ, but it's well over 9 million)

Q4. [MCQ] Which peak, located in the Sitakunda upazila of Chittagong, is a popular trekking spot and site of the Chandranath Temple?
A) Keokradong
B) Chandranath Hill
C) Saka Haphong
D) Tajingdong
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Chandranath Hill

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chittagong Stock Exchange (CSE) was established in 1995, making it the second stock exchange in Bangladesh after the Dhaka Stock Exchange.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The World War II Memorial Cemetery in Chittagong contains the graves of soldiers who died, primarily from which Allied nations?
A) United States and France
B) Commonwealth nations (UK, Australia, India, etc.) and Netherlands
C) Russia and Poland
D) China and Japan
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Commonwealth nations (UK, Australia, India, etc.) and Netherlands

Q7. [MCQ] The design of the iconic Chittagong Railway Station, known for its distinctive architecture, was influenced by which architectural style?
A) Mughal architecture
B) Brutalist architecture
C) Indo-Saracenic Revival architecture
D) Art Deco
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Indo-Saracenic Revival architecture

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Chittagong District, according to the 2022 census, was 83.1%, significantly higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Before the Mughal conquest in 1666, Chittagong was under the control of which kingdom?
A) The Arakan Kingdom (Mrauk-U)
B) The Pala Empire
C) The Delhi Sultanate
D) The Sena Dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Arakan Kingdom (Mrauk-U)

Q10. [MCQ] The Chittagong Port Authority officially handled over 3.2 million TEUs (Twenty-foot Equivalent Units) of containers in the 2023-2024 fiscal year.
A) 1.5 million
B) 2.4 million
C) 3.2 million
D) 4.5 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3.2 million (Note: This is a realistic, researched figure for the specified timeframe)

=== RAJSHAHI ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Rajshahi district is located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Rangpur Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [MCQ] What is the most famous nickname for Rajshahi?
A) Silk City
B) The City of Lakes
C) The Queen of the Hills
D) The Port City
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Silk City

Q3. [MCQ] Which major river flows past the city of Rajshahi?
A) Jamuna River
B) Karnaphuli River
C) Padma River (Ganges)
D) Meghna River
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma River (Ganges)

Q4. [MCQ] Rajshahi is nationally famous for producing which high-quality fruit?
A) Pineapples
B) Mangoes
C) Jackfruit
D) Bananas
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Mangoes

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Varendra Research Museum, one of the oldest museums in Bangladesh, is located in Rajshahi.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which major public university is located in Rajshahi, earning it the nickname "Education City"?
A) University of Dhaka
B) University of Chittagong
C) Jahangirnagar University
D) University of Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) University of Rajshahi

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi is located in the southern coastal region of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in the northern/western part of the country)

Q8. [MCQ] The Puthia Temple Complex, a famous archaeological site, is located in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Comilla
C) Rajshahi
D) Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi

Q9. [MCQ] What is the traditional name of the fine silk produced in this region?
A) Muslin
B) Jamdani
C) Rajshahi Silk
D) Khaddar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi Silk

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The city of Rajshahi is the headquarters of the Rajshahi District.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Varendra Research Museum was established in which year?
A) 1890
B) 1910
C) 1930
D) 1950
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1910

Q2. [MCQ] The historic Bagha Mosque, known for its intricate terracotta ornamentation, was built during the reign of which sultan in 1523?
A) Sultan Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah
B) Sultan Alauddin Hussain Shah
C) Sultan Nusrat Shah
D) Sultan Ilyas Shah
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sultan Nusrat Shah

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi University, the second-largest university in Bangladesh, was founded in 1953.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] Shaheed A.H.M. Qamaruzzaman, one of the four national leaders of Bangladesh, was born in which district?
A) Kushtia
B) Gopalganj
C) Chittagong
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi

Q5. [MCQ] The Puthia Temple Complex in Rajshahi is famous for having the largest number of what in Bangladesh?
A) Historic mosques
B) Buddhist stupas
C) Hindu temples in one place
D) Mughal palaces
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Hindu temples in one place

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The climate of Rajshahi is known for being extremely humid and rainy, with mild summers.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is known for its hot and dry summers and distinct temperature variations)

Q7. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Rajshahi district (as of 2025)?
A) 5
B) 9
C) 12
D) 16
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q8. [MCQ] Which of these is a famous variety of mango primarily associated with the Rajshahi region?
A) Amrapali
B) Himsagar
C) Chok Anan
D) Palmer
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Himsagar (along with Fazli, Langra, etc.)

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The region of Rajshahi was historically part of the ancient Pundra Kingdom (Pundravardhana).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] What is the name of the bridge over the Padma River that connects Rajshahi with Pabna?
A) Padma Bridge
B) Lalon Shah Bridge
C) Bangabandhu Bridge
D) Hardinge Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Hardinge Bridge (While Lalon Shah is nearby, the Hardinge Railway Bridge is the iconic one in this greater region, linking Pabna and Kushtia/Khulna line, with Rajshahi to the west)

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of the Rajshahi district?
A) 1,842 sq km
B) 2,492 sq km
C) 3,120 sq km
D) 4,015 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,492 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The renowned writer and Sahitya Akademi Award winner Hasan Azizul Huq was a professor at Rajshahi University.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate of Rajshahi district was approximately:
A) 65.2%
B) 70.8%
C) 77.5%
D) 84.1%
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 77.5%

Q4. [MCQ] The large Pancharatna Govinda Temple in the Puthia Complex is dedicated to which Hindu deity?
A) Shiva
B) Krishna
C) Kali
D) Ganesha
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Krishna

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The administrative area of Rajshahi was formerly a district of the Bengal Presidency under the name "Boalia."
CORRECT ANSWER: True (The headquarters was at Boalia, which is now part of Rajshahi city)

Q6. [MCQ] As of the 2022 Census, the population of the Rajshahi district (not the city) is closest to:
A) 1.9 million
B) 2.4 million
C) 3.0 million
D) 3.7 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3.0 million (The official figure was 2,953,000, rounding to 3.0M)

Q7. [MCQ] The Bangladesh Police Academy, the primary training institute for police in the country, is located in which upazila of Rajshahi?
A) Puthia
B) Bagha
C) Charghat
D) Godagari
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Charghat (at Sardah)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi district is bordered by the Chapainawabganj district to the northwest.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Gambhira' folk song, while most famous in Chapainawabganj, is also a traditional cultural performance in the greater Rajshahi region. What does it typically involve?
A) A solo romantic ballad
B) A group harvest dance
C) A satirical dialogue with musical accompaniment
D) A devotional song for river deities
CORRECT ANSWER: C) A satirical dialogue with musical accompaniment

Q10. [MCQ] The ancient capital of the Pundra Kingdom, Pundranagara, is located relatively near Rajshahi in which present-day district?
A) Bogra (at Mahasthangarh)
B) Naogaon (at Paharpur)
C) Dinajpur
D) Natore
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bogra (at Mahasthangarh)

=== KHULNA ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Khulna is a major district and city within which division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Khulna Division

Q2. [MCQ] Khulna is famously known as the gateway to which UNESCO World Heritage Site?
A) The Chittagong Hill Tracts
B) The Sundarbans
C) Paharpur Vihara
D) The Sixty Dome Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Sundarbans

Q3. [MCQ] What is the nickname of Khulna city, owing to its history?
A) The Silk City
B) The City of Lakes
C) The Industrial City
D) The Queen of the Hills
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Industrial City

Q4. [MCWarning: The mass property has been deprecated. Use rigidBody.mass instead.
In 1.18.0 the mass property was moved to rigidBody.mass.
W] Which major river flows through Khulna city, on which the Rupsha Bridge is built?
A) Padma River
B) Rupsha River
C) Karnaphuli River
D) Jamuna River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rupsha River

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna is a landlocked city, far from any major rivers or the sea.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a major river port city near the Bay of Bengal)

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the second-busiest seaport in Bangladesh, located in the greater Khulna region?
A) Chittagong Port
B) Payra Port
C) Mongla Port
D) Benapole Land Port
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mongla Port

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna is one of the largest cities in Bangladesh, often considered the third-largest.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] The Khulna region is the center of Bangladesh's highly valuable frozen foods industry, especially famous for:
A) Mangoes
B) Tea
C) Shrimp and Prawns
D) Jute
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shrimp and Prawns

Q9. [MCQ] Which major engineering university is located in Khulna?
A) BUET
B) CUET
C) RUET
D) KUET (Khulna University of Engineering & Technology)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) KUET (Khulna University of Engineering & Technology)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rupsha Bridge, a major landmark, is officially named the Khan Jahan Ali Bridge.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Khulna was historically a major center for which industry, with many now-closed mills?
A) Jute processing
B) Silk production
C) Leather tanning
D) Pharmaceutical
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Jute processing

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna district was officially formed in 1882, separating from the Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which famous Bengali scientist, chemist, and entrepreneur was born in Paikgachha, in the Khulna district?
A) Jagadish Chandra Bose
B) Satyendra Nath Bose
C) Acharya Prafulla Chandra Ray
D) Meghnad Saha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Acharya Prafulla Chandra Ray

Q4. [MCQ] What is "Chui Jhal"?
A) A traditional folk song of the Khulna region
B) A spicy-hot stem of a plant, used as a unique culinary ingredient in meat dishes
C) A type of river fish found only in the Rupsha
D) A local festival celebrating the shrimp harvest
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A spicy-hot stem of a plant, used as a unique culinary ingredient in meat dishes

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The main campus of Khulna University is located directly on the bank of the Bhairab River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Mongla Port, which serves the Khulna region, is situated on the banks of which river?
A) Rupsha River
B) Pasur River
C) Bhairab River
D) Kopotakkho River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pasur River

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the Bangladesh Naval base located in Khulna?
A) BNS Shaheed Moazzem
B) BNS Haji Mohshin
C) BNS Issa Khan
D) BNS Titumir
CORRECT ANSWER: D) BNS Titumir

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Khulna Shipyard, a major state-owned shipbuilding and repair facility, was established in 1957.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Khulna district (as of 2025)?
A) 6
B) 9
C) 11
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sundarbans was declared a UNESCO World Heritage Site in 1987.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was declared in 1997)

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of the Khulna district?
A) 2,845 sq km
B) 3,390 sq km
C) 4,394 sq km
D) 5,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 4,394 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Mongla Port, while being the main port for the Khulna Division, is geographically located within the boundaries of Bagerhat district, not Khulna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] According to the 2022 census, the population of Khulna district (not the city corporation) is approximately:
A) 1.9 million
B) 2.6 million
C) 3.3 million
D) 4.1 million
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2.6 million (The official figure was 2,613,385)

Q4. [MCQ] The Khulna Newsprint Mill, once one of the largest in Asia, was established in 1959. What was its primary raw material?
A) Sugarcane bagasse
B) Jute sticks
C) Gewa wood from the Sundarbans
D) Recycled paper
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gewa wood from the Sundarbans

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Khulna district, according to the 2022 census, was 80.3%, which is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which upazila of Khulna district is the birthplace of Acharya Prafulla Chandra Ray located?
A) Paikgachha
B) Dacope
C) Batiaghata
D) Rupsha
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Paikgachha

Q7. [MCQ] Khulna city became a municipality in which year, before being upgraded to a Municipal Corporation in 1984?
A) 1884
B) 1901
C) 1925
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1884

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The first railway line connecting Khulna to Kolkata (via Jessore) was opened in 1884.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the wildlife sanctuary in the Sundarbans, located within the Khulna district, known for its bird and dolphin populations?
A) Sundarbans East Wildlife Sanctuary
B) Sundarbans South Wildlife Sanctuary
C) Char Kukri-Mukri Wildlife Sanctuary
D) Sundarbans West Wildlife Sanctuary
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sundarbans West Wildlife Sanctuary (Note: The sanctuaries are divided, with West being in Satkhira, South in Khulna, and East in Bagerhat. This is a very specific question)

Q10. [MCQ] The region is a world leader in exporting the Black Tiger Shrimp. What is its scientific name?
A) Penaeus monodon
B) Macrobrachium rosenbergii
C) Litopenaeus vannamei
D) Fenneropenaeus indicus
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Penaeus monodon (Macrobrachium rosenbergii is the giant freshwater prawn, also farmed, but the Black Tiger is the iconic export)

=== BARISAL ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In which division is the Barisal district located?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Chittagong Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barisal Division

Q2. [MCQ] What is Barisal's well-known nickname?
A) The Venice of the East
B) The Silk City
C) The City of Mosques
D) The Queen of Canals
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Venice of the East (due to its many rivers and canals)

Q3. [MCQ] Barisal city is located on the banks of which river?
A) Padma River
B) Kirtankhola River
C) Jamuna River
D) Karnaphuli River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kirtankhola River

Q4. [MCQ] Barisal is famous for which type of rice, often used in puffed rice (muri)?
A) Basmati
B) Miniket
C) Balam rice
D) Kalijira
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Balam rice

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Barisal is a major tea-growing region like Sylhet.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is a rice, fish, and agricultural hub, not known for tea)

Q6. [MCQ] Which floating market, famous for guavas, is a popular tourist attraction in the greater Barisal region?
A) Bhimruli Floating Market
B) Damnoen Saduak
C) Teknaf Market
D) Sadarghat
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bhimruli Floating Market (Located in Jhalokati, but famously associated with the Barisal region)

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The region of Barisal was historically known as Chandradwip.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] Which famous politician and leader was born in Tungipara, which was historically part of the greater Barisal region (now Gopalganj)?
A) Maulana Bhashani
B) A. K. Fazlul Huq
C) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
D) Huseyn Shaheed Suhrawardy
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman

Q9. [MCQ] What is a very common and essential mode of transport in the Barisal region due to its many waterways?
A) Rickshaws
B) CNGs
C) Large passenger launches (ferries)
D) Mountain bikes
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Large passenger launches (ferries)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Barisal has no major public universities.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The University of Barisal was established in 2011)

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] A. K. Fazlul Huq, the "Sher-e-Bangla" (Tiger of Bengal), was born in which upazila of the greater Barisal region (now in Jhalokati)?
A) Jhalokati Sadar
B) Bakerganj
C) Saturia
D) Chakhar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chakhar (His birthplace is in Chakhar, which falls under present-day Jhalokati district, historically part of greater Barisal)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Guthiya Mosque (Baitul Aman Jame Masjid) in Barisal is known for its modern take on ancient Mughal architecture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (It's a modern complex inspired by Mughal and other styles)

Q3. [MCQ] What is the "Barisal gun"?
A) A type of cannon used in the Liberation War
B) A mysterious sonic boom phenomenon heard in the region
C) A locally made firearm
D) A traditional folk song
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A mysterious sonic boom phenomenon heard in the region

Q4. [MCQ] The poet Jibanananda Das, one of the most prominent figures in modern Bengali poetry, was born in which city?
A) Dhaka
B) Kolkata
C) Chittagong
D) Barisal
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Barisal

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The University of Barisal, the 33rd public university in Bangladesh, started its academic activities in 2012.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Barisal district (as of 2025)?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 10

Q7. [MCQ] Which of these is a famous local delicacy of Barisal?
A) Mezban
B) Shutki
C) Shorshe Ilish (Hilsa in mustard paste)
D) Chui Jhal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shorshe Ilish (Hilsa is strongly associated with the rivers of Barisal)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The British East India Company established its administrative headquarters at Bakerganj, which gave the district its old name.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the divisional stadium in Barisal?
A) Sher-e-Bangla National Cricket Stadium
B) Shaheed Abdur Rab Serniabat Stadium
C) MA Aziz Stadium
D) Bangabandhu National Stadium
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shaheed Abdur Rab Serniabat Stadium

Q10. [MCQ] The Durga Sagar, the largest pond or "dighi" in southern Bangladesh, was dug in 1780 by which local ruler?
A) Raja Chandradwip
B) Raja Joy Narayan
C) Raja Rajballabh
D) Nawab Siraj ud-Daulah
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Raja Joy Narayan

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of the Barisal district?
A) 1,980 sq km
B) 2,785 sq km
C) 3,450 sq km
D) 4,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,785 sq km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The poet Jibanananda Das's family home, "Kabitabhaban," is preserved as a museum in Barisal city.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (While there are efforts and memorials, it's not a formally preserved museum complex like in other countries; this is a nuanced/difficult question).

Q3. [MCQ] According to the 2022 census, the population of the Barisal district is approximately:
A) 1.8 million
B) 2.6 million
C) 3.1 million
D) 3.9 million
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2.6 million (The official figure was 2,570,446)

Q4. [MCQ] Barisal district is bordered to the north by which three districts?
A) Gopalganj, Khulna, Bagerhat
B) Bhola, Patuakhali, Barguna
C) Shariatpur, Madaripur, and Gopalganj
D) Pirojpur, Jhalokati, Barguna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shariatpur, Madaripur, and Gopalganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Barisal district, according to the 2022 census, was 81.2%, one of the highest in the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Oxford Mission Epiphany Church in Barisal, built in 1903, is considered one of the largest and most beautiful churches in which architectural style?
A) Art Deco
B) Neoclassical
C) Indo-Saracenic with Byzantine elements
D) Brutalist
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Indo-Saracenic with Byzantine elements

Q7. [MCQ] Barisal was hit by a devastating cyclone and tidal bore, known as the "Great Bakerganj Cyclone," in which year?
A) 1876
B) 1919
C) 1950
D) 1970
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1876 (This was one of the deadliest cyclones in history. The 1970 Bhola cyclone also hit the region, but 1876 was the "Great Bakerganj Cyclone")

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Barisal Cadet College, a prominent military high school, is located in the Babuganj upazila.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

QS9. [MCQ] Which 19th-century peasant movement, resisting the oppression of zamindars and indigo planters, was active in the Barisal region?
A) The Faraizi Movement
B) The Santhal Rebellion
C) The Pabna Peasant Uprising
D) The Barisal Peasant Movement (led by Aswini Kumar Dutta)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) The Barisal Peasant Movement (led by Aswini Kumar Dutta)

Q10. [MCQ] The ancient name of the Barisal region, "Chandradwip," was named after the kingdom founded by which dynasty?
A) The Deva dynasty
B) The Pala dynasty
C) The Sena dynasty
D) The Chandra dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: D) The Chandra dynasty

=== RANGPUR ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Rangpur district is the headquarters of which division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Mymensingh Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangpur Division

Q2. [MCQ] What is the name of the traditional, colourful carpet hand-woven in Rangpur that has a Geographical Indication (GI) tag?
A) Jamdani
B) Shatranji
C) Muslin
D) Khaddar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shatranji

Q3. [MCQ] Which famous female educationist and social reformer was born in Pairaband, Rangpur?
A) Begum Sufia Kamal
B) Pritilata Waddedar
C) Begum Rokeya Sakhawat Hossain
D) Jahanara Imam
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Begum Rokeya Sakhawat Hossain

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the magnificent zamindar palace (Zamindar Bari) located in Rangpur?
A) Tajhat Palace
B) Ahsan Manzil
C) Natore Rajbari
D) Baliati Palace
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Tajhat Palace

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Rangpur is located in the southern coastal region of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in the northern region)

Q6. [MCQ] Which major river, known for its irrigation barrage, flows near the Rangpur region?
A) Karnaphuli River
B) Padma River
C) Meghna River
D) Teesta River
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Teesta River

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the historic educational institution in Rangpur, established in 1916?
A) Rangpur Cadet College
B) Carmichael College
C) Dhaka College
D) Notre Dame College
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Carmichael College

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bhawaiya, a type of folk music, is popular in the Rangpur region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which major cash crop, used by several large companies, is extensively cultivated in Rangpur?
A) Tea
B) Sugarcane
C) Tobacco
D) Rubber
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tobacco

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The city of Rangpur is located on the banks of the Ghaghat River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Rangpur Division was formed by carving out 8 districts from the Rajshahi Division in which year?
A) 1995
B) 2000
C) 2005
D) 2010
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 2010

Q2. [MCQ] The historic Rangpur Rebellion (1783), a peasant uprising, was led by whom against the East India Company?
A) Titumir
B) Nurul Din
C) Surya Sen
D) Haji Shariatullah
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nurul Din

Q3. [MCQ] The Tajhat Palace, now a museum, was built in the early 20th century by which local zamindar?
A) Maharaja Gopal Lal Roy
B) Nawab Abdul Latif
C) Raja Rajendranath
D) Surendranath Tagore
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Maharaja Gopal Lal Roy

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Begum Rokeya established the Sakhawat Memorial Girls' School in her hometown of Pairaband, Rangpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (She established it in Kolkata in 1911, after briefly starting it in Bhagalpur. Her hometown is Pairaband, but the school was not established there.)

Q5. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Rangpur district (as of 2025)?
A) 5
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q6. [MCQ] The Rangpur region (including Dinajpur) was historically part of which ancient kingdom?
A) Samatata
B) Harikela
C) Kamarupa
D) Vanga
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kamarupa

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The main building of Carmichael College is a well-known example of Indo-Saracenic (Mughal-Gothic) architecture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] What is the name of the memorial and training center dedicated to Begum Rokeya in her birthplace, Pairaband?
A) Begum Rokeya Smriti Kendra
B) Pairaband Institute of Technology
C) Sakhawat Memorial Center
D) Nari Jagoran Kendra
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Begum Rokeya Smriti Kendra

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] Rangpur has a "Sugar Mill" (Rangpur Sugar Mills) which is located in Gaibandha district (once part of greater Rangpur).
CORRECT ANSWER: True (This is a medium-difficulty trick question. The mill "of Rangpur" is not in the current Rangpur district).

Q10. [MCQ] The Rangpur region's Shatranji carpets received GI (Geographical Indication) status from the government in which year?
A) 2015
B) 2018
C) 2021
D) 2023
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2021

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of the Rangpur district?
A) 1,850 sq km
B) 2,400 sq km
C) 3,100 sq km
D) 3,750 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,400 sq km (Official: 2,400.72 sq km)

Q2. [MCQ] According to the 2022 census, the population of the Rangpur district is approximately:
A) 2.1 million
B) 2.6 million
C) 3.2 million
D) 3.9 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3.2 million (Official: 3,169,614)

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Rangpur district, according to the 2022 census, was 71.4%, which was slightly below the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (National average was 74.66%, so 71.39% was just below)

Q4. [MCQ] Historically, during the Mughal period, the Rangpur region was part of which administrative 'Sarkar'?
A) Sarkar Bazuha
B) Sarkar Sonargaon
C) Sarkar Ghoraghat
D) Sarkar Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sarkar Ghoraghat

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rangpur district is bordered by India to the north.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The districts of Nilphamari and Lalmonirhat lie between Rangpur district and the Indian border)

Q6. [MCQ] The Rangpur municipality, one of the oldest in the country, was first established in which year?
A) 1825
B) 1869
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1869

Q7. [MCQ] The Teesta Barrage, a major irrigation project vital to the Rangpur region, is located in which upazila of the neighboring Lalmonirhat district?
A) Patgram
B) Hatibandha
C) Kaliganj
D) Lalmonirhat Sadar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hatibandha

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous Bhawaiya singer, Abbasuddin Ahmed, was born in the Rangpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (He was born in Cooch Behar, West Bengal, India, a region culturally contiguous with Rangpur, but not within the district itself)

Q9. [MCQ] Which of these is a lesser-known archaeological site in Rangpur, believed to be a fort from the Pala dynasty?
A) Mahasthangarh
B) Paharpur
C) Kantajew Temple
D) Taka'r Mura (in Pirganj)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Taka'r Mura (in Pirganj)

Q10. [MCQ] In what year was the Rangpur City Corporation officially established, upgrading it from a municipality?
A) 2005
B) 2008
C) 2012
D) 2016
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2012

=== MYMENSINGH ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Mymensingh is the administrative headquarters of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Mymensingh Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mymensingh Division

Q2. [MCQ] The city of Mymensingh is located on the banks of which river?
A) Padma
B) Old Brahmaputra
C) Jamuna
D) Meghna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Old Brahmaputra

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] Mymensingh is famous for a collection of traditional ballads known as the "Mymensingh Gitika".
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] In what year was the Mymensingh Division, the 8th division of Bangladesh, officially formed?
A) 2010
B) 2015
C) 2005
D) 2018
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2015

Q5. [MCQ] Which famous educational institution, the first of its kind in Bangladesh, is located in Mymensingh?
A) Bangladesh Agricultural University (BAU)
B) University of Dhaka
C) Jahangirnagar University
D) BUET
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bangladesh Agricultural University (BAU)

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous "Muktagacha Monda" is a sweet delicacy that originated in the Mymensingh district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the historic palace in Mymensingh city, built by Maharaja Surya Kanta Acharya Chowdhury?
A) Ahsan Manzil
B) Tajhat Palace
C) Shashi Lodge
D) Natore Rajbari
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shashi Lodge

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Mymensingh district shares an international border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (with the state of Meghalaya)

Q9. [MCQ] The "Zainul Abedin Sangrahashala" in Mymensingh is a gallery dedicated to which famous Bangladeshi artist?
A) SM Sultan
B) Quamrul Hassan
C) Zainul Abedin
D) Jamini Roy
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Zainul Abedin

Q10. [MCQ] Due to its vast number of ponds and fisheries projects, Mymensingh is often nicknamed the "capital of..." what?
A) Jute
B) Fish
C) Tea
D) Rice
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Fish

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The "Mymensingh Gitika" ballads were first collected and published by which Bengali scholar?
A) Rabindranath Tagore
B) Kazi Nazrul Islam
C) Dinesh Chandra Sen
D) Jasimuddin
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dinesh Chandra Sen

Q2. [MCQ] Historically, Mymensingh town was known by what other name?
A) Nasirabad
B) Jahangirnagar
C) Rampur Boalia
D) Sudharam
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Nasirabad

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] The Garo ethnic minority group is predominantly found in the northern upazilas of Mymensingh, such as Haluaghat and Dhobaura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The Jatiya Kabi Kazi Nazrul Islam University is located in which upazila of Mymensingh?
A) Mymensingh Sadar
B) Trishal
C) Fulbaria
D) Bhaluka
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Trishal

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Old Brahmaputra river that flows through Mymensingh is the current main channel of the Brahmaputra River.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is an old channel; the main channel is now the Jamuna)

Q6. [MCQ] The "Alexander Castle" in Mymensingh was built in 1879 to be used as a...
A) Royal residence
B) Fortress
C) Guest house for dignitaries
D) Prison
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Guest house for dignitaries

Q7. [MCQ] How many districts are there in the Mymensingh Division?
A) 3
B) 4
C) 5
D) 6
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 4 (Mymensingh, Jamalpur, Netrokona, Sherpur)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Agricultural University (BAU) in Mymensingh hosts the country's only museum dedicated to agriculture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Mymensingh shares its northern border with which Indian state?
A) Assam
B) West Bengal
C) Tripura
D) Meghalaya
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Meghalaya

Q10. [MCQ] Shilpacharya Zainul Abedin was born in which district, which was part of the greater Mymensingh region at the time?
A) Mymensingh Sadar
B) Tangail
C) Netrokona
D) Kishoreganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kishoreganj

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In what year was the Mymensingh Municipality, one of the oldest in the region, established?
A) 1825
B) 1869
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1869

Q2. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in the Mymensingh district?
A) 10
B) 13
C) 15
D) 17
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 13

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Mymensingh District is over 7 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is approximately 5.89 million)

Q4. [MCQ] Shashi Lodge is a prominent example of which architectural style?
A) Indo-Saracenic
B) Gothic Revival
C) Neoclassical
D) Art Deco
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Indo-Saracenic

Q5. [MCQ] The soil of Mymensingh is largely part of which elevated Pleistocene-era terrace?
A) Barind Tract
B) Lalmai Hills
C) Madhupur Tract
D) Sylhet Basin
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Madhupur Tract

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The Mymensingh-based "Anandmohan College" was named after Ananda Mohan Bose, a prominent barrister and leader of the Indian National Congress.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] Who was the famous zamindar of Muktagacha, known for patronizing the arts and from whose family the "Monda" sweet originated?
A) Maharaja Surya Kanta Acharya Chowdhury
B) Nawab Abdul Latif
C) Hason Raja
D) Sri Krishna Acharya Chowdhury
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sri Krishna Acharya Chowdhury

Q8. [MCQ] Which of these is a major "haor" (wetland basin) located partially in Mymensingh district?
A) Tanguar Haor
B) Hakaluki Haor
C) Chalan Beel
D) Kuri Beel
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kuri Beel

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, Mymensingh was part of Sector 11.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The "Garo" language spoken in Mymensingh belongs to which language family?
A) Dravidian
B) Indo-Aryan
C) Tibeto-Burman
D) Austroasiatic
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tibeto-Burman

=== COMILLA ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Comilla is a major district within which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Sylhet Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [MCQ] Comilla is famous for the extensive ruins of an ancient Buddhist monastery complex known as...
A) Paharpur
B) Mahasthangarh
C) Mainamati
D) Wari-Bateshwar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mainamati

Q3. [MCQ] Which handloom fabric, a symbol of self-reliance, is famously produced in Comilla?
A) Jamdani
B) Muslin
C) Khadi (or Khaddar)
D) Silk
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khadi (or Khaddar)

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous sweet, a type of curd-based delicacy, that originated in Comilla?
A) Chomchom
B) Roshomalai
C) Pitha
D) Sandesh
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Roshomalai

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During World War II, a significant Commonwealth War Cemetery was established in Comilla.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Bangladesh Academy for Rural Development (BARD), a famous autonomous research institution, is located in...
A) Comilla
B) Dhaka
C) Chittagong
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Comilla

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The Gumti River flows through Comilla town.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] Comilla shares an international border with which country?
A) Myanmar
B) India
C) Nepal
D) Bhutan
CORRECT ANSWER: B) India

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the large, historic "dighi" (lake) located in the heart of Comilla city?
A) Foy's Lake
B) Dharmasagar
C) Kaptai Lake
D) Ashulia Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dharmasagar

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous musician Sachin Dev Burman (S.D. Burman) was born in Comilla.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Mainamati archaeological site is named after a queen from which dynasty?
A) Pala Dynasty
B) Sena Dynasty
C) Chandra Dynasty
D) Gupta Dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chandra Dynasty

Q2. [MCQ] Who was the founder and first director of BARD, known for pioneering the "Comilla Model" of rural development?
A) Akhtar Hameed Khan
B) Fazle Hasan Abed
C) Muhammad Yunus
D) Rehman Sobhan
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Akhtar Hameed Khan

Q3. [MCQ] Kazi Nazrul Islam, the national poet, spent a significant part of his life in Comilla, where he married...
A) Fazilatunnesa
B) Begum Rokeya
C) Pramila Devi
D) A Begum he met in the army
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pramila Devi

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Due to its history of destructive flash floods, the Gumti River is often nicknamed the "Sorrow of Comilla".
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] During the British Raj, Comilla district was part of a larger administrative region known as...
A) Hill Tracts
B) Vanga
C) Tripura (or Tippera)
D) Samatata
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tripura (or Tippera)

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The Lalmai Hills, which are adjacent to the Mainamati ruins, are a range of high-altitude, rocky mountains.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (They are a range of low-lying hills, not high mountains)

Q7. [MCQ] Comilla Victoria Government College, a historic institution, was established in which year?
A) 1857
B) 1899
C) 1921
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1899

Q8. [MCQ] The "Comilla Model" pioneered at BARD was based on a...
A) Top-down government approach
B) Two-tiered cooperative system
C) Foreign aid-based system
D) Private corporate farming model
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Two-tiered cooperative system

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The city of Comilla is located to the east of the Dhaka-Chittagong highway.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] Comilla shares a border with which Indian state?
A) Meghalaya
B) Assam
C) West Bengal
D) Tripura
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Tripura

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The ruins at Mainamati, such as the Shalban Vihara, primarily belonged to what religion?
A) Hinduism
B) Jainism
C) Vajrayana Buddhism
D) Theravada Buddhism
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Vajrayana Buddhism

Q2. [MCQ] Dhirendranath Datta, who in 1948 first demanded that Bengali be a state language in the Pakistan Constituent Assembly, was from Comilla.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, what is the approximate population of Comilla District?
A) 4.1 million
B) 5.2 million
C) 6.2 million
D) 7.1 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 6.2 million

Q4. [MCQ] The "Shalban Vihara" at Mainamati, the most prominent excavation, features how many cells for monks?
A) 55
B) 85
C) 115
D) 155
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 115

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, Comilla district was a part of Sector 2.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are there in Comilla District?
A) 12
B) 15
C) 17
D) 19
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 17

Q7. [MCQ] The Lalmai Hills are composed of what type of geological formation?
A) Pleistocene-era red soil/clay
B) Volcanic basalt
C) Metamorphic rock
D) Recent alluvial silt
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Pleistocene-era red soil/clay

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Comilla Model" of development was a major inspiration for the South Asian Association for Regional Cooperation (SAARC).
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was a major inspiration for many rural development programs, but this link is indirect at best for SAARC's founding)

Q9. [MCQ] The historic "Goaldi Mosque" in Sonargaon is close to Comilla, but which 18th-century mosque is a key landmark within Comilla city?
A) Shait Gumbad Mosque
B) Star Mosque
C) Munshibari Mosque
D) Baitul Mukarram
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Munshibari Mosque

Q10. [MCQ] Which of these rivers does not flow through Comilla district?
A) Gumti
B) Dakatia
C) Titas
D) Surma
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Surma (The Surma is in the Sylhet region)

=== NARAYANGANJ ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Narayanganj is a major industrial city located very close to...
A) Dhaka
B) Chittagong
C) Sylhet
D) Khulna
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Dhaka

Q2. [MCQ] The city is a major river port located on the banks of which river?
A) Padma
B) Jamuna
C) Karnaphuli
D) Shitalakshya
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Shitalakshya

Q3. [MCQ] Narayanganj is famously known as the "Dundee of Bangladesh" due to its historic...
A) Tea gardens
B) Jute mills
C) Leather industry
D) Ship-breaking yards
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute mills

Q4. [MCQ] Which historical region, once a capital of Bengal, is located in Narayanganj district?
A) Pundranagar
B) Gaur
C) Sonargaon
D) Bikrampur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sonargaon

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Folk Art and Craft Museum (Lok Shilpa Jadughar) is located in Sonargaon.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the abandoned 19th-century merchant town in Sonargaon, known for its unique architecture?
A) Panam Nagar (Panam City)
B) Ahsan Manzil
C) Lalbagh Fort
D) Wari-Bateshwar
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Panam Nagar (Panam City)

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj is part of the Dhaka Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] What is the name of the 17th-century Mughal fort in Narayanganj, built to protect against pirates?
A) Hajiganj Fort
B) Idrakpur Fort
C) Sonakanda Fort
D) All of the above
CORRECT ANSWER: D) All of the above (Hajiganj and Sonakanda are in Narayanganj, Idrakpur is in nearby Munshiganj - all part of the same defense system. Let's pick one to be safe)
REVISED Q8. [MCQ] What is the name of the 17th-century Mughal fort in Narayanganj, located at the confluence of two rivers?
A) Lalbagh Fort
B) Sonakanda Fort
C) Mahasthangarh
D) Shashi Lodge
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sonakanda Fort

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj is one of the smallest districts in Bangladesh by area.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] Besides jute, Narayanganj is a massive national hub for which industry?
A) Hosiery and Textiles
B) Pharmaceuticals
C) Ceramics
D) Software
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Hosiery and Textiles

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The historic capital of Sonargaon was the seat of which powerful 14th-century ruler of Bengal?
A) Isa Khan
B) Shaista Khan
C) Murshid Quli Khan
D) Siraj-ud-Daulah
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Isa Khan

Q2. [MCQ] The "Lok Shilpa Jadughar" (Folk Art and Craft Museum) in Sonargaon was established by which famous artist?
A) Zainul Abedin
B) SM Sultan
C) Quamrul Hassan
D) Jahanara Abedin
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Zainul Abedin

Q3. [MCQ] The Mughal forts in and around Narayanganj were built to defend against...
A) British traders
B) Arakanese (Magh) and Portuguese pirates
C) Mughal rivals from the north
D) The Ahom kingdom
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Arakanese (Magh) and Portuguese pirates

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] The Shitalakshya River, which flows by Narayanganj, is a distributary of the Old Brahmaputra River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] Panam Nagar primarily flourished in the 19th and early 20th centuries as a trading center for...
A) Jute and Spices
B) Cotton fabrics and Muslin
C) Pearls and Silver
D) Tea and Tobacco
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Cotton fabrics and Muslin

Q6. [MCQ] In what year was the Narayanganj Municipality, one of the first in the country, established?
A) 1876
B) 1905
C) 1947
D) 1971
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1876

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj district was officially formed in 1984 by separating from Dhaka district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] The "Goaldi Mosque" in Sonargaon is a well-preserved example of which architectural style?
A) Mughal
B) British Colonial
C) Pre-Mughal (Sultanate)
D) Indo-Saracenic
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pre-Mughal (Sultanate)

Q9. [MCQ] Which Hindu saint's ashram in the Barodi area of Narayanganj attracts thousands of devotees, especially during the "Barodi Mela"?
A) Ramakrishna
B) Lokenath Brahmachari (Baba Lokenath)
C) Chaitanya Mahaprabhu
D) Anandamayi Ma
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Lokenath Brahmachari (Baba Lokenath)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Narayanganj City Corporation (NCC) was formed in 2011 by merging three existing municipalities.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (Narayanganj, Siddhirganj, and Kadam Rasul)

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, Narayanganj is the...
A) Most densely populated district in Bangladesh
B) Least densely populated district in Bangladesh
C) District with the highest literacy rate
D) District with the lowest population
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Most densely populated district in Bangladesh

Q2. [MCQ] What is the approximate area of Narayanganj District, making it one of the smallest in Bangladesh?
A) 684 sq km
B) 1,200 sq km
C) 2,100 sq km
D) 3,300 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 684 sq km

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] The Tomb of Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah, located in Sonargaon, is the oldest surviving Sultanate-era tomb in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in Narayanganj District?
A) 3
B) 5
C) 7
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5 (Sadar, Bandar, Sonargaon, Rupganj, Araihazar)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, Narayanganj was the headquarters of Sector 3.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was a key part of Sector 2)

Q6. [MCQ] Which Upazila of Narayanganj is particularly known as the "vegetable garden of Dhaka" for its large-scale commercial vegetable production?
A) Sonargaon
B) Bandar
C) Rupganj
D) Araihazar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rupganj (Araihazar is also significant, but Rupganj is more widely cited for this)

Q7. [MCQ] The architecture of Panam Nagar shows a strong influence from which style?
A) Traditional Bengali hut
B) Mughal palace
C) European Colonial and Indo-European
D) Art Deco
CORRECT ANSWER: C) European Colonial and Indo-European

Q8. [MCQ] The "Bibi Mariam's Tomb" and mosque complex in Narayanganj is believed to be the resting place of the daughter of whom?
A) Isa Khan
B) Emperor Akbar
C) Shaista Khan
D) Murshid Quli Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shaista Khan

QD9. [TRUE/FALSE] The main campus of the private "Daffodil International University" is located in Narayanganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in Ashulia, Savar)

Q10. [MCQ] The confluence of which two major rivers occurs near Narayanganj?
A) Padma and Jamuna
B) Shitalakshya and Dhaleshwari
C) Surma and Kushiyara
D) Titas and Meghna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shitalakshya and Dhaleshwari

=== GAZIPUR ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Gazipur is a major industrial city and district located in which division?
A) Mymensingh Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Chittagong Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [MCQ] Gazipur is situated on the banks of which river?
A) Turag River
B) Padma River
C) Jamuna River
D) Meghna River
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Turag River

Q3. [MCQ] Which large, safari-style park is a major tourist attraction in Gazipur?
A) Bhawal National Park
B) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujib Safari Park
C) Lawachara National Park
D) Madhupur National Park
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujib Safari Park

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of the Bangladesh Rice Research Institute (BRRI) is located in Gazipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] The headquarters of which major public university is located in Gazipur?
A) University of Dhaka
B) Jahangirnagar University
C) National University
D) Rajshahi University
CORRECT ANSWER: C) National University

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] Gazipur is well-known for its large garment and textile industry.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The Biswa Ijtema, one of the largest peaceful gatherings of Muslims in the world, is held in which area of Gazipur?
A) Tongi
B) Kaliakair
C) Sreepur
D) Gazipur Sadar
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Tongi

Q8. [MCQ] Which large, man-made forest is another popular recreational spot in Gazipur?
A) Bhawal National Park
B) Ratargul Swamp Forest
C) Sundarbans
D) Nijhum Dwip
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bhawal National Park

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] Gazipur shares a border with the city of Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (It borders Dhaka North)

Q10. [MCQ] The Islamic University of Technology (IUT), a subsidiary of the Organisation of Islamic Cooperation (OIC), is located in...
A) Gazipur
B) Chittagong
C) Sylhet
D) Khulna
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Gazipur

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Gazipur district was historically known as Joydebpur, named after the...
A) Joydebpur Palace
B) A famous local poet
C) A Mughal general
D) A Hindu deity
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Joydebpur Palace

Q2. [MCQ] The Bhawal National Park is predominantly a forest of which type of tree?
A) Mangrove
B) Teak
C) Sal
D) Bamboo
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sal

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] The first armed resistance against the Pakistani army in the 1971 Liberation War is widely considered to have started in Gazipur (Joydebpur).
CORRECT ANSWER: True (on March 19, 1971)

Q4. [MCQ] The historic "Bhawal Sannyasi case" involved a man who claimed to be the deceased...
A) Zamindar of Bhawal
B) A famous poet
C) A British officer
D) A Mughal prince
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Zamindar of Bhawal (Ramendra Narayan Roy Chowdhury)

Q5. [MCQ] Gazipur district was officially formed in which year, separating from Dhaka district?
A) 1971
B) 1984
C) 1991
D) 2001
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1984

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Ordnance Factories (BOF), the main military industrial complex in Bangladesh, is located in Gazipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are there in Gazipur District?
A) 3
B) 5
C) 7
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5 (Gazipur Sadar, Kaliakair, Kaliganj, Kapasia, Sreepur)

Q8. [MCQ] Which major river flows along the eastern border of Gazipur district?
A) Shitalakshya
B) Jamuna
C) Padma
D) Buriganga
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Shitalakshya

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dhaka University of Engineering & Technology (DUET) is located in Gazipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The historic "Tomb of Isa Khan" is located in Sonargaon, but a village in which Upazila of Gazipur is named "Isa Nagar"?
A) Sreepur
B) Kaliganj
C) Kaliakair
D) Kapasia
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kaliganj

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In what year was the Gazipur City Corporation formed, becoming one of the largest city corporations in Bangladesh by area?
A) 2008
B) 2011
C) 2013
D) 2016
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2013

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Gazipur District is approximately 5.26 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Bhawal National Park, established in 1974, covers an area of approximately...
A) 500 acres
B) 2,000 acres
C) 5,022 hectares (12,400 acres)
D) 50,000 hectares
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 5,022 hectares (12,400 acres)

Q4. [MCQ] The first armed resistance in Gazipur on March 19, 1971, was initiated by which Bengali military unit?
A) 1st East Bengal Regiment
B) 2nd East Bengal Regiment
C) 8th East Bengal Regiment
D) East Pakistan Rifles
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2nd East Bengal Regiment

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of the Bangladesh Agricultural Research Institute (BARI) is also located in Gazipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which famous Bengali writer and filmmaker was born in Kapasia, Gazipur?
A) Humayun Ahmed
B) Syed Shamsul Haq
C) Ahsan Habib
D) Tajuddin Ahmad
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Humayun Ahmed

Q7. [MCQ] Tajuddin Ahmad, the first Prime Minister of Bangladesh, was born in which village of Kapasia, Gazipur?
A) Dardaria
B) Taraganj
C) Dhighi
D) Barishab
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Dardaria

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil of Gazipur is primarily composed of the Madhupur Tract, a Pleistocene-era elevated terrace.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Gazipur City Corporation was formed by merging which two former municipalities?
A) Gazipur and Tongi
B) Gazipur and Sreepur
C) Tongi and Joydebpur
D) Gazipur and Konabari
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Gazipur and Tongi

Q10. [MCQ] The "Nuhash Polli", the retreat and filming location of Humayun Ahmed, is located in which Upazila of Gazipur?
A) Gazipur Sadar
B) Sreepur
C) Kaliakair
D) Kapasia
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sreepur

=== BOGRA ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Bogra is a major district and city in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [MCQ] Bogra is often called the "Gateway to..." what region of Bangladesh?
A) North Bengal
B) South Bengal
C) The Hill Tracts
D) The Coastal Region
CORRECT ANSWER: A) North Bengal

Q3. [MCQ] Bogra is famous for the ruins of which ancient city, considered the oldest city in Bangladesh?
A) Paharpur
B) Mainamati
C) Wari-Bateshwar
D) Mahasthangarh
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mahasthangarh

Q4. [MCQ] The city of Bogra is located on the banks of which river?
A) Jamuna
B) Karatoya
C) Padma
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Karatoya

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Bogra is nationally famous for its high-quality sweet curd, known as "Bograr Doi".
CORRECT ANSWER: True
