Q6. [MCQ] The ancient name for the city at Mahasthangarh was...
A) Pundranagar
B) Samatata
C) Gaur
D) Bikrampur
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Pundranagar

Q7. [MCQ] The "Behular Bashor Ghor" (Gokul Medh), a significant archaeological site, is located in Bogra.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] Which two major rivers form the eastern and western boundaries of Bogra district?
A) Padma and Meghna
B) Jamuna and Atrai
C) Titas and Gumti
D) Karatoya and Mahananda
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamuna and Atrai

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] Bogra is a major hub for rice and potato cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The "Nawab Palace" of Bogra, also known as "Mohammad Ali Palace," is a prominent landmark.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Mahasthangarh was the capital of the Pundra Kingdom and was a prosperous city until which century?
A) 3rd Century BC
B) 4th Century AD
C) 8th Century AD
D) 12th Century AD
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 12th Century AD

Q2. [MCQ] Which former President of Bangladesh was born in Bogra?
A) Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
B) Ziaur Rahman
C) Hussain Muhammad Ershad
D) Abdur Rahman Biswas
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ziaur Rahman

Q3. [MCQ] The Karatoya River, which flows through Bogra, is mentioned in which ancient Hindu epic?
A) Ramayana
B) Mahabharata
C) Rigveda
D) Puranas
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Mahabharata

QQ4. [TRUE/FALSE] The Shaheed Chandu Stadium in Bogra is an internationally recognized Test cricket venue.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] The "Vasrhu Bihar" and "Govinda Bhita" are two important archaeological sites located within the...
A) Mainamati complex
B) Paharpur Vihara
C) Mahasthangarh complex
D) Wari-Bateshwar ruins
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mahasthangarh complex

Q6. [MCQ] The rural development framework known as the "Bogra Model" was developed by...
A) The Rural Development Academy (RDA)
B) BRAC
C) Grameen Bank
D) BARD
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Rural Development Academy (RDA)

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Poet's Palace" (Kobi Bari) in Bogra is dedicated to the famous poet Jasimuddin.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is not a major landmark associated with him)

Q8. [MCQ] The Mazar (shrine) of which 11th-century Muslim saint is a major pilgrimage site at Mahasthangarh?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Shah Makhdum
C) Shah Sultan Balkhi
D) Khan Jahan Ali
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Sultan Balkhi

Q9. [MCQ] Bogra district has a specialized "Spice Research Center" (Masla Gobeshona Kendro) located in which upazila?
A) Bogra Sadar
B) Sherpur
C) Shibganj
D) Gabtali
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shibganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil of Bogra is largely part of the Barind Tract, an elevated Pleistocene-era terrace.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] In what year was the Bogra Municipality (Pourashava) established?
A) 1821
B) 1876
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1876

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Bogra District is approximately 3.7 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are there in Bogra District?
A) 9
B) 10
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 12

Q4. [MCQ] The ancient citadel of Pundranagar (Mahasthangarh) was first "discovered" and identified by which British archaeologist?
A) Alexander Cunningham
B) Francis Buchanan-Hamilton
C) James Rennell
D) Mortimer Wheeler
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Francis Buchanan-Hamilton (in 1808)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, Bogra was part of Sector 7.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The distinctive red chili from Bogra, famous for its pungency, is often grown in which Upazila?
A) Sariakandi
B) Dhunat
C) Sonatala
D) All of the above
CORRECT ANSWER: D) All of the above (The char lands of these upazilas are famous for chili)

Q7. [MCQ] The Rural Development Academy (RDA) in Bogra was established in which year?
A) 1959
B) 1971
C) 1974
D) 1982
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1974

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The distance from Mahasthangarh's northern wall to its southern wall is approximately 1,525 metres.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCCON] The "Gokul Medh" (Behular Bashor Ghor) is primarily a...
A) Buddhist stupa
B) Hindu temple podium
C) Muslim tomb
D) Pala-era fortress
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hindu temple podium (believed to be from the Sena dynasty, built on earlier ruins)

Q10. [MCQ] Which of these is a major river that flows through the Sherpur Upazila of Bogra?
A) Bengali River
B) Tista River
C) Surma River
D) Karnaphuli River
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Bengali River

=== JESSORE ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Jessore is a major district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Khulna Division

Q2. [MCQ] Jessore is historically significant for being the...
A) First capital of Bengal
B) First district of Bangladesh (established in 1781)
C) Location of the first university
D) Largest tea-growing region
CORRECT ANSWER: B) First district of Bangladesh (established in 1781)

Q3. [MCQ] Which is the largest and most important land port in Bangladesh, located in Jessore district?
A) Hili
B) Tamabil
C) Benapole
D) Akhaura
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Benapole

Q4. [MCQ] The village of Sagardari in Jessore is the birthplace of which famous Bengali poet?
A) Rabindranath Tagore
B) Kazi Nazrul Islam
C) Michael Madhusudan Dutt
D) Jibanananda Das
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Michael Madhusudan Dutt

Q5. [MCQ] Jessore is often called the "Capital of Flowers" in Bangladesh due to its large-scale flower cultivation, especially in...
A) Godkhali
B) Benapole
C) Jessore Sadar
D) Manirampur
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Godkhali

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kopotakkho River (Kabadak) is famously associated with Michael Madhusudan Dutt's poetry.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] Jessore is nationally famous for its "Nolen Gur" which is a type of...
A) Date palm jaggery
B) Sugarcane candy
C) Sweet curd
D) Puffed rice
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Date palm jaggery

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jessore district shares an international border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (with West Bengal)

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the first-ever digital park in Bangladesh, located in Jessore?
A) Jessore Hi-Tech Park
B) Sheikh Hasina Software Technology Park
C) Bangabandhu Hi-Tech City
D) Digital Bangladesh Park
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sheikh Hasina Software Technology Park

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Air Force Academy (BAF Academy) is located in Jessore.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The name "Jessore" is believed to have come from the word "Jashohar," meaning...
A) "Glory Stripper"
B) "Beautiful Forest"
C) "City of Victory"
D) "River's Edge"
CORRECT ANSWER: A) "Glory Stripper" (as in, it took the glory from Gaur)

Q2. [MCQ] In what year was the Jessore Municipality (Pourashava) established?
A) 1781
B) 1864
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1864

Q3. [MCWHAT] The "Chanchra Rajbari" (Chanchra Palace) in Jessore is a notable example of...
A) Mughal architecture
B) A 12th-century zamindar house
C) A British colonial building
D) An ancient Buddhist monastery
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A 12th-century zamindar house (though mostly ruins)

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, Jessore was the first district in Bangladesh to be liberated from Pakistani forces.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (on December 6, 1971)

Q5. [MCQ] The largest "beel" (wetland) in Jessore district is...
A) Chalan Beel
B) Hakaluki Haor
C) Beel Dakatia
D) Beel Bhabadah
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Beel Bhabadah (known for its waterlogging issues)

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these is a famous 18th-century "Imambara" located in Jessore?
A) Hussaini Dalan
B) Niyamat Imambara
C) Mirzapur Imambara
D) Taltala Imambara
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Niyamat Imambara

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The Jessore Cantonment, established in 1966, is the headquarters of the Bangladesh Army's 55th Infantry Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] Michael Madhusudan Dutt's home at Sagardari is now a museum called...
A) Madhu Palli
B) Kopotakkho Kunjo
C) Sagardari Bhaban
D) Madhusudan Museum
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Madhu Palli

Q9. [MCQ] The "Jessore Comb" (Jeshurer Chira) is a well-known local product. What is it?
A) A type of fish
B) A sweet
C) A handmade decorative comb
D) A type of flattened rice
CORRECT ANSWER: D) A type of flattened rice

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Benapole Land Port handles approximately 90% of all land-based trade between Bangladesh and India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, Jessore was the headquarters of which Sector?
A) Sector 6
B) Sector 7
C) Sector 8
D) Sector 9
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sector 8

Q2. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in Jessore District?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 9
D) 10
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Jessore District is approximately 3.07 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The "Bhawdaha" waterlogging problem in Jessore is primarily caused by...
A) Deforestation
B) Siltation of the Kopotakkho and other rivers
C) Excessive rainfall
D) A tectonic shift
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Siltation of the Kopotakkho and other rivers

QD5. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Chandina" area of Jessore is famous for producing the country's best-quality brass and bell-metal crafts.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (This is more associated with regions like Dhamrai or Jamalpur)

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the 11-domed historic mosque in Abhaynagar, Jessore?
A) Shait Gumbad Mosque
B) Goaldi Mosque
C) Bagdhani Mosque
D) Churiwala Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bagdhani Mosque

Q7. [MCJ] The first public library in Bangladesh, the "Jessore Public Library," was established in...
A) 1854
B) 1899
C) 1921
D) 1952
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1854

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Sheikh Hasina Software Technology Park" in Jessore was inaugurated in 2017.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The "Jessore plate" is a famous breed of what?
A) Cattle
B) Chicken
C) Pigeons
D) Horses
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pigeons

Q10. [MCQ] Before the 1947 partition, Jessore district was part of which administrative division of British India?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Presidency Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Assam Province
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Presidency Division

=== DINAJPUR ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Dinajpur is a major district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Rangpur Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rangpur Division

Q2. [MCQ] Dinajpur is nationally famous for producing which high-quality fruit, often called the "king of fruits"?
A) Mango
B) Jackfruit
C) Litchi (Lychee)
D) Pineapple
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Litchi (Lychee)

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous 18th-century Hindu temple in Dinajpur, known for its intricate terracotta decorations?
A) Kantajew Temple (Kantanagar Temple)
B) Dhakeshwari Temple
C) Puthia Temple Complex
D) Adinath Temple
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Kantajew Temple (Kantanagar Temple)

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Dinajpur district shares an international border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True (with West Bengal)

Q5. [MCQ] Besides litchis, Dinajpur is a major producer of...
A) Tea
B) Fine-grained aromatic rice (Chinigura, Kataribhog)
C) Jute
D) Rubber
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Fine-grained aromatic rice (Chinigura, Kataribhog)

Q6. [MCQ] Which major river flows through Dinajpur town?
A) Jamuna
B) Padma
C) Punarbhaba
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Punarbhaba

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Shopnopuri" is a popular man-made amusement park and tourist spot in Dinajpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] The "Ramsagar" in Dinajpur, a major tourist spot, is a...
A) Large man-made lake (dighi)
B) National park
C) Hill range
D) Mughal fort
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Large man-made lake (dighi)

Q9. [MCQ] The soil in parts of Dinajpur belongs to which elevated Pleistocene-era tract?
A) Madhupur Tract
B) Lalmai Hills
C) Barind Tract
D) Sundarbans
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barind Tract

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Hili Land Port, a major land port for trade with India, is located in Dinajpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Kantajew Temple was built by which Maharaja of Dinajpur?
A) Maharaja Pran Nath and his son Ram Nath
B) Maharaja Surya Kanta
C) Maharaja Jagat Joity
D) Raja Sitaram Ray
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Maharaja Pran Nath and his son Ram Nath

Q2. [MCQ] Which major coal field, one of the largest in Bangladesh, is located in Dinajpur district?
A) Dighipara Coal Field
B) Barapukuria Coal Field
C) Khalashpir Coal Field
D) Jamalganj Coal Field
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Barapukuria Coal Field

Q3. [MCQ] The Barapukuria Coal Mine is unique in Bangladesh because it is the only...
A) Open-pit mine
B) Active underground mine
C) Mine operated by a private company
D) Mine that also produces oil
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Active underground mine

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] The Teesta River forms the eastern border of Dinajpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The Jamuna River is far to the east; the Teesta is further north and east of Dinajpur)

Q5. [MCQ] The "Ghughu-danga Zamindar Bari" is a historical site in which upazila of Dinajpur?
A) Dinajpur Sadar
B) Parbatipur
C) Ghoraghat
D) Hakimpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ghoraghat

Q6. [MCQ] The economy of Dinajpur is heavily reliant on agriculture, and it is often referred to as the...
A) "Textile Hub of the North"
B) "Fisheries Capital"
C) "Breadbasket of Bangladesh"
D) "Tea Kingdom"
CORRECT ANSWER: C) "Breadbasket of Bangladesh"

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dinajpur Rajbari (palace) is now completely in ruins.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (While parts are dilapidated, significant structures and a temple still exist and are visited)

Q8. [MCQ] In which year was the Ramsagar Lake excavated by Maharaja Ram Nath?
A) 1650s
B) 1750s
C) 1850s
D) 1950s
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1750s (to provide water during a severe famine)

Q9. [MCQ] Parbatipur in Dinajpur is a major national hub for...
A) River ports
B) Railway junctions and workshops
C) Air force training
D) Software technology
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Railway junctions and workshops

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Kataribhog" rice from Dinajpur has received a Geographical Indication (GI) tag.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, the majority of Dinajpur district was part of which Sector?
A) Sector 6
B) Sector 7
C) Sector 8
D) Sector 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sector 7 (Some parts were also under Sector 6)

Q2. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in Dinajpur District?
A) 9
B) 11
C) 13
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 13

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Dinajpur District is approximately 3.3 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The Kantajew Temple, when originally built, had nine spires (ratnas), making it a "Nava-ratna" temple. When did it lose its spires?
A) During the 1971 war
B) During the 1947 partition
C) In a major earthquake in 1897
D) Due to a cyclone in 1965
CORRECT ANSWER: C) In a major earthquake in 1897

Q5. [MCQ] The Barapukuria Thermal Power Plant in Dinajpur is notable for being...
A) Solar-powered
B) Nuclear-powered
C) Coal-fired
D) Hydro-powered
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Coal-fired (using domestic coal from the adjacent mine)

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science and Technology University (HSTU) is located in Dinajpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The "Singra Forest", a natural Sal forest, is located in which upazila of Dinajpur?
A) Birganj
B) Hakimpur
C) Biral
D) Kaharole
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Birganj

Q8. [MCQ] Which of these rivers does not flow through Dinajpur district?
A) Punarbhaba
B) Atrai
C) Dhepa
D) Titas
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Titas (The Titas is in the Comilla/Brahmanbaria region)

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic "Ghoraghat Fort" was a significant administrative and military center during the early Mughal period.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The "Chehelgazi Mazar" in Dinajpur is a shrine dedicated to...
A) A famous poet
B) A Mughal governor
C) 40 (chehel) unknown warriors/saints
D) A 19th-century zamindar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 40 (chehel) unknown warriors/saints

=== PABNA ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Pabna is a major district and city located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [MCQ] Pabna city is located on the north bank of which major river?
A) Jamuna River
B) Padma River
C) Meghna River
D) Karatoya River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Padma River

QGET. [MCQ] The Hardinge Bridge, a famous steel railway bridge, is located near Pabna over the...
A) Jamuna River
B) Padma River
C) Meghna River
D) Shitalakshya River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Padma River (It connects Pabna and Kushtia districts)

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Pabna is nationally famous for its traditional handloom (taant) industry.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] Which famous film actress of the Indian subcontinent was born in Pabna?
A) Nargis
B) Madhubala
C) Suchitra Sen
D) Kabori Sarwar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Suchitra Sen

Q6. [MCQ] Pabna is also famous for its high-quality "ghee" and a sweet called...
A) Roshomalai
B) Balish Misti
C) Chomchom
D) Pera Sandesh
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Pera Sandesh

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the large wetland (beel) that covers a significant part of Pabna district?
A) Chalan Beel
B) Tanguar Haor
C) Hakaluki Haor
D) Beel Dakatia
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Chalan Beel

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Pabna Mental Hospital is the oldest and largest mental hospital in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The confluence of which two major rivers occurs near the Pabna district?
A) Teesta and Brahmaputra
B) Surma and Kushiyara
C) Padma and Jamuna
D) Meghna and Padma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma and Jamuna (at Goalondo, near Pabna)

Q10. [MCQ] Which major nuclear power plant is being constructed in the Rooppur area of Pabna?
A) Pabna Nuclear Power Plant
B) Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant
C) Bangladesh Nuclear Power Plant
D) Padma Nuclear Power Plant
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Lalon Shah Bridge, a major road bridge, runs parallel to which other bridge near Pabna?
A) Jamuna Bridge
B) Meghna Bridge
C) Hardinge Bridge
D) Bhairab Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Hardinge Bridge

Q2. [MCQ] In what year was the Hardinge Bridge officially opened for railway traffic?
A) 1899
B) 1905
C) 1915
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1915

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Pabna Uprising" (Pabna Bidroho) of 1873-1876 was a peasant movement against the local zamindars.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The ancestral home of Suchitra Sen, now a museum, is located in...
A) Pabna Sadar
B) Ishwardi
C) Chatmohar
D) Sujanagar
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Pabna Sadar

Q5. [MCQ] Which Upazila of Pabna is a major railway junction and home to the Ishwardi Airport?
A) Pabna Sadar
B) Atgharia
C) Ishwardi
D) Sathia
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ishwardi

Q6. [MCQ] The "Shahzadpur Mosque" in Pabna district is a well-preserved example of...
A) Mughal architecture
B) Colonial architecture
C) Pre-Mughal Sultanate architecture
D) Modern architecture
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pre-Mughal Sultanate architecture

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] The Pabna University of Science and Technology (PUST) is the main public university in the district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] The name "Pabna" is believed to be derived from...
A) A Mughal governor
B) A type of grass (Paban)
C) A Hindu deity
D) The name of a local king
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A type of grass (Paban)

Q9. [MCQ] The "Square Group," one of Bangladesh's largest industrial conglomerates (especially in pharmaceuticals), was founded in Pabna.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The Chalan Beel is a...
A) Single large lake
B) Series of interconnected wetlands, channels, and smaller beels
C) Man-made reservoir
D) Mountain valley
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Series of interconnected wetlands, channels, and smaller beels

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, Pabna was a part of which Sector?
A) Sector 7
B) Sector 8
C) Sector 9
D) Sector 11
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sector 7 (Some parts were also under Sector 8)

Q2. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in Pabna District?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Pabna District is approximately 2.86 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant is being built in collaboration with which country's state atomic energy corporation?
A) United States
B) China
C) India
D) Russia (Rosatom)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Russia (Rosatom)

Q5. [MCQ] The Hardinge Bridge was designed by Sir...
A) Robert Napier
B) Alexander Meadows Rendel
C) Robert William Gales
D) Louis Kahn
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Alexander Meadows Rendel (Gales was the engineer in charge of construction)

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Pabna Peasant Uprising" led to the passage of the Bengal Tenancy Act of 1885.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The "Jor Bangla Temple" in Pabna, a rare example of its architectural style, is located in which Upazila?
A) Pabna Sadar
B) Sujanagar
C) Chatmohar
D) Bera
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Pabna Sadar (in the village of Gunaighara)

Q8. [MCQ] Which famous leader of the "Faraizi Movement" was born in Pabna?
A) Titumir
B) Haji Shariatullah
C) Dudu Miyan
D) Maulana Abdul Hamid Khan Bhashani
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Haji Shariatullah

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The Ishwardi Export Processing Zone (EPZ) is a major industrial zone in the district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] Which of these is a major river port in Pabna, located in the Bera Upazila?
A) Nagarbari Ghat
B) Goalondo Ghat
C) Sadarghat
D) Benapole
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Nagarbari Ghat

=== TANGAIL ===

--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Tangail is a prominent district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Mymensingh Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [MCQ] Tangail is world-famous for what traditional handloom product?
A) Muslin
B) Jamdani
C) Tangail Saree
D) Khadi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tangail Saree

Q3. [MCQ] The Bangabandhu Bridge, a major multipurpose bridge, crosses which river to connect Tangail with Sirajganj?
A) Padma River
B) Jamuna River
C) Meghna River
D) Shitalakshya River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamuna River

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Tangail is famous for a unique sweet delicacy called "Chomchom".
CORRECT ANSWER: True (The "Porabari Chomchom" is from Tangail)

Q5. [MCQ] Which famous political leader, known as the "Red Maulana," is buried in Tangail?
A) Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
B) Hussain Muhammad Ershad
C) Maulana Abdul Hamid Khan Bhashani
D) Tajuddin Ahmad
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Maulana Abdul Hamid Khan Bhashani

Q6. [MCQ] The Madhupur Tract, a large elevated area of older soil, is a major geographical feature of Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The Madhupur Tract is home to a large forest of which type of tree?
A) Sal
B) Mangrove
C) Teak
D) Pine
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sal

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Atia Mosque," a historic 17th-century mosque, is located in Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which river is the main river flowing through Tangail district (not just bordering it)?
A) Jamuna
B) Dhaleshwari
C) Padma
D) Surma
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaleshwari

Q10. [MCQ] The Jamuna Bridge (Bangabandhu Bridge) is a...
A) Road bridge only
B) Railway bridge only
C) Road and railway bridge
D) Road, railway, and power grid bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Road, railway, and power grid bridge (it also carries gas pipelines)

--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Tangail Saree was officially recognized as a Geographical Indication (GI) product of Bangladesh in...
A) 2010
B) 2016
C) 2020
D) 2024
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 2024

Q2. [MCQ] The Maulana Bhashani Science and Technology University (MBSTU) is located in...
A) Tangail Sadar
B) Madhupur
C) Ghatail
D) Kalihati
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Tangail Sadar

Q3. [MCQ] The "Porabari" area of Tangail, famous for its Chomchom, is located on the banks of which river?
A) Jamuna
B) Dhaleshwari
C) Pungli
D) Lohajang
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaleshwari

Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] The Madhupur National Park is located within the Madhupur Sal Forest in Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q5. [MCQ] Which famous freedom fighter and military commander (Sector 11) was born in Tangail?
A) Ziaur Rahman
B) M. A. G. Osmani
C) Kader Siddique (Bagha Siddique)
D) Khaled Mosharraf
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kader Siddique (Bagha Siddique)

Q6. [MCQ] The historic Atia Mosque, built in 1609, is famously depicted on which Bangladeshi taka note?
A) 5 Taka note
B) 10 Taka note
C) 20 Taka note
D) 100 Taka note
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 10 Taka note

Q7. [TRUE/FALSE] Tangail was originally a part of the greater Mymensingh district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q8. [MCQ] The "Dhanbari Nawab Palace" (Nawab Manzil) is a historic landmark in which upazila of Tangail?
A) Madhupur
B) Dhanbari
C) Gopalpur
D) Bhuapur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhanbari

Q9. [MCQ] The name "Tangail" is said to have originated from the word "Tangail," which refers to...
A) A type of fishing net
B) A high place or "ail"
C) A Mughal general
D) A type of boat
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A high place or "ail" (referring to a high point in the "ail" or dam-like paths in the beel)

Q10. [MCQ] Which ethnic minority group is predominantly found in the Madhupur area of Tangail?
A) Chakma
B) Marma
C) Garo (Mandi)
D) Santal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Garo (Mandi)

--- HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, Tangail was the headquarters of which famous guerrilla force?
A) Bengal Tigers
B) Kaderia Bahini
C) Mukti Bahini Sector 9
D) Crack Platoon
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kaderia Bahini

Q2. [MCQ] As of 2025, how many Upazilas are in Tangail District?
A) 10
B) 12
C) 14
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 12

Q3. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Population and Housing Census, the population of Tangail District is approximately 4.03 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q4. [MCQ] The "Mohera Zamindar Bari," now a Police Training Center, is a massive 19th-century palace complex in which upazila?
A) Mirzapur
B) Kalihati
C) Nagarpur
D) Basail
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Mirzapur

Q5. [MCQ] In which year was the Bangabandhu Bridge (Jamuna Bridge) officially inaugurated?
A) 1991
B) 1998
C) 2001
D) 2005
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1998

Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Kumudini Hospital," founded by philanthropist R. P. Saha, is a major healthcare institution in Mirzapur, Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q7. [MCQ] The "Kaderia Bahini" operated largely within the area of which official Liberation War Sector?
A) Sector 2
B) Sector 7
C) Sector 9
D) Sector 11
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sector 11

Q8. [MCQ] Which of these is a major river port in Tangail, located on the Jamuna river?
A) Nagarbari
B) Elasin Ghat
C) Bhuapur
D) All of the above
CORRECT ANSWER: D) All of the above (Bhuapur and Elasin are key ghats in Tangail)

Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Tangail Football Training Centre" is the first and only FIFA-funded football academy in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The BFF academy is in Dhaka; Sylhet has a BKSP academy. This is not a major fact for Tangail)
REVISED Q9. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dhaleshwari River is a distributary of the Jamuna River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q10. [MCQ] The "Mymensingh Gitika" ballads, collected by Dinesh Chandra Sen, include folk stories from the greater Mymensingh region, which included Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True


=== Jamalpur ===
--- EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---
Q1. [MCQ] Jamalpur District is located in which division of Bangladesh? 
A) Chittagong Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division
Q2. [MCQ] How many upazilas does Jamalpur District have? 
A) 5
B) 6
C) 7
D) 8
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 7
Q3. [MCQ] Jamalpur is officially known as the Land of which traditional handicraft? 
A) Jamdani Saree
B) Nakshi Kantha (embroidered quilt)
C) Dokra Brassware
D) Shital Pati (mat weaving)
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nakshi Kantha (embroidered quilt)
Q4. [TRUE/FALSE] Jamalpur is officially branded as the Land of Nakshi Kantha by the government of Bangladesh. 
CORRECT ANSWER: True
Q5. [MCQ] In which year was Jamalpur District officially established? 
A) 1971
B) 1978
C) 1990
D) 2001
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1978
Q6. [MCQ] Jamalpur District shares an international border with which Indian state? 
A) Assam
B) West Bengal
C) Meghalaya
D) Tripura
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Meghalaya
Q7. [MCQ] The main town of Jamalpur is situated on the bank of which river? 
A) Jamuna River
B) Old Brahmaputra River
C) Meghna River
D) Padma River
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Old Brahmaputra River
Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jamalpur Sadar Upazila is the largest upazila of Jamalpur District by area. 
CORRECT ANSWER: True
Q9. [MCQ] According to the 2022 census, Jamalpur Districts population is closest to which figure? 
A) 1.0 million
B) 1.5 million
C) 2.5 million
D) 3.0 million
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2.5 million
Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Over 99% of the households in Jamalpur District have access to electricity. 
CORRECT ANSWER: True
--- MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---
Q1. [MCQ] Which significant historical movement against British indigo planters took place in Jamalpur? 
A) Fakir-Sannyasi Resistance (17721790)
B) Indigo Rebellion (1829)
C) Sepoy Mutiny (1857)
D) Non-cooperation Movement (1920)
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Indigo Rebellion (1829)
Q2. [MCQ] The Battle of Kamalpur during the 1971 Liberation War took place in which upazila of Jamalpur?
A) Sarishabari
B) Dewanganj
C) Bakshiganj
D) Madarganj
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bakshiganj
Q3. [MCQ] In which decade was the Jamalpur Gandhi Ashram established? 
A) 1920s
B) 1930s
C) 1940s
D) 1950s
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1930s
Q4. [MCQ] The Jamalpur Freedom Struggle Museum was founded in which year? 
A) 1991
B) 2001
C) 2007
D) 2015
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2007
Q5. [MCQ] Which major state-owned factory is located in Jamalpur District? 
A) Ghorashal Urea Fertilizer Factory
B) Jamuna Fertilizer Company Limited
C) Titas Gas Transmission Company
D) Bogura Textile Mill
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamuna Fertilizer Company Limited
Q6. [TRUE/FALSE] Bangladesh Economic Zones Authority (BEZA) has established an economic zone in Jamalpur to promote industrial development. 
CORRECT ANSWER: True
Q7. [MCQ] What was Jamalpur Districts literacy rate (age 7+) according to the 2022 census? 
A) 45.2%
B) 61.7%
C) 74.8%
D) 85.3%
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 61.7%
Q8. [MCQ] Which sector is the dominant source of income in Jamalpur District? 
A) Agriculture
B) Industry
C) Tourism
D) Remittances (foreign income)
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Agriculture
Q9. [MCQ] What traditional folk sport involving sticks is practiced in rural Jamalpur? 
A) Dhopkhel
B) Lathi Khela
C) Kabbadi
D) Malla Yuddha (wrestling)
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Lathi Khela
Q10. [MCQ] Which local dish is considered a culinary speciality of Jamalpur? 
A) Biriyani
B) Pithali (millet porridge)
C) Pitha (rice cake)
D) Rasgulla (sweet)
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pithali (millet porridge)

B) 2,115 km
C) 2,500 km
D) 3,000 km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,115 km

B) 2200'2300' N
C) 2434'2526' N
D) 2600'2700' N

B) 800 per km
C) 1,182 per km

B) Dewanganj
C) Bakshiganj
D) Sarishabari
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bakshiganj

A) 950
B) 1000
C) 1055
D) 1100

A) Jamalpur Sadar
B) Sarishabari
C) Melandaha
D) Islampur

A) 10.5%
B) 19.1%
C) 25.0%
D) 33.3%
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 19.1%

CORRECT ANSWER: True
Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The former name of Jamalpur District was Shinghajani.

=== RAJSHAHI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Rajshahi is situated on the banks of which major river?
A) Jamuna
B) Meghna
C) Padma
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi is widely known as the "Silk City" of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Varendra Research Museum, one of the oldest museums in Bangladesh, is located in which city?
A) Khulna
B) Rajshahi
C) Bogra
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rajshahi

Q4. [MCQ] Besides silk, Rajshahi is nationally famous for producing which fruit?
A) Jackfruit
B) Pineapple
C) Lychee
D) Mango
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mango

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi belongs to the Khulna Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Puthia Temple Complex, a famous archaeological site with numerous Hindu temples, is located in which district?
A) Dinajpur
B) Comilla
C) Rajshahi
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi

Q7. [MCQ] What is a common nickname for Rajshahi due to its focus on universities and colleges?
A) The City of Lakes
B) The Royal City
C) The Education City
D) The Garden City
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Education City

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Shah Makhdum Airport serves the city of Rajshahi.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Rajshahi is located in which geographical part of Bangladesh?
A) Southeastern
B) Northwestern
C) Southwestern
D) Northeastern
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Northwestern

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of the Rajshahi Krishi Unnayan Bank (RAKUB), a specialized bank for agriculture, is located in Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Varendra Research Museum was established in which year, making it the first museum in what was then East Bengal?
A) 1890
B) 1910
C) 1925
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1910

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The magnificent Pancharatna Govinda Temple in the Puthia Temple Complex is noted for its exquisite terracotta ornamentation depicting the stories of Radha and Krishna.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The region of Rajshahi was historically part of an ancient territory known as:
A) Samatata
B) Varendra (Barind)
C) Harikela
D) Gauda
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Varendra (Barind)

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Rajshahi district?
A) 5
B) 9
C) 12
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The silk industry in Rajshahi began to flourish significantly after the independence of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following institutions is located in Rajshahi?
A) Bangladesh Agricultural University
B) University of Chittagong
C) University of Rajshahi
D) Islamic University of Technology
CORRECT ANSWER: C) University of Rajshahi

Q7. [MCQ] The ancient city of Pundra Kingdom, whose capital was near modern-day Rajshahi, was known as:
A) Mahasthangarh
B) Vikrampur
C) Vijayanagara
D) Gauda
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Vijayanagara

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The main administrative body of the city is the Rajshahi City Corporation (RCC).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The great Shiva Temple in Puthia, considered the largest in Bangladesh, was built by which Rani of the Puthia Royal Family?
A) Rani Bhabani
B) Rani Lakshmipriya
C) Rani Vobonmoyee
D) Rani Premmoyee
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rani Vobonmoyee

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajshahi has a significantly lower population density compared to Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The establishment of the Varendra Research Society, the precursor to the museum, was led by which three prominent figures?
A) A.K. Fazlul Huq, Huseyn Shaheed Suhrawardy, and Khwaja Nazimuddin
B) Kumar Sarat Kumar Ray, Aksaya Kumar Maitreya, and Ramaprasad Chanda
C) Jagadish Chandra Bose, Prafulla Chandra Roy, and Satyendra Nath Bose
D) Rabindranath Tagore, Kazi Nazrul Islam, and Jasimuddin

B) 1876

B) Education

D) Trading

A) 1692
B) 1723
C) 1778
D) 1823
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1778

Q7. [MCQ] The area of Rajshahi was part of the zamindari of which powerful Pathan jagirdar before it was granted to the ancestor of the Puthia Raj family by the Mughals?
A) Isa Khan
B) Lashker Khan
C) Usman Khan
D) Bayazid Karrani
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Lashker Khan

B) Jahangir

=== KHULNA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Khulna is the headquarters of which administrative division?
A) Barisal Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna is considered the gateway to the Sundarbans, the world's largest mangrove forest.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Mongla, the second-largest seaport in Bangladesh, is located in the Khulna Division.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q4. [MCQ] Khulna city is situated on the banks of which two rivers?
A) Padma and Jamuna
B) Rupsha and Bhairab
C) Karnaphuli and Halda
D) Surma and Kushiara
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rupsha and Bhairab

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna is primarily a hilly region with high elevations.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major industry historically associated with Khulna?
A) Silk production
B) Tea processing
C) Jute mills
D) Leather tanning
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jute mills

Q7. [MCQ] The famous Khan Jahan Ali Bridge is built over which river in Khulna?
A) Pasur River
B) Bhairab River
C) Rupsha River
D) Shibsa River
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rupsha River

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna University of Engineering & Technology (KUET) is a prominent educational institution in the city.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Khulna is located in which geographical part of Bangladesh?
A) Northeastern
B) Northern
C) Southeastern
D) Southwestern
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Southwestern

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The main naval base in Khulna is named BNS Titumir.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Port of Mongla was originally founded in 1950 and was known by what name?
A) Jessore Port
B) Rupsha Port
C) Bhairab Port
D) Chalna Port
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chalna Port

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna Shipyard, a major shipbuilding and repair facility, is operated by the Bangladesh Navy.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Khulna district was officially formed in 1882 by combining subdivisions from which two existing districts?
A) Dhaka and Faridpur
B) Jessore and 24 Parganas
C) Barisal and Patuakhali
D) Pabna and Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jessore and 24 Parganas

Q4. [MCQ] Which saint is credited with establishing the first Muslim settlements in the greater Khulna-Sundarbans region in the 14th century?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Bayazid Bostami
C) Khan Jahan Ali
D) Shah Makhdum
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khan Jahan Ali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate in Khulna District is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The economy of Khulna is significantly supported by the processing and export of which product?
A) Tea
B) Rubber
C) Shrimp and frozen seafood
D) Spices
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shrimp and frozen seafood

Q7. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Khulna district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, the first encounter between the Pak army and freedom fighters in Khulna took place at the Gallamari Radio Station.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Mongla port is situated at the confluence of which two rivers?
A) Rupsha and Bhairab
B) Bhairab and Shibsa
C) Pasur and Mongla
D) Arpangachhia and Koyra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pasur and Mongla

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Khulna does not have an Export Processing Zone (EPZ).
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] Khulna Shipyard was originally established in 1957 with technical support from which country?
A) United Kingdom
B) Soviet Union
C) West Germany
D) Japan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) West Germany

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Before the Bangladesh Navy took over in 1999, Khulna Shipyard was a consistently profitable state-owned enterprise.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) 2,845 sq km
B) 3,789 sq km
C) 4,394 sq km
D) 5,123 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 4,394 sq km

A) Dacope
B) Batiaghata
C) Paikgachha
D) Terokhada
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Paikgachha

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the Hindu population percentage in Khulna District is higher than the Muslim population percentage.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Vanga
B) Samatata
C) Khalifatabad
D) Jessore Kingdom
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jessore Kingdom

C) Savar Cantonment

CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) 7.5 meters
B) 8.5 meters
C) 9.5 meters
D) 10.5 meters
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 9.5 meters

B) Meghna

=== COMILLA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Comilla is a district in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Sylhet Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous sweet dish "Roshmalai" is a specialty of Comilla.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The ancient Buddhist archaeological site of Mainamati is located in which district?
A) Bogra
B) Naogaon
C) Comilla
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Comilla

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the large, historic water tank (dighi) located in the heart of Comilla city?
A) Ramsagar
B) Dharmasagar
C) Kamlasagar
D) Dudhsagar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dharmasagar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Comilla is famous for its hand-loomed textile product known as Khadi or Khaddar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Bangladesh Academy for Rural Development (BARD), a renowned research and training institute, is located in:
A) Savar
B) Gazipur
C) Kotbari, Comilla
D) Pahartali, Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kotbari, Comilla

Q7. [MCQ] Which major national highway connects Dhaka to Comilla?
A) N1 (Dhaka-Chittagong Highway)
B) N3 (Dhaka-Mymensingh Highway)
C) N5 (Dhaka-Rangpur Highway)
D) N8 (Dhaka-Barisal Highway)
CORRECT ANSWER: A) N1 (Dhaka-Chittagong Highway)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Gumti River flows through the Comilla district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Comilla War Cemetery contains the burials of soldiers who died during which conflict?
A) The Sepoy Mutiny of 1857
B) World War I
C) The Bangladesh Liberation War of 1971
D) World War II
CORRECT ANSWER: D) World War II

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Comilla is a coastal district bordering the Bay of Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Historically, the district of Comilla was known by what name?
A) Samatata
B) Vanga
C) Tippera (Tripura)
D) Gauda
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tippera (Tripura)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The renowned musician and composer S.D. Burman (Sachin Dev Burman) was born into the royal family of Tripura, which is historically linked to Comilla.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Mainamati archaeological site is primarily known for the ruins of numerous Buddhist:
A) Stupas and Chaityas
B) Viharas (monasteries)
C) Royal Palaces
D) Fortifications
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Viharas (monasteries)

Q4. [MCQ] Dhirendranath Datta, who first demanded Bengali to be a state language in the Constituent Assembly of Pakistan in 1948, was from which district?
A) Faridpur
B) Dhaka
C) Barisal
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Comilla

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The "Comilla Model" of rural development, pioneered by Akhtar Hameed Khan at BARD, became famous internationally.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Comilla district?
A) 12
B) 15
C) 17
D) 19
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 17

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is the most prominent excavated monastery at the Mainamati site?
A) Ananda Vihara
B) Shalban Vihara
C) Somapura Mahavihara
D) Jagaddala Mahavihara
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shalban Vihara

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Comilla Victorians are a franchise team in the Bangladesh Premier League (BPL) for cricket.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The original Roshmalai of Comilla was pioneered by which confectioner family?
A) Ghosh family (Matri Bhandar)
B) Saha family
C) Dutta family
D) Pal family
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Ghosh family (Matri Bhandar)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kazi Nazrul Islam Memorial Hall is located in Comilla, commemorating the poet's stay in the city.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Mainamati ruins are located on a series of low hills known as the:
A) Chittagong Hill Tracts
B) Garo Hills
C) Lalmai-Mainamati hill range
D) Madhupur Tract
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lalmai-Mainamati hill range

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Comilla district was formed in 1790 by the British, and its original headquarters was in the city of Daudkandi.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] The copper plates found at Mainamati provide evidence of which ruling dynasty between the 7th and 8th centuries AD?
A) The Pala Dynasty
B) The Sena Dynasty
C) The Deva Dynasty
D) The Gupta Dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Deva Dynasty

Q4. [MCQ] Shib Narayan Das, one of the designers of the first flag of Bangladesh, was a student activist from which city?
A) Dhaka
B) Chittagong
C) Comilla
D) Jessore
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Comilla

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the population density of Comilla District is higher than that of Chittagong District.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Dharmasagar tank was excavated in 1714 by which Maharaja of Tripura to provide water to the local population?
A) Maharaja Krishna Kishore Manikya
B) Maharaja Dharma Manikya I
C) Maharaja Govinda Manikya
D) Maharaja Birchandra Manikya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Maharaja Dharma Manikya I

Q7. [MCQ] The establishment of the Comilla Cooperative Karkhana, a key part of the "Comilla Model," focused primarily on what?
A) Textile manufacturing
B) Production and maintenance of agricultural machinery
C) Food processing
D) Handicrafts marketing
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Production and maintenance of agricultural machinery

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Comilla Cantonment, established during World War II, is one of the largest in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] General M. A. G. Osmani, the Commander-in-Chief of the Bangladesh Forces during the 1971 Liberation War, had a political constituency in which region?
A) Sylhet
B) Dhaka
C) Comilla
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sylhet

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Comilla is believed to have been derived from the ancient term "Kamalanka," which means "City of Lotuses."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== NARAYANGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Narayanganj is a major river port city located in which division?
A) Chittagong Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The city of Narayanganj is situated on the banks of the Shitalakshya River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is a common nickname for Narayanganj due to its historical importance in the textile trade?
A) The Port City
B) The Silk City
C) The Dundee of Bangladesh
D) The Tea Capital
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Dundee of Bangladesh

Q4. [MCQ] The historic Sonargaon, once the capital of Bengal, is located in which present-day district?
A) Munshiganj
B) Dhaka
C) Gazipur
D) Narayanganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Narayanganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj is known for its large-scale production of mangoes.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The traditional Jamdani sari, a UNESCO recognized cultural heritage, is primarily woven in which district?
A) Tangail
B) Rajshahi
C) Narayanganj
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Narayanganj

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous historical fort located in Narayanganj?
A) Lalbagh Fort
B) Hajiganj Fort
C) Mahasthangarh
D) Idrakpur Fort
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hajiganj Fort

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kanchpur Bridge connects Narayanganj with the capital city, Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Panam Nagar, a historic and abandoned city of wealthy Hindu merchants, is a major tourist attraction in:
A) Comilla
B) Sonargaon, Narayanganj
C) Puthia, Rajshahi
D) Bagerhat
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sonargaon, Narayanganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj is one of the oldest municipalities in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Who was the powerful 15th-century ruler of the Bhati region who established his capital in Sonargaon?
A) Shaista Khan
B) Islam Khan
C) Isa Khan
D) Murshid Quli Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Isa Khan

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Narayanganj is believed to have originated from Bicon Lal Pandey, a Hindu religious leader who was also known as Benur Thakur or 'Laxmi Narayan Thakur'.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Bangladesh Folk Art and Craft Foundation Museum is located in which historic area?
A) Panam Nagar
B) Bara Sardarbari, Sonargaon
C) Hajiganj Fort
D) Kadam Rasul Shrine
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bara Sardarbari, Sonargaon

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) does the Narayanganj district have?
A) 3
B) 5
C) 7
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The first jute mill in what is now Bangladesh was established in Narayanganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Hajiganj Fort was built by the Mughals on the bank of the Shitalakshya river to protect Dhaka from what threat?
A) British invaders
B) Arakanese and Portuguese pirates
C) Land-based rebels from the north
D) Burmese invasion
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Arakanese and Portuguese pirates

Q7. [MCQ] In which year was the Narayanganj City Corporation officially formed?
A) 1991
B) 2001
C) 2011
D) 2015
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2011

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous Goaldi Mosque in Sonargaon was built during the Sultanate period, predating Mughal rule.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The tomb of which renowned Mughal general, who fought against Isa Khan, is located in Narayanganj?
A) Man Singh I
B) Mir Jumla II
C) Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah
D) Shaista Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Narayanganj has the highest population density of any district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The renowned Moroccan traveler Ibn Battuta visited Sonargaon in the 14th century during the reign of which sultan?
A) Shamsuddin Ilyas Shah
B) Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah
C) Sikandar Shah
D) Fakhruddin Mubarak Shah
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Fakhruddin Mubarak Shah

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Adamjee Jute Mills in Narayanganj was once the largest jute mill in the world.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Panam Nagar is architecturally unique for its fusion of which two styles?
A) Mughal and Persian
B) Traditional Bengali and Indo-Islamic
C) European colonial and Mughal
D) Neoclassical and Art Deco
CORRECT ANSWER: C) European colonial and Mughal

Q4. [MCQ] The shrine of Kadam Rasul is revered for supposedly containing the footprint of which religious figure?
A) The Prophet Muhammad (PBUH)
B) Hazrat Shah Jalal (R)
C) Isa Khan
D) Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Prophet Muhammad (PBUH)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate in Narayanganj District is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Narayanganj District in square kilometers, making it one of the smallest districts in Bangladesh?
A) 684 sq km
B) 950 sq km
C) 1,210 sq km
D) 1,530 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 684 sq km

Q7. [MCQ] The construction of the Goaldi Mosque is attributed to which year during the reign of Sultan Alauddin Hussain Shah?
A) 1493
B) 1519
C) 1555
D) 1582
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1519

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before the rise of Narayanganj as a port, Saptagram (in modern-day West Bengal) was the dominant port of the region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic 'Tin Murti' (Three Figures) sculpture in Sonargaon was created by which famous Indian artist?
A) Nandalal Bose
B) Jamini Roy
C) Ramkinkar Baij
D) Subodh Gupta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ramkinkar Baij

CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== GAZIPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Gazipur is a major city in which administrative division?

D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Dhaka Division

A) Mymensingh
B) Gazipur
C) Savar
D) Bogra

A) Jessore
B) Cox's Bazar
C) Gazipur
D) Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gazipur

A) University of Dhaka
B) Bangladesh University of Engineering and Technology (BUET)
C) Islamic University of Technology (IUT)

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Islamic University of Technology (IUT)

A) The Royal City
B) The Gateway to Dhaka
C) The City of Lakes
D) The Industrial City

A) Dhaka
B) Gopalganj
C) Gazipur
D) Kushtia
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gazipur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Gazipur is a coastal district with direct access to the Bay of Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] Historically, the area of Gazipur was known as the center of the Bhawal Estate or Bhawal Pargana, ruled by which zamindar family?

C) The Roys of Bhawal
D) The Palas of Bengal

B) 5

D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

CORRECT ANSWER: False

B) Yusu Shah

D) Hussain Shah

Q7. [MCQ] The National University of Bangladesh, the world's fifth-largest university by enrollment, has its headquarters in which district?

B) Chittagong
C) Gazipur

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gazipur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Tongi, a major industrial area, is part of the Gazipur City Corporation.

=== BOGRA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Bogra district is located in which administrative division?
A) Rangpur Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The ancient archaeological site of Mahasthangarh, the oldest known city in Bangladesh, is located in Bogra.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is Bogra famously known as in the context of Northern Bangladesh?
A) The Tea Capital
B) The Silk City
C) The Gateway to North Bengal
D) The Rice Bowl
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Gateway to North Bengal

Q4. [MCQ] Bogra is renowned for producing which dairy product, a specialty of the region?
A) Cheese
B) Ghee
C) Butter
D) Sweet Curd (Doi)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sweet Curd (Doi)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Jamuna River flows directly through the middle of Bogra town.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Shaheed Chandu Stadium, an international cricket venue, is located in which city?
A) Rajshahi
B) Rangpur
C) Bogra
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bogra

Q7. [MCQ] The historic Behular Bashor Ghor (Gokul Medh), associated with a famous folk tale, is located in which district?
A) Dinajpur
B) Naogaon
C) Bogra
D) Joypurhat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bogra

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The district of Bogra was named after Sultan Ghiyasuddin Iwaj Shah.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Prafulla Chaki, a famous revolutionary of the anti-British independence movement, was born in which district?
A) Mymensingh
B) Kushtia
C) Chittagong
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bogra

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in the Bogra region is highly suitable for potato cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The ancient city at Mahasthangarh was known by what name, serving as the capital of the Pundra Kingdom?
A) Pundranagara
B) Gauda
C) Samatata
D) Varendra
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Pundranagara

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Karatoya River, mentioned in the ancient Mahabharata, flows past the ruins of Mahasthangarh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Bogra town was established and named in 1821 in honor of whom?
A) The Mughal emperor Aurangzeb
B) The British collector Mr. Bogel
C) The local zamindar Bogra Khan
D) Sultan Nasiruddin Bughra Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sultan Nasiruddin Bughra Khan

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Bogra district?
A) 8
B) 10
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 12

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous "Kherua Mosque" in Sherpur Upazila of Bogra was built during the Mughal period.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which former President of Bangladesh was born in Bogra?
A) Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
B) Hussain Muhammad Ershad
C) Ziaur Rahman
D) Abdur Rahman Biswas
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ziaur Rahman

Q7. [MCQ] The Rural Development Academy (RDA) in Bogra was established in 1974 as a specialized institution for:
A) Agricultural research
B) Rural development training and research
C) Microfinance management
D) Public health education
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rural development training and research

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The archaeological museum at Mahasthangarh primarily displays artifacts recovered from the Pala and Sena dynasty periods.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which famous brand of sweet curd from Bogra is known for its unique preparation in clay pots?
A) Matri Bhandar
B) Porabari
C) Asia Sweets
D) Shampa Doi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Shampa Doi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bogra Cantonment is one of the most important and largest military bases in North Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] A limestone slab bearing a Brahmi inscription, the earliest epigraphic evidence of writing in Bangladesh, was discovered at which site in Bogra?
A) Vasu Vihara
B) Gokul Medh
C) Mahasthangarh
D) Kherua Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mahasthangarh

B) Mymensingh
C) Bogra
D) Gaibandha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bogra

=== JESSORE ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Jessore district is part of which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Benapole, the largest land port in Bangladesh, is located in the Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Jessore is widely recognized as the first district of British Bengal, established in which year?
A) 1686
B) 1786
C) 1886
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1786

Q4. [MCQ] The region of Jessore, particularly Gadkhali, is famously known as the "Flower Capital" of Bangladesh for its extensive cultivation of:
A) Roses and Tuberoses
B) Orchids and Lilies
C) Sunflowers and Marigolds
D) Tulips and Daffodils
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Roses and Tuberoses

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Air Force Academy, a premier training institute for air force cadets, is located in Jessore.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The great epic poet Michael Madhusudan Dutt, a central figure in Bengali literature, was born in which village of Jessore?
A) Keshobpur
B) Sagardari
C) Monirampur
D) Jhikargacha
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sagardari

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the airport that serves the city of Jessore?
A) Shah Makhdum Airport
B) Osmani International Airport
C) Jessore Airport
D) Saidpur Airport
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jessore Airport

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jessore is a coastal district directly bordering the Bay of Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional Nakshi Kantha, a type of embroidered quilt, is a well-known handicraft from which region?
A) Sylhet
B) Rangpur
C) Jessore
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jessore

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] After the independence of Bangladesh in 1971, Dhaka was immediately declared the capital, and Jessore never served in that capacity.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic name of Jessore was "Jashohar," which in Bengali means:
A) River of Glory
B) City of Victory
C) Stripper of Glory
D) Land of Flowers
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Stripper of Glory

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British period, Jessore was a major center of the Indigo Revolt, a peasant movement against exploitative indigo planters.

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Jessore district?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q4. [MCQ] The military base in Jessore is known by what name?

B) Savar Cantonment

D) Mainamati Cantonment
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jessore Cantonment

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Bir Shrestha Lance Naik Nur Mohammad Sheikh, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, is buried in Jessore.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Bhairab River flows through the heart of Jessore city.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] What famous variety of date molasses, known as "Nolen Gur," is a winter specialty of the Jessore region?
A) Patali Gur
B) Jhola Gur
C) Akhi Gur
D) Dana Gur
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Patali Gur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The first public library in Bengal, the Jessore Public Library, was established in 1854.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) Bagherpara
B) Abhaynagar

D) Chaugachha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Keshobpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Munshi Meherullah, a prominent Islamic scholar and social reformer, was a native of the Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

D) Mr. Tilman Henckell

Q4. [MCQ] During the reign of which 16th-century ruler of Bengal did the name "Jashohar" first gain prominence?
