C) Maharaja Pratapaditya
D) Isa Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Maharaja Pratapaditya

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate in Jessore District is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The headquarters of the Bangladesh Army's 55th Infantry Division is located in which cantonment?
A) Dhaka Cantonment
B) Savar Cantonment
C) Mymensingh Cantonment
D) Jessore Cantonment
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jessore Cantonment

Q7. [MCQ] The Jessore comb, an intricately carved hair accessory made from buffalo horn, was a famous local craft that received a certificate at which international exposition?
A) The Great Exhibition of 1851 in London
B) The 1900 Exposition Universelle in Paris
C) The 1904 Louisiana Purchase Exposition in St. Louis
D) The 1939 New York World's Fair
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Great Exhibition of 1851 in London

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Jessore-Jhenidah Railway, one of the first railway lines in the region, was established in 1913 primarily to transport indigo.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Madhur Mela', a week-long fair celebrating the birth anniversary of Michael Madhusudan Dutt, is held annually on the bank of which river?
A) Bhairab
B) Kopotakkho
C) Betna
D) Ichamati
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kopotakkho

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] On December 6, 1971, Jessore became the first district of Bangladesh to be liberated from Pakistani forces.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== DINAJPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Dinajpur district is located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Rangpur Division
C) Mymensingh Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Dinajpur is famous for producing a fine, aromatic variety of rice called "Kataribhog."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The historic Kantajew Temple, renowned for its exquisite terracotta ornamentation, is located in which district?
A) Bogra
B) Naogaon
C) Dinajpur
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dinajpur

Q4. [MCQ] Besides rice, Dinajpur is the leading producer of which popular fruit in Bangladesh?
A) Mango
B) Jackfruit
C) Pineapple
D) Litchi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Litchi

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Ramsagar, the largest man-made pond (dighi) in Bangladesh, is situated in Dinajpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main river that flows through Dinajpur town?
A) Teesta
B) Karatoya
C) Punarbhaba
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Punarbhaba

Q7. [MCQ] The Hili Land Port, an important trade point with India, is located in which district?
A) Jessore
B) Lalmonirhat
C) Panchagarh
D) Dinajpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Dinajpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dinajpur region is completely flat and has no mineral resources.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The historic Dinajpur Rajbari (Royal Palace) is a major landmark in the city.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Dinajpur is located in the southern part of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Barapukuria Coal Mine, the only active coal mine in Bangladesh, is located in which upazila of Dinajpur?
A) Parbatipur
B) Phulbari
C) Birampur
D) Ghoraghat
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Parbatipur

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kantajew Temple is dedicated to the Hindu deity Shiva.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] The construction of the Kantajew Temple was initiated in the early 18th century by which Maharaja of Dinajpur?
A) Maharaja Ramnath
B) Maharaja Pran Nath
C) Maharaja Girijanath Roy
D) Maharaja Jagadish Nath
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Maharaja Pran Nath

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Dinajpur district?
A) 9
B) 11
C) 13
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 13

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Historically, the region of Dinajpur was part of the ancient Pundravardhana kingdom.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Ramsagar was excavated in the mid-18th century by which Maharaja to provide drinking water to the local people?
A) Maharaja Pran Nath
B) Maharaja Ram Nath
C) Maharaja Baidyanath
D) Maharaja Shyamal Roy
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Maharaja Ram Nath

Q7. [MCQ] The Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science and Technology University (HSTU) is a major public university located in:
A) Rangpur
B) Dinajpur
C) Bogra
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dinajpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The original nine spires (Navaratna) of the Kantajew Temple were destroyed by a fire in the 19th century.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of these is another significant river flowing through Dinajpur district?
A) Jamuna
B) Padma
C) Meghna
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Atrai

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate in Dinajpur is significantly higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The terracotta plaques on the walls of the Kantajew Temple primarily depict scenes from which epic Hindu texts?
A) The Vedas and Upanishads
B) The Ramayana and the Mahabharata
C) The Puranas and the Tantras
D) The Gita Govinda and the Chaitanya Charitamrita
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Ramayana and the Mahabharata

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sitakot Vihara, the ruins of a 5th-century Buddhist monastery, is located in Nawabganj upazila of Dinajpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Dinajpur District in square kilometers?
A) 2,850 sq km
B) 3,120 sq km
C) 3,444 sq km
D) 3,980 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3,444 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] During the British period, the Dinajpur district was part of which larger commissionership or division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Presidency Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi Division

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Barapukuria Coal Mine uses the open-pit mining method to extract coal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The historical region of Ghoraghat in southern Dinajpur served as a frontier fort and administrative center during the reign of which empire?
A) The Sena Empire
B) The Delhi Sultanate
C) The Mughal Empire
D) The British Empire
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Mughal Empire

Q7. [MCQ] The construction of the Kantajew Temple, started by Maharaja Pran Nath, was completed by his adopted son, Maharaja:
A) Baidyanath
B) Jagat Joaddar
C) Ramnath
D) Shyamal Roy
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ramnath

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the Santal and Oraon ethnic groups constitute the largest indigenous populations in Dinajpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The famous "Chehelgazi Mazar" in Dinajpur is believed to be the tomb of forty Arab warriors who accompanied which famous general?
A) Bakhtiyar Khilji
B) Mir Jumla
C) Islam Khan
D) None of the above
CORRECT ANSWER: D) None of the above

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Parbatipur railway junction in Dinajpur is one of the largest in Bangladesh and was a major center for steam locomotive maintenance.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== PABNA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Pabna is a district in which administrative division of Bangladesh?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant, the first of its kind in Bangladesh, is being constructed in the Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Suchitra Sen, a legendary actress of Bengali and Hindi cinema, was born in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Pabna
C) Kolkata
D) Kushtia
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pabna

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous institution in Pabna, the largest of its kind in Bangladesh?
A) Pabna Medical College
B) Pabna Mental Hospital
C) Pabna Textile Engineering College
D) Pabna Cadet College
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pabna Mental Hospital

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Hardinge Bridge, a famous railway bridge over the Padma River, is located in Pabna.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which major river forms the southern boundary of the Pabna district?
A) Jamuna
B) Meghna
C) Padma
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma

Q7. [MCQ] The Lalon Shah Bridge connects Pabna with which neighboring district?
A) Kushtia
B) Sirajganj
C) Rajbari
D) Manikganj
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Kushtia

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Pabna is well-known for its large-scale tea cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major industry in Pabna?
A) Shipbuilding
B) Hosiery and Textiles
C) Leather processing
D) Coal mining
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hosiery and Textiles

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Pabna University of Science and Technology is a prominent public university in the region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic Pabna Peasant Uprising of 1873 was a resistance movement against whom?
A) The British government
B) Oppressive zamindars (landlords)
C) Indigo planters
D) Religious leaders
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Oppressive zamindars (landlords)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Hardinge Bridge was named after Lord Curzon, the Viceroy of India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] The administrative headquarters of the Bangladesh Sugarcane Research Institute (BSRI) is located in which upazila of Pabna?
A) Pabna Sadar
B) Ishwardi
C) Chatmohar
D) Santhia
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ishwardi

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Pabna district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The ancestral home (kuthibari) of the Nobel laureate poet Rabindranath Tagore is located in Shilaidaha, which is now in the Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Ghosh Dairy' of Pabna is particularly famous for producing high-quality:
A) Roshmalai
B) Ghee and Curd
C) Sandesh
D) Chomchom
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ghee and Curd

Q7. [MCQ] The Lalon Shah Bridge is built over which river?
A) Jamuna
B) Ichamati
C) Atrai
D) Padma
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Padma

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] General Jagjit Singh Aurora, who accepted the surrender of the Pakistani forces in 1971, had family roots in the Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic Jor Bangla Temple, a fine example of terracotta art, is located in which upazila of Pabna?
A) Bera
B) Atgharia
C) Pabna Sadar
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pabna Sadar

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Pabna was separated from the Rajshahi district and became an independent district in 1832.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Hardinge Bridge was designed by the British engineer Sir Robert Richard Gales and was completed in which year?
A) 1905
B) 1915
C) 1925
D) 1935
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1915

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant is being built with technical and financial assistance primarily from the United States.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Pabna District in square kilometers?
A) 1,950 sq km
B) 2,376 sq km
C) 2,890 sq km
D) 3,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,376 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Pabna Peasant Uprising led to the enactment of which significant legislation by the British government to protect tenant rights?
A) The Permanent Settlement Act of 1793
B) The Bengal Tenancy Act of 1885
C) The Land Acquisition Act of 1894
D) The Rowlatt Act of 1919
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Bengal Tenancy Act of 1885

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Pabna is believed to be derived from "Pundra," the ancient kingdom whose capital was Mahasthangarh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Pabna Mental Hospital, originally known as the Pabna Lunatic Asylum, was established in which year?
A) 1898
B) 1918
C) 1938
D) 1957
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 1957

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following notable Bengali writers, known for his novel 'Padma Nadir Majhi', has strong literary connections to the Pabna region?
A) Bankim Chandra Chatterjee
B) Manik Bandopadhyay
C) Bibhutibhushan Bandopadhyay
D) Sarat Chandra Chattopadhyay
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Manik Bandopadhyay

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Chalan Beel, the largest wetland in Bangladesh, covers a significant area within the Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Rooppur Nuclear Power Plant will use which type of nuclear reactor technology?
A) PWR (Pressurized Water Reactor)
B) BWR (Boiling Water Reactor)
C) VVER-1200 (Water-Water Energetic Reactor)
D) CANDU (Canada Deuterium Uranium)
CORRECT ANSWER: C) VVER-1200 (Water-Water Energetic Reactor)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the population growth rate of Pabna is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

=== TANGAIL ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Tangail district is located in which administrative division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Mymensingh Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Tangail is world-famous for a special type of handwoven sari known as the Tangail Saree.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Bangabandhu Bridge, one of the longest bridges in Bangladesh, is built over which major river?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Teesta
D) Jamuna
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jamuna

Q4. [MCQ] The traditional sweet dish "Chomchom" from Porabari is a famous specialty of which district?
A) Comilla
B) Tangail
C) Bogra
D) Mymensingh
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Tangail

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Madhupur National Park, known for its Sal forests, is located in Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Maulana Abdul Hamid Khan Bhashani, a renowned political leader, is buried in which district?
A) Sirajganj
B) Bogra
C) Tangail
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tangail

Q7. [MCQ] Which of these is a historic mosque located in Tangail, known for its unique architecture?
A) Sixty Dome Mosque
B) Star Mosque
C) Atia Mosque
D) Choto Sona Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Atia Mosque

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Tangail is a coastal district with a seaport.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The main administrative town of Tangail district is also named Tangail.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Jamuna Bridge connects the eastern part of Bangladesh with the northern (Rajshahi and Rangpur) divisions.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Maulana Bhashani Science and Technology University is a public university located in which district?
A) Pabna
B) Tangail
C) Gazipur
D) Sirajganj
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Tangail

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangabandhu Bridge is exclusively a road bridge and does not have a railway line.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] The Madhupur Tract, where the Madhupur National Park is located, is a distinct geological feature known as a:
A) Floodplain
B) Delta
C) Pleistocene Terrace
D) Coastal plain
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pleistocene Terrace

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Tangail district?
A) 8
B) 10
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 12

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Atia Mosque, a protected archaeological site, was built during the Sultanate period.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Tangail Saree was granted Geographical Indication (GI) status by Bangladesh, recognizing its unique origin and quality.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] Bir Shrestha Hamidur Rahman, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, was born in which upazila of Tangail?
A) Ghatail
B) Kalihati
C) Madhupur
D) His ancestral home is in present-day Jhenaidah, not Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: D) His ancestral home is in present-day Jhenaidah, not Tangail.

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous freedom fighter Kader Siddique, known as "Tiger," led the liberation forces in the Tangail region during the 1971 war.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Dhaleshwari River, a distributary of the Jamuna, flows through which district?
A) Mymensingh
B) Comilla
C) Tangail
D) Jessore
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tangail

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Pineapple is a major agricultural product of the Madhupur region in Tangail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic Atia Mosque was built in 1609 by which Mughal zamindar of the region?
A) Isa Khan
B) Sayeed Khan Panni
C) Karrani Khan
D) Mir Jumla II
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sayeed Khan Panni

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The image of the Atia Mosque is depicted on the Bangladeshi 10 Taka banknote.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the total length of the Bangabandhu Bridge (Jamuna Multi-purpose Bridge)?
A) 3.6 km
B) 4.8 km
C) 6.2 km
D) 9.8 km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 4.8 km

Q4. [MCQ] The name 'Tangail' is believed to have originated from the term 'Tanga-il', where 'Tanga' referred to a type of horse-drawn carriage and 'il' meant:
A) A high dam or embankment
B) A marketplace
C) A river crossing
D) A forested area
CORRECT ANSWER: A) A high dam or embankment

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate in Tangail District is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Tangail District in square kilometers?
A) 2,540 sq km
B) 2,980 sq km
C) 3,414 sq km
D) 3,820 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3,414 sq km

Q7. [MCQ] Maulana Bhashani's famous "Kagmari Conference" of 1957, a major political gathering, was held in which upazila of Tangail?
A) Nagarpur
B) Bhuapur
C) Tangail Sadar
D) Delduar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tangail Sadar

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Madhupur Tract is geologically older than the surrounding alluvial floodplains of the Jamuna and Brahmaputra rivers.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional spinning wheel used in the preliminary stage of making Tangail Saree thread is locally known as:
A) Charka
B) Dhol
C) Noli
D) Piri
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Charka

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of the Tangail district was shifted from Atia to the present location in 1869 due to river erosion.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== JAMALPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Jamalpur is a district in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Mymensingh Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Mymensingh Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Old Brahmaputra River flows through Jamalpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Jamalpur is particularly famous for which traditional form of embroidered quilt?
A) Jamdani
B) Shataranji
C) Nakshi Kantha
D) Khadi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nakshi Kantha

Q4. [MCQ] The Jamuna Fertilizer Company Ltd. (JFCL), one of the largest fertilizer factories in Bangladesh, is located in which district?
A) Sirajganj
B) Jamalpur
C) Tangail
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamalpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of Jamalpur district is in a town called Sherpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major crop grown in Jamalpur?
A) Tea
B) Sugarcane
C) Jute
D) Cotton
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jute

Q7. [MCQ] The Dayamoyee Temple is a prominent Hindu temple and historical landmark located in which city?
A) Mymensingh
B) Netrokona
C) Jamalpur
D) Sherpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jamalpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jamalpur shares a border with the country of Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The Bahadurbad Ghat is a major river terminal in Jamalpur located on the bank of which river?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Teesta
D) Jamuna
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jamuna

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Jamalpur is a completely plain region with no hills or elevated land.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Jamalpur district was carved out of which larger district in 1978?
A) Dhaka
B) Tangail
C) Pabna
D) Mymensingh
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mymensingh

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Nakshi Kantha of Jamalpur has received Geographical Indication (GI) status from Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which sector commander of the Liberation War, who was later killed in a coup in 1975, was a native of Jamalpur?
A) Major General Ziaur Rahman
B) Major General K M Shafiullah
C) Major General Khaled Mosharraf
D) Colonel Abu Taher
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Major General Khaled Mosharraf

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Jamalpur district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Garo ethnic community has a significant presence in the northern parts of Jamalpur bordering the Garo Hills.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Jamuna Fertilizer Company Ltd. (JFCL) in Tarakandi primarily produces what type of fertilizer?
A) Potash
B) Phosphate
C) Urea
D) Ammonium Sulphate
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Urea

Q7. [MCQ] The name Jamalpur is believed to be in honor of which 15th-century saint?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Shah Makhdum
C) Shah Jamal
D) Khan Jahan Ali
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Jamal

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British Raj, Jamalpur was connected by a major railway line primarily for the transport of jute to Calcutta.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The area around Bakshiganj in Jamalpur is known for the cultivation of a unique local aromatic rice variety called:
A) Kataribhog
B) Chinigura
C) Tulshimala
D) Kalijira
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tulshimala

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district of Jamalpur was liberated from Pakistani forces on December 10, 1971, just before the final victory.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Lafarge Surma Cement plant, located across the Indian border, has a conveyor belt that transports limestone and shale over the hills to which upazila of Jamalpur?
A) Islampur
B) Dewanganj
C) Bakshiganj
D) This conveyor belt is in Sunamganj, not Jamalpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: D) This conveyor belt is in Sunamganj, not Jamalpur.

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Jamalpur district is higher than the average literacy rate of the Mymensingh division, according to the 2022 census.

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Jamalpur District in square kilometers?
A) 1,650 sq km
B) 2,115 sq km
C) 2,530 sq km
D) 2,980 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,115 sq km

A) Melandaha
B) Sarishabari
C) Bakshiganj
D) Jamalpur Sadar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bakshiganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic Dayamoyee Temple was established by the zamindar family of Gouripur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Noted playwright and actor Abdullah al Mamun, a key figure in the "Nattayatra" movement, was born in which district?
A) Tangail
B) Jamalpur
C) Sirajganj
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamalpur

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major tributary that joins the Jamuna river within the borders of Jamalpur district?
A) Teesta
B) Dharla
C) Dudhkumar
D) Jhinai
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jhinai

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Jamalpur district does not have an official Export Processing Zone (EPZ).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional folk theatre form known as "Ghatu Gaan," involving young boys in female attire, was once prevalent in which greater region?
A) Chittagong Hill Tracts
B) Sylhet Basin
C) Mymensingh-Jamalpur region
D) Barind Tract
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mymensingh-Jamalpur region

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Jamalpur is primarily composed of non-calcareous dark grey floodplain soil, which is ideal for jute cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== KUSHTIA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Kushtia is a district within which administrative division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Khulna Division

D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Kushtia is famously known as the cultural capital of Bangladesh.

Q3. [MCQ] The shrine and akhra (commune) of which great mystic saint and baul singer is located in Kushtia?
A) Hason Raja
B) Shah Abdul Karim
C) Lalon Shah
D) Radharaman Dutta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lalon Shah

Q4. [MCQ] The Shilaidaha Kuthibari, a country house where Nobel laureate Rabindranath Tagore spent many years, is located in which district?
A) Pabna
B) Kushtia
C) Jessore
D) Jhenaidah
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kushtia

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Hardinge Bridge, a famous steel railway bridge, connects Kushtia with the district of Pabna over the Padma river.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which major river flows through Kushtia district?
A) Jamuna
B) Meghna
C) Padma
D) Karnaphuli
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous confectionery from Kushtia made from sesame seeds and jaggery?
A) Monda
B) Roshmalai
C) Tiler Khaja
D) Chomchom
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tiler Khaja

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Islamic University, one of the major public universities in Bangladesh, is located in Kushtia.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Lalon Shah Bridge is a road bridge built parallel to which other famous bridge?
A) Jamuna Bridge
B) Meghna Bridge
C) Rupsha Bridge
D) Hardinge Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Hardinge Bridge

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Kushtia is a major producer of tea in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] Mir Mosharraf Hossain, one of the first modern Muslim Bengali writers, is best known for his novel "Bishad Sindhu." He was born in which district?
A) Faridpur
B) Jessore
C) Kushtia
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kushtia

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The main campus of the Islamic University is located entirely within the Kushtia district.

A) Faraizi Movement
B) Indigo Revolt

CORRECT ANSWER: B) Indigo Revolt

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Kushtia district?
A) 5
B) 6
C) 7
D) 8
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

Q6. [MCQ] The "Lalon Mela" is an annual festival held at the shrine of Lalon Shah to celebrate his birth and death anniversaries.
A) True
B) False

Q7. [MCQ] Kushtia town is situated on the south bank of which river?
A) Gorai River
B) Kumar River
C) Bhairab River
D) Nabaganga River
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Gorai River

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Hardinge Bridge was named after Lord Hardinge, who was the Viceroy of India when its construction began.

Q9. [MCQ] The main industrial product of the Jagati region in Kushtia is:
A) Jute goods
B) Sugar
C) Paper
D) Ready-made garments
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sugar

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Kushtia was the first district in independent Bangladesh to have a fully functional broadcasting radio station (Bangladesh Betar).

D) 1913

B) 1979
C) 1985
D) 1990

B) Kumarkhali

D) Daulatpur

=== FARIDPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Faridpur is a district in which administrative division of Bangladesh?
A) Khulna Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The mighty Padma River flows along the northern boundary of Faridpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The renowned   (Palli Kobi) or "Pastoral Poet" Jasimuddin, was born in which district?
A) Kushtia
B) Faridpur
C) Bogra
D) Mymensingh
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Faridpur

Q4. [MCQ] Faridpur is well-known for producing which major agricultural crop?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Cotton
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The ancestral home of the Nobel laureate Rabindranath Tagore is located in Faridpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous folk art form associated with the Faridpur region?
A) Shataranji weaving
B) Nakshi Kantha embroidery
C) Terracotta pottery
D) Jamdani weaving
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nakshi Kantha embroidery

Q7. [MCQ] The district of Faridpur was named after which famous Sufi saint?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Khan Jahan Ali
C) Shah Fariduddin Masud
D) Bayazid Bostami
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Fariduddin Masud

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Faridpur is a landlocked district with no direct border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The popular winter delicacy "Khejur Gur" (date palm jaggery) is a famous product of which district?
A) Sylhet
B) Rangpur
C) Faridpur
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Faridpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The city of Faridpur has a major international airport.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Faraizi Movement, an influential Islamic reformist movement in 19th-century Bengal, was initiated by whom?
A) Titumir
B) Mir Mosharraf Hossain
C) Haji Shariatullah
D) Dudu Miyan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Haji Shariatullah

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous epic poem "Nakshi Kanthar Math" (Field of the Embroidered Quilt) was written by Jasimuddin, depicting life in rural Faridpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Faridpur district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q4. [MCQ] The great filmmaker Mrinal Sen, a prominent figure in Indian cinema, was born in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Barisal
C) Faridpur
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Faridpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The tomb of the great saint Shah Ali Baghdadi is a major pilgrimage site in Faridpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What was the historical name of the greater Faridpur region during the Sultanate and Mughal periods?
A) Varendra
B) Samatata
C) Fatehabad
D) Gauda
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Fatehabad

Q7. [MCQ] Dudu Miyan, who led the Faraizi Movement after his father's death, was born in which upazila of the greater Faridpur region?
A) Faridpur Sadar
B) Bhanga
C) Madaripur (then part of Faridpur)
D) Goalundo
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Madaripur (then part of Faridpur)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Faridpur district was one of the first districts in Bangladesh to have a railway connection established during the British era.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The "Gerakol," a unique local form of wrestling, is a traditional sport of which region?
A) Chittagong Hill Tracts
B) Faridpur
C) Sylhet
D) Dinajpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Faridpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate in Faridpur is significantly lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] The historic Mathurapur Deul (temple), a tall terracotta monument, is believed to have been built to commemorate the victory of which Mughal general?
A) Man Singh I
B) Islam Khan Chishti
C) Mir Jumla II
D) It was built before the Mughals.
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Islam Khan Chishti

CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Padma
B) Madhumati
C) Kumar

D) 2,980 sq km

A) Paturia Ghat
B) Mawa Ghat
C) Goalundo Ghat
D) Aricha Ghat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Goalundo Ghat

A) The Tariqah-i-Muhammadiya movement
B) The Faraizi Movement
C) The Ahmadiyya Movement
D) The Wahhabi Movement
CORRECT ANSWER: A) The Tariqah-i-Muhammadiya movement

B) 1869

D) 1909

A) Nabinagar
B) Sarail
C) Shibpur

B) Roshmalai
C) Chomchom
D) Chhanamukhi

A) Comilla
B) Brahmanbaria

Q1. [MCQ] Adwaita Mallabarman, the author of the classic novel "Titas Ekti Nadir Naam" (A River Called Titas), was born in which district?

D) Habiganj

=== NARSINGDI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Narsingdi is a district located in which administrative division?

CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Narsingdi is famously known as the "Manchester of Bangladesh" due to its large textile and garments industry.

A) Comilla
B) Gazipur
C) Narsingdi

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Narsingdi

A) Mango
B) Litchi
C) Banana
D) Pineapple
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Banana

A) Brahmanbaria
B) Narayanganj
C) Narsingdi
D) Gazipur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Narsingdi

A) Jamdani Saree

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lungi and Gamcha

B) Dhaka
C) Narsingdi
D) Faridpur

MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The ruins at Wari-Bateshwar suggest the existence of a fortified urban center and trading post dating back to:
A) The Pala period (8th century AD)
B) The Mughal period (16th century AD)
C) The Iron Age (around 450 BC)
D) The British period (19th century AD)
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Iron Age (around 450 BC)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Narsingdi was established as a separate district in 1984, having previously been a part of the greater Dhaka district.

B) 6

CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The discovery of punch-marked coins at Wari-Bateshwar indicates that the city had trade relations with which ancient civilizations?
A) Roman and Egyptian
B) Southeast Asian and Chinese
C) Mesopotamian and Persian
D) Mauryan and ancient Greek
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Southeast Asian and Chinese

C) Satish Pakrashi
D) Titumir
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Satish Pakrashi

CORRECT ANSWER: True

CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Meghna-Dhonagoda Irrigation Project (MDIP), which provides irrigation to a large area of Narsingdi and Chandpur, is a type of:
A) Barrage project
B) Embankment and drainage project

CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== SIRAJGANJ ===
**EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Sirajganj is a district in which administrative division of Bangladesh?
A) Rangpur Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangabandhu Bridge, connecting the eastern and western parts of Bangladesh, has its western end in Sirajganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Sirajganj is located on the bank of which major river?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Teesta
D) Jamuna
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jamuna

Q4. [MCQ] The district is particularly famous for which hand-loomed product?
A) Jamdani Saree
B) Shataranji Carpet
C) Lungi and Gamcha
D) Silk Fabric
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lungi and Gamcha

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Shahzadpur sub-district of Sirajganj is known for its high-quality milk and dairy products.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The ancestral home (Kuthibari) of which Nobel laureate poet is a major tourist attraction in Shahzadpur?
A) Kazi Nazrul Islam
B) Michael Madhusudan Dutt
C) Rabindranath Tagore
D) Jasimuddin
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rabindranath Tagore

Q7. [MCQ] The Bangabandhu Bridge is also known by what other name?
A) Lalon Shah Bridge
B) Hardinge Bridge
C) Jamuna Bridge
D) Bhairab Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jamuna Bridge

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Sirajganj is a major tea-producing district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Huseyn Shaheed Suhrawardy, a former Prime Minister of Bengal and Pakistan, was born in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Sirajganj
C) Faridpur
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sirajganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The vast wetland area known as Chalan Beel covers parts of Sirajganj district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
**MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The district was named after a local zamindar named:
A) Siraj ud-Daulah
B) Siraj Ali Chowdhury
C) Siraj Islam
D) Siraj Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Siraj Ali Chowdhury

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The headquarters of the state-owned dairy company "Milk Vita" is located in Shahzadpur, Sirajganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Maulana Abdul Hamid Khan Bhashani, a prominent political leader, spent a significant part of his life and started his political career in which district?
A) Tangail
B) Pabna
C) Sirajganj
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sirajganj

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Sirajganj district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangabandhu Bridge was opened to traffic in 1998.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The historic Hatikumrul Navaratna Temple, a fine example of terracotta art, is located in which upazila of Sirajganj?
A) Shahzadpur
B) Ullapara
C) Raiganj
D) Kazipur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ullapara

Q7. [MCQ] Besides the Jamuna, which other river flows through Sirajganj?
A) Teesta
B) Karatoya
C) Punarbhaba
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Karatoya

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Sirajganj was upgraded from a subdivision to a district in 1984.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The construction of an economic zone is underway near the western end of the Bangabandhu Bridge in which upazila?
A) Sirajganj Sadar
B) Belkuchi
C) Chauhali
D) Kazipur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Belkuchi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Sirajganj district is higher than the national average, as per the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
**HARD LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The Hatikumrul Navaratna Temple was built by a Nayeb Dewan named Ramnath Bhaduri during the reign of which Mughal emperor?
A) Akbar
B) Jahangir
C) Shah Jahan
D) Aurangzeb
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Aurangzeb

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sirajganj Economic Zone is being developed as a public-private partnership project led by the Bangladesh Economic Zones Authority (BEZA).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Sirajganj District in square kilometers?
A) 1,980 sq km
B) 2,498 sq km
C) 2,850 sq km
D) 3,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,498 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The famous writer and filmmaker Zahir Raihan's ancestral home is in which upazila of Sirajganj?
A) Shahzadpur
B) Raiganj
C) Tarash
D) His ancestral home is in Feni, not Sirajganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: D) His ancestral home is in Feni, not Sirajganj.

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British Raj, Sirajganj was a major river port and center for the jute trade, administered under the Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Bangabandhu Railway Bridge, being built parallel to the existing Jamuna Bridge, is funded primarily by a loan from which country?
A) China
B) India
C) Japan
D) Russia
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Japan

Q7. [MCQ] The folk songs of Sirajganj are often thematically linked to the river life of the Jamuna and are locally known as:
A) Bhawaiya
B) Bhatiali
C) Jari Gaan
D) Gombhira
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bhatiali

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Sirajganj is predominantly composed of active and young Jamuna floodplain deposits, which are subject to frequent changes due to river erosion and accretion.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] M. A. Matin, a former Deputy Prime Minister of Bangladesh, was a prominent political figure from which district?
A) Bogra
B) Pabna
C) Sirajganj
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sirajganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the female literacy rate in Sirajganj is higher than the male literacy rate.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== NOAKHALI ===
**EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Noakhali is a coastal district in which division?
A) Barisal Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters of Noakhali is a town called Maijdee.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which major river's estuary shapes the coastline of Noakhali?
A) Padma
B) Jamuna
C) Karnaphuli
D) Meghna
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Meghna

Q4. [MCQ] The famous island of Hatiya is an upazila of which district?
A) Bhola
B) Patuakhali
C) Noakhali
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Noakhali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The local dialect spoken in Noakhali is known for its distinct accent and is widely recognized across Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product of Noakhali?
A) Tea
B) Rice
C) Jute
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rice

Q7. [MCQ] The newly developed island used to shelter Rohingya refugees is known as:
A) Nijhum Dwip
B) Sandwip
C) Bhasan Char
D) Saint Martin's Island
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bhasan Char

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Noakhali shares a land border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional buffalo yogurt (Mohisher Doi) is a famous dairy product from which region?
A) Bogra
B) Sirajganj
C) Noakhali
D) Tangail
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Noakhali

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The original town of Noakhali was completely lost to river erosion.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
**MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] The historical name of the Noakhali region was:
A) Samatata
B) Harikela
C) Bhulua
D) Tippera
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bhulua

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The name "Noakhali" originated from the excavation of a new "khal" (canal) to save the area from flooding.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The famous island park, Nijhum Dwip, known for its herd of spotted deer, is administratively under which upazila?
A) Companiganj
B) Hatiya
C) Subarnachar
D) Kabirhat
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hatiya

Q4. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Noakhali district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Mahatma Gandhi visited Noakhali in 1946 to promote peace following communal riots.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Obaidul Quader, a prominent politician and the current General Secretary of the Awami League, hails from which upazila of Noakhali?
A) Noakhali Sadar
B) Begumganj
C) Senbagh
D) Companiganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Companiganj

Q7. [MCQ] The main economic activities in Noakhali are agriculture and:
A) Garment manufacturing
B) Ship breaking
C) Tourism
D) Foreign remittances
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Foreign remittances

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bajra Shahi Mosque, a well-preserved Mughal-era mosque, is located in Noakhali.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The first female Speaker of the Bangladesh National Parliament, Shirin Sharmin Chaudhury, has ancestral roots in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Noakhali
C) Faridpur
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Noakhali

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Noakhali district is one of the lowest in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] The Bajra Shahi Mosque was built in the 18th century during the reign of which Mughal emperor?
A) Aurangzeb
B) Shah Jahan
C) Muhammad Shah
D) Bahadur Shah Zafar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Muhammad Shah

A) 1921
B) 1935
C) 1951
D) 1965

D) 5,110 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 4,202 sq km

CORRECT ANSWER: True

D) BNS Surma
CORRECT ANSWER: B) BNS Palash

CORRECT ANSWER: A) Begumganj

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bhasan Char island is geologically older and more stable than the neighboring Sandwip island.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Comilla
B) Noakhali
C) Chandpur
D) Feni
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Noakhali

=== FENI ===
**EASY LEVEL (10 Questions) ---

Q1. [MCQ] Feni is a small district in the southeastern part of Bangladesh, belonging to which division?
A) Sylhet Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dhaka-Chittagong Highway, a major national artery, passes directly through Feni town.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Feni shares an international border with which state of India?
A) West Bengal
B) Meghalaya
C) Assam
D) Tripura
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Tripura

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows through Feni district?
A) Titas
B) Gumti
C) Feni
D) Karnaphuli
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Feni

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Khaleda Zia, a former Prime Minister of Bangladesh, was born in Feni.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The famous historic water tank (dighi) named Bijoy Singh Dighi is located in which district?
A) Comilla
B) Noakhali
C) Feni
D) Chandpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Feni

Q7. [MCQ] The Muhuri Irrigation Project is a large-scale project for flood control and irrigation in which district?
A) Brahmanbaria
B) Feni
C) Lakshmipur
D) Cox's Bazar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Feni

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Feni is a major tea-growing region of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district headquarters of Feni is also named Feni.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Feni has a direct railway connection linking Dhaka and Chittagong.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] Feni was established as a separate district in which year?
A) 1971
B) 1978
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q3. [MCQ] The renowned journalist and writer Abdus Salam was a native of which district?
A) Comilla
B) Feni
C) Noakhali
D) Chandpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Feni

A) 4
B) 6
C) 8
D) 10
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

A) Modernist
B) Pala Buddhist
C) Mughal
D) European Colonial
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mughal

Q7. [MCQ] The Feni Girls' Cadet College is one of the few cadet colleges in Bangladesh exclusively for female students.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) Pabna
B) Faridpur
C) Feni
D) Dhaka
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Feni

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate in Feni is one of the highest in the country, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] The name 'Feni' is believed to be derived from the word 'Faniya', which in the local dialect means:
A) A type of boat
B) A ferry crossing
C) A muddy canal
D) A marketplace

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Muhuri Irrigation Project, involving a dam and regulator on the Feni River, was constructed with financial and technical assistance from the World Bank.

B) 975 sq km
C) 1,120 sq km
D) 1,350 sq km

A) A Sena dynasty king
B) A Pala dynasty king
C) A Tripura king

CORRECT ANSWER: C) A Tripura king

CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) Feni Sadar

D) Ramgarh (in Khagrachari district)

A) Gauda
B) Vanga
C) Samatata
D) Pundra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Samatata

A) November 15
B) December 6
C) December 10
D) December 14
CORRECT ANSWER: B) December 6

=== LAKSHMIPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Lakshmipur is a coastal district in which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Chittagong Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The mighty Meghna River flows along the western boundary of Lakshmipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Lakshmipur is widely known in Bangladesh for its abundant production of which fruit?
A) Mango
B) Litchi
C) Coconut
D) Jackfruit
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Coconut

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural crop in Lakshmipur?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Sugarcane
D) Rice
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rice

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters of Lakshmipur is also a town named Lakshmipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Historically, Lakshmipur was a part of which greater district?
A) Comilla
B) Feni
C) Noakhali
D) Chandpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Noakhali

Q7. [MCQ] What is a common nickname for Lakshmipur due to its agricultural output?
A) The Granary of Bengal
B) The Land of Coconuts
C) The City of Hilsa
D) The Tea Capital
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Land of Coconuts

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Lakshmipur has a major international seaport.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major upazila and river port in Lakshmipur?
A) Hatiya
B) Ramgati
C) Char Fasson
D) Daulatkhan
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ramgati

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Lakshmipur is generally fertile as it is part of a large delta.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Lakshmipur established as a separate district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Tota Mosque in Raipur upazila is a well-known historical landmark in Lakshmipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Lakshmipur district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] The "Lakshmi Narayan Mandir", after which the district is believed to be named, was built by which historical group?
A) The Mughals
B) The Pala Dynasty
C) The family of a zamindar named Dalal Raja
D) The British East India Company
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The family of a zamindar named Dalal Raja

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The economy of Lakshmipur is heavily dependent on industrial manufacturing.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Khoa Sagor Dighi, a large historic water tank, is located in which upazila of Lakshmipur?
A) Lakshmipur Sadar
B) Ramganj
C) Raipur
D) Ramgati
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Raipur

Q7. [MCQ] Mohammad Mohammadullah, a former President of Bangladesh, hailed from which district?
A) Feni
B) Noakhali
C) Lakshmipur
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lakshmipur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, the Battle of Ajgora was a significant armed conflict that took place in Lakshmipur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Besides coconuts and rice, which of the following is an important cash crop in Lakshmipur?
A) Betel nut
B) Tea
C) Rubber
D) Coffee
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Betel nut

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Lakshmipur is lower than the national average, as per the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

=== CHANDPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Chandpur is a district in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Chandpur is famously known as the "City of Hilsa" (Ilish er Bari).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The city of Chandpur is located at the confluence of which three major rivers?
A) Jamuna, Teesta, and Karatoya
B) Padma, Meghna, and Dakatia
C) Surma, Kushiara, and Kalni
D) Karnaphuli, Halda, and Sangu
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Padma, Meghna, and Dakatia

Q4. [MCQ] What is the most common mode of long-distance transport connecting Chandpur with Dhaka?
A) Airplane
B) Train
C) Bus
D) Launch (ferry)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Launch (ferry)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Chandpur is generally sandy and not suitable for agriculture.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major industry in Chandpur?
A) Tea processing
B) Jute mills
C) Leather tanning
D) Shipbuilding
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute mills

Q7. [MCQ] The big junction of the Padma and Meghna rivers near Chandpur is locally called:
A) Mohona
B) Char
C) Beel
D) Haor
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Mohona

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a separate district, Chandpur was a part of the greater Comilla district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The main administrative town of the district is also named Chandpur.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Chandpur shares a direct border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The district of Chandpur was established in which year?
A) 1971
B) 1978
C) 1984
D) 1990
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The largest wholesale market for Hilsa fish in Bangladesh is located in Chandpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Chandpur district?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q4. [MCQ] The name Chandpur is believed to have originated from a 15th-century ruler named:
A) Chand Roy
B) Chand Sawdagar
C) Chand Gazi
D) Chandidas
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Chand Roy

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Meghna-Dhonagoda Irrigation Project is a large-scale project that protects parts of Chandpur from flooding.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] M. A. Wadud, a pioneering language movement veteran and father of the former education minister Dr. Dipu Moni, was from which district?
A) Faridpur
B) Noakhali
C) Comilla
D) Chandpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chandpur

Q7. [MCQ] The historic Lohagarh Math, a tall monastery-like structure, is located in which upazila of Chandpur?
A) Chandpur Sadar
B) Matlab
C) Hajiganj
D) Faridganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Faridganj

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chandpur Power Station primarily uses coal as its fuel source.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a prominent historical mosque in Chandpur?
A) Sixty Dome Mosque
B) Star Mosque
C) Hajiganj Bara Mosque
D) Kusumba Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Hajiganj Bara Mosque

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Chandpur is higher than the national average, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The renowned painter and cartoonist Shishir Bhattacharjee, known for his political satire, was born in which district?
A) Dhaka
B) Chittagong
C) Chandpur
D) Barisal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chandpur

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the population of Chandpur district is over 3 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Chandpur District in square kilometers?
A) 1,305 sq km
B) 1,704 sq km
C) 1,980 sq km
D) 2,150 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,704 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, Operation Barisal, a major naval commando operation, targeted vessels near which port?
A) Chittagong Port
B) Mongla Port
C) Chandpur Port
D) Narayanganj Port
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chandpur Port

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The first national daily newspaper published from outside Dhaka, "Daily Chandpur Kantha," was established before 1990.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Rupsa Zamindar Bari, known for its unique architecture, is located in which upazila?
A) Kachua
B) Shahrasti
C) Faridganj
D) Haimchar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Faridganj

Q7. [MCQ] The geographical location of Chandpur is particularly vulnerable to river erosion due to a phenomenon known as:
A) Tidal bore
B) Tectonic uplift
C) Scouring at the river confluence
D) Siltation
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Scouring at the river confluence

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chandpur Science and Technology University was officially approved and established before the year 2020.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic Bakhtiyar Khan Mosque in Hajiganj dates back to the rule of which dynasty?
A) The Sena Dynasty
B) The Suri Dynasty
C) The Mughal Dynasty
D) The Baro-Bhuiyans
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Suri Dynasty

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district of Chandpur has the highest number of river fire stations in Bangladesh due to the heavy launch traffic.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== MUNSHIGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Munshiganj is a district in which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Chittagong Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Padma Bridge, one of the largest infrastructure projects in Bangladesh, connects Munshiganj with the southern districts.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Munshiganj is famous for being the leading producer of which vegetable in Bangladesh?
A) Tomato
B) Potato
C) Cauliflower
D) Brinjal
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Potato

Q4. [MCQ] The historic and ancient name of the Munshiganj region was:
A) Gauda
B) Samatata
C) Harikela
D) Bikrampur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bikrampur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous Idrakpur Fort is located in the heart of Munshiganj town.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Dhaleshwari River is one of the main rivers flowing through Munshiganj.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous sweet from Bhagyakul in Munshiganj?
A) Chomchom
B) Roshmalai
C) Monda
D) Ghee-based sweets (Gurer Mishti)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Ghee-based sweets (Gurer Mishti)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Munshiganj has many large tea gardens.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district is located immediately to the south of which major city?
A) Chittagong
B) Sylhet
C) Dhaka
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dhaka

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous writer and filmmaker Humayun Ahmed was born in Munshiganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Atisa Dipankara, a renowned Buddhist scholar who played a major role in spreading Buddhism to Tibet, was born in which region?
A) Mainamati, Comilla
B) Mahasthangarh, Bogra
C) Bikrampur, Munshiganj
D) Paharpur, Naogaon
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bikrampur, Munshiganj

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Idrakpur Fort was built by the Mughals to defend the region from Magh and Portuguese pirates.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Munshiganj district?
A) 4
B) 6
C) 8
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

A) Faridpur
B) Dhaka
C) Munshiganj
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Munshiganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Munshiganj was established as a separate district before the independence of Bangladesh.

A) Trade and commerce
B) Military training
C) Learning and education
D) Shipbuilding
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Learning and education

Q7. [MCQ] The construction of the Idrakpur Fort is attributed to which Mughal general in the 17th century?
A) Shaista Khan
B) Islam Khan
C) Mir Jumla II
D) Man Singh I
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mir Jumla II

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Mawa ferry ghat, which was the main crossing point before the Padma Bridge, is located in Munshiganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The writer and intellectual Humayun Azad was a native of which upazila in Munshiganj?
A) Sirajdikhan
B) Sreenagar
C) Lohajang
D) Tongibari
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sirajdikhan

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate in Munshiganj is higher than in the neighboring Narayanganj district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] What is the most unique architectural feature of the Idrakpur Fort?
A) Its towering main gate
B) A large circular drum on the roof used as a watchtower
C) Its extensive underground tunnels
D) Its intricate terracotta plaques
CORRECT ANSWER: B) A large circular drum on the roof used as a watchtower

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The archaeological site of 'Nateshwar Deul' in Munshiganj has revealed the remains of an ancient Buddhist city and monastery.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Munshiganj District in square kilometers, making it one of the country's smallest districts?
A) 955 sq km
B) 1,120 sq km
C) 1,350 sq km
D) 1,510 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 955 sq km

B) Tongibari

D) Lohajang
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sreenagar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, Munshiganj has a higher percentage of Hindu population compared to the national average.

A) Buddhism
B) Jainism
C) Shaivism (Hinduism)
D) Vaishnavism (Hinduism)
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shaivism (Hinduism)

Q7. [MCQ] In which year was Munshiganj officially established as a district?
A) 1978
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The first private university in Bangladesh, North South University, was founded by a group of philanthropists, many of whom hailed from Munshiganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

B) Dharmapala

CORRECT ANSWER: D) Ramapala

=== MANIKGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Manikganj is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The mighty Padma River flows along the southern border of Manikganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The famous Baliati Palace, a large and ornate zamindar's residence, is the most popular tourist attraction in which district?
A) Tangail
B) Gazipur
C) Manikganj
D) Munshiganj
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Manikganj

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product for which Manikganj is known?
A) Tea
B) Sugarcane
C) Maize (Corn)
D) Cotton
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Maize (Corn)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Paturia ferry ghat, a major river crossing point, is located in Manikganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which major river forms the western boundary of Manikganj district?
A) Meghna
B) Teesta
C) Jamuna
D) Karnaphuli
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jamuna

Q7. [MCQ] What is a common nickname for Manikganj?
A) The City of Palaces
B) The Gateway to the West
C) The Cultural Capital
D) The Granary of Dhaka
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Gateway to the West

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Manikganj is famous for its large-scale salt production.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district was named after a Sufi saint named:
A) Shah Jalal
B) Khan Jahan Ali
C) Manik Shah
D) Shah Makhdum
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Manik Shah

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Manikganj shares a direct land border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] The Baliati Palace complex consists of how many separate main blocks or palaces?
A) Two
B) Four
C) Seven
D) Nine
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Four

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Manikganj was established as a separate district in 1984, before which it was a subdivision of the Dhaka district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Manikganj district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

A) Manikganj Sadar
B) Saturia
C) Singair
D) Ghior
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Manikganj Sadar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous folk music genre known as "Baul Gaan" has no historical roots in the Manikganj region.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Heeralal Sen, considered one of the pioneers of cinema in India and the first Indian to make a feature film, hailed from which district?
A) Kushtia
B) Faridpur
C) Dhaka
D) Manikganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Manikganj

Q7. [MCQ] The Dhaleshwari river is a major distributary of which river that flows through Manikganj?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Jamuna
D) Brahmaputra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jamuna

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The economy of Manikganj is heavily reliant on the ready-made garment (RMG) industry.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The Teota Rajbari, another historic zamindar palace, is located in which upazila of Manikganj?
A) Harirampur
B) Daulatpur
C) Shivalaya
D) Saturia
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shivalaya

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the literacy rate of Manikganj is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] The construction of the Baliati Palace was started by Gobinda Ram Saha and was primarily built during which century?
A) 17th Century
B) 18th Century
C) 19th Century
D) 20th Century

C) 1,620 sq km
D) 1,890 sq km

B) 1953
C) 1966

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Manikganj is primarily composed of Calcareous Brown Floodplain soils, which are less acidic than soils in the northern regions.

A) Salt merchant
B) Jute trader

=== KISHOREGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Kishoreganj is a district located in which administrative division?

B) Dhaka Division

D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The largest Eid congregation in Bangladesh is held at the Sholakia Eidgah Maidan in Kishoreganj.

Q3. [MCQ] The vast, bowl-shaped wetland ecosystems, for which Kishoreganj is famous, are known as:
A) Beels
B) Chars
C) Haors
D) Dighis
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Haors

A) Gopalganj
B) Mymensingh
C) Kishoreganj
D) Tangail
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kishoreganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Brahmaputra River flows directly through Kishoreganj town.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Hilsa
B) Shrimp
C) Freshwater fish (e.g., Boal, Rui)

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Freshwater fish (e.g., Boal, Rui)

A) Meghna
B) Brahmaputra

CORRECT ANSWER: B) Brahmaputra

B) Kolkata

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mymensingh (in a village now in Kishoreganj)

=== NETROKONA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Netrokona is a district located in the northern part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Sylhet Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mymensingh Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Netrokona shares a long international border with the Indian state of Meghalaya.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The landscape of Netrokona is unique for its small hills and the beautiful blue-green water of the Someshwari River, especially in which area?
A) Durgapur (Birishiri)
B) Kalmakanda
C) Kendua
D) Mohanganj
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Durgapur (Birishiri)

Q4. [MCQ] Which major ethnic minority group has a significant presence in the northern part of Netrokona?
A) Chakma
B) Marma
C) Santal
D) Garo
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Garo

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Humayun Ahmed, one of the most popular authors in Bengali literature, was born in Netrokona.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the unique natural resource, a type of white clay, mined in the Birishiri area?
A) Limestone
B) China Clay (Kaolin)
C) Gravel
D) Peat
CORRECT ANSWER: B) China Clay (Kaolin)

Q7. [MCQ] The region of Netrokona is known for which type of folk music?
A) Bhatiali
B) Bhawaiya
C) Jari Gaan and Baul songs
D) Gombhira
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jari Gaan and Baul songs

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Netrokona is a major industrial district with many large factories.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The famous poet Nirmalendu Goon hails from which district?
A) Jamalpur
B) Mymensingh
C) Netrokona
D) Sherpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Netrokona

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Netrokona is completely a plain land with no hilly areas.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Someshwari River originates in which geographical feature in India?
A) The Himalayas
B) The Garo Hills
C) The Lushai Hills
D) The Arakan Mountains
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Garo Hills

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Netrokona was established as a separate district in 1984, after being a part of the Mymensingh district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Netrokona district?
A) 8
B) 10
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 10

Q4. [MCQ] The "Tanka Movement" of the 1940s was a significant peasant uprising in the Netrokona region against which system?
A) The Zamindari system
B) The Indigo plantation system
C) The practice of paying rent in cash (taka)
D) The practice of paying rent with a fixed amount of produce (paddy)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) The practice of paying rent with a fixed amount of produce (paddy)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Birishiri Cultural Academy was established to preserve and promote the culture of the local ethnic minorities.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Humayun Ahmed's father, Faizur Rahman Ahmed, was a police officer who was martyred during which conflict?
A) World War II
B) The 1965 Indo-Pak War
C) The 1971 Bangladesh Liberation War

CORRECT ANSWER: C) The 1971 Bangladesh Liberation War

Q7. [MCQ] The historic 'Dharma-Rajar Bari' is an archaeological site located in which upazila?
A) Netrokona Sadar
B) Kendua
C) Barhatta
D) Purbadhala
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kendua

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Netrokona is among the highest in the Mymensingh division.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Besides the Garo, which other ethnic group is prominent in the Kalmakanda and Durgapur upazilas?
A) Khasi
B) Hajong
C) Manipuri
D) Tripura
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hajong

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Netrokona has a direct railway connection to the capital city, Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] The Tanka Movement was primarily led by which political party?
A) The Muslim League
B) The Indian National Congress
C) The Krishak Praja Party
D) The Communist Party of India
CORRECT ANSWER: D) The Communist Party of India

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, Netrokona district has a population of less than 2.5 million.

C) 3,120 sq km
D) 3,480 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,810 sq km

A) Nachole Uprising
B) Baishakh Revolt
C) Hajong Rebellion
D) Battle of Baushi Ganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The geological formation of the Sushang-Durgapur area is part of the Dihing and Dupi Tila formations of the Tertiary and Quaternary periods.

B) False

B) Mohanganj
C) Kendua
D) Atpara
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kendua

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British period, a significant portion of the Netrokona subdivision was under the Susang zamindari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Kangsha River is a major river in Netrokona and is a tributary of which larger river?
A) Brahmaputra
B) Surma-Meghna
C) Jamuna
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Surma-Meghna

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Birishiri region is one of the very few places in Bangladesh where archaeological evidence of a prehistoric (stone age) settlement has been found.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== SHERPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Sherpur is a district in the northern part of which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rangpur Division
C) Sylhet Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mymensingh Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Sherpur shares an international border with the Indian state of Meghalaya.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The foothills of which mountain range extend into the northern part of Sherpur?
A) Himalayan Range
B) Garo Hills
C) Lushai Hills
D) Arakan Mountains
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Garo Hills

Q4. [MCQ] The Ghazni Abokash Kendra, a popular picnic and tourist spot, is located in which upazila of Sherpur?
A) Sherpur Sadar
B) Jhenaigati
C) Sreebardi
D) Nalitabari
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jhenaigati

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Sherpur is one of the major tea-producing districts of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following ethnic minority groups has a significant presence in Sherpur?
A) Chakma
B) Marma
C) Garo and Hajong
D) Santal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Garo and Hajong

Q7. [MCQ] What is the main agricultural crop of Sherpur?
A) Jute
B) Sugarcane
C) Rice
D) Wheat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rice

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The district of Sherpur was named after the Mughal emperor Sher Shah Suri.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major river flowing through Sherpur?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Bhogai
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bhogai

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Sherpur has a major railway junction connecting it to the rest of the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Sherpur established as a separate district, having previously been a part of Jamalpur?
A) 1978
B) 1981
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Pagal Panthi' movement, a peasant rebellion against the British and zamindars, had its roots in the Sherpur region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas (sub-districts) are there in the Sherpur district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Garh Jaripar Fort' is an ancient ruined fort located in which upazila of Sherpur?
A) Sherpur Sadar
B) Nakla
C) Sreebardi
D) Jhenaigati
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sherpur Sadar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The economy of Sherpur is significantly supported by stone and sand extraction from the Someshwari riverbed.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Tipu Shah was the leader of which significant 19th-century peasant rebellion in the greater Mymensingh region?
A) Faraizi Movement
B) Indigo Revolt
C) Pagal Panthi Movement
D) Tebhaga Movement
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pagal Panthi Movement

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Mariam Nagar Mission', an old Roman Catholic church, is a historical landmark located in which upazila?
A) Nalitabari
B) Nakla
C) Jhenaigati
D) Sreebardi
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Nalitabari

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Sherpur is higher than the average literacy rate of the Mymensingh Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Shah Kamal, a companion of Hazrat Shah Jalal (R), has his shrine (mazar) in which district?
A) Sylhet
B) Sunamganj
C) Mymensingh
D) Sherpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sherpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The land in the northern part of Sherpur is elevated and part of the Pleistocene terraces, similar to the Madhupur Tract.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The 'Pagal Panthi' movement, led by Karam Shah and later his son Tipu Shah, was unique for its syncretic blend of which beliefs?
A) Hinduism, Buddhism, and Jainism
B) Sufism, Vaishnavism, and local folk beliefs
C) Shia and Sunni Islam
D) Christianity and Animism
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sufism, Vaishnavism, and local folk beliefs

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Sherpur district is below 1.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Sherpur District in square kilometers?
A) 1,150 sq km
B) 1,364 sq km
C) 1,580 sq km
D) 1,720 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,364 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The historic 'Baro Duari Mosque' (Twelve-Door Mosque) in Garh Jaripar is attributed to which period?
A) Sena Dynasty
B) Pala Dynasty
C) Sultanate Period
D) Mughal Period
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sultanate Period

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Garo people of Sherpur traditionally follow a patrilineal system of inheritance, where property is passed down through the male line.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Khandaker Abdul Hamid, a prominent journalist and politician who served as a minister, was popularly known by what title for his satirical newspaper column?
A) Tokai
B) Bhaichal
C) Monpobon
D) Moner Kotha
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bhaichal

Q7. [MCQ] The name 'Jhenaigati' upazila is derived from the 'jhinai' or oyster shells found abundantly in its rivers.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British period, the area of modern-day Sherpur was administered as a 'pargana' under the Jamalpur subdivision.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Nalitabari Shaheed Minar' is a memorial built to commemorate the massacre by Pakistani forces during the 1971 Liberation War in which village?
A) Sohagpur
B) Nalitabari Sadar
C) Jhenaigati
D) Kakorkandhi
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Sohagpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Sherpur has the highest percentage of forest land among all districts in the Mymensingh Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== MADARIPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Madaripur is a district within which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Padma River flows along the northern border of Madaripur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The district is named after which renowned 15th-century Sufi saint?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Shah Makhdum
C) Khan Jahan Ali
D) Shah Madar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Shah Madar

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product of Madaripur?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Cotton
D) Pineapple
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a separate district, Madaripur was a part of the greater Faridpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The famous Dargah of Shah Madar is located in which upazila of Madaripur?
A) Madaripur Sadar
B) Shibchar
C) Rajoir
D) Kalkini
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Madaripur Sadar

Q7. [MCQ] Which major bridge provides a direct road link from Madaripur to the capital city, Dhaka?
A) Bangabandhu Bridge
B) Lalon Shah Bridge
C) Padma Bridge
D) Rupsha Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Padma Bridge

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Madaripur is famous for its large hilly areas and forests.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The Arial Khan River is one of the main rivers flowing through the district.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Madaripur is a leading producer of coconuts in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Madaripur officially established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Haji Shariatullah, the founder of the influential Faraizi Movement, was born in a village that is now part of Madaripur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Madaripur district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] The historic 'Algi Kazibari Mosque' is a well-preserved structure from which period?
A) Pala Dynasty
B) Sena Dynasty
C) Sultanate Period
D) British Period
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sultanate Period

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous filmmaker Tareque Masud, director of "Matir Moina", hailed from Madaripur.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (He was from Faridpur)

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Shokuni Lake' is a large, historic water body located in the heart of which town?
A) Faridpur
B) Gopalganj
C) Madaripur
D) Shariatpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Madaripur

Q7. [MCQ] The economy of Madaripur is significantly boosted by agriculture and:
A) Tourism
B) Heavy industry
C) Foreign remittances
D) Garment factories
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Foreign remittances

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The tomb of Bir Shrestha Lance Naik Munshi Abdur Rouf is located in Madaripur.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in Rangamati)

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the approach road to the Padma Bridge that runs through Shibchar upazila?
A) Dhaka-Khulna Highway
B) Dhaka-Barisal Highway
C) Expressway
D) Padma Link Road
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Expressway

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Madaripur district is lower than the national average, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Faraizi Movement, initiated by Haji Shariatullah, primarily aimed to:
A) Promote English education
B) Overthrow the British
C) Purify Islam by adhering strictly to its fundamental duties (fara'id)
D) Establish a separate state for Muslims
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Purify Islam by adhering strictly to its fundamental duties (fara'id)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Madaripur district is more than 2 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Madaripur District in square kilometers?
A) 980 sq km
B) 1,125 sq km
C) 1,350 sq km
D) 1,510 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,125 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Ambikacharan Majumdar, a prominent lawyer and politician who served as the President of the Indian National Congress in 1916, was from which greater district?
A) Dhaka
B) Barisal
C) Faridpur (including modern-day Madaripur)
D) Khulna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Faridpur (including modern-day Madaripur)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Madaripur sub-division, one of the oldest in Bengal, was established in 1854.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The historic 'Raja Ram Mandir' in Rajoir upazila is a testament to the influence of which religious sect?
A) Shaivism
B) Shaktism
C) Vaishnavism
D) Buddhism
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Vaishnavism

Q7. [MCQ] The geography of Madaripur is dominated by a landscape of low-lying marshes and interconnected rivers, which is known as:
A) Barind Tract
B) Madhupur Tract
C) Haor Basin
D) Bil Tract
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bil Tract

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, the Pakistani army faced significant resistance from freedom fighters at the Samaddar Bridge in Madaripur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The first jute mill established in the greater Faridpur region was the Madaripur Jute Mills.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Madaripur is classified as Ganges River Floodplain soil, which is ideal for both Aus and Aman rice cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== GOPALGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Gopalganj is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Barisal Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Gopalganj is famously known as the birthplace of the Father of the Nation, Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The mausoleum complex of Bangabandhu is located in which upazila of Gopalganj?
A) Gopalganj Sadar
B) Kotalipara
C) Tungipara
D) Muksudpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tungipara

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows through Gopalganj?
A) Padma
B) Madhumati
C) Jamuna
D) Meghna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Madhumati

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Gopalganj was a part of the greater Faridpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The current Prime Minister of Bangladesh, Sheikh Hasina, hails from which district?
A) Madaripur
B) Dhaka
C) Gopalganj
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gopalganj

Q7. [MCQ] The region of Gopalganj is known for its vast low-lying wetland areas called:
A) Haors
B) Chars
C) Beels
D) Dighis
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Beels

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Gopalganj is a major industrial hub with many large factories.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the science and technology university located in Gopalganj?
A) Gopalganj University of Science and Technology
B) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University
C) Madhumati Science and Technology University
D) Tungipara University of Science and Technology
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district was named after a British administrator named Gopal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Gopalganj upgraded from a subdivision to a district?
A) 1972
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Orakandi Thakur Bari' is a major pilgrimage site for the Matua community, located in Gopalganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Gopalganj district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] The poet Sukanta Bhattacharya, known for his revolutionary and patriotic poems, was born in a village that is now part of which upazila?
A) Tungipara
B) Gopalganj Sadar
C) Kotalipara
D) Kashiani
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kotalipara

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The mausoleum of Bangabandhu in Tungipara was designed by the same architect who designed the Jatiya Sangsad Bhaban.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
