A) Muksudpur
B) Kashiani
C) Kotalipara
D) Gopalganj Sadar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Gopalganj Sadar

Q7. [MCQ] The Matua community, a Hindu reformist sect, was founded by whom?
A) Lalon Shah
B) Harichand Thakur
C) Chaitanya Mahaprabhu
D) Ramakrishna Paramahamsa
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Harichand Thakur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Gopalganj district is higher than the national average, as per the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Bornir Baor' is a large wetland in Gopalganj famous for what traditional event?
A) Buffalo fighting
B) Horse racing
C) Bullock cart racing
D) Boat racing
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Boat racing

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War, the Pakistani army was able to easily capture Tungipara due to its lack of defenses.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The ancient region of Kotalipara in Gopalganj is believed to have been a part of which Mauryan-era province?
A) Gauda
B) Samatata
C) Vanga
D) Pundra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Vanga

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Gopalganj is derived from a local zamindar named Gopal Das who established a 'ganj' (market) in the area in the 19th century.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Gopalganj District in square kilometers?
A) 1,160 sq km
B) 1,468 sq km
C) 1,750 sq km
D) 1,980 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,468 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Kotalipara is a significant archaeological site where several copper plate inscriptions of which post-Gupta dynasty were found?
A) Pala Dynasty
B) Sena Dynasty
C) Deva Dynasty
D) Chandra Dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chandra Dynasty

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The landscape of Gopalganj is part of the 'Ganges Tidal Floodplain', characterized by numerous tidal creeks and low-lying basins.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University (BSMRSTU) officially established?
A) 1991
B) 1996
C) 2001
D) 2006
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 2001

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Charda Chashi Bidroho' (Peasant Revolt of Charda) in Muksudpur upazila was a historical uprising against:
A) British Indigo planters
B) Local zamindars
C) Pakistani army
D) Religious leaders
CORRECT ANSWER: A) British Indigo planters

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, Gopalganj has the lowest population density among the five districts of the greater Faridpur region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Sheikh Lutfar Rahman, the father of Bangabandhu, served in which professional capacity at the Gopalganj Civil Court?
A) Lawyer
B) Judge
C) Sheristadar (Record keeper)
D) Magistrate
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sheristadar (Record keeper)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bill Rout Canal, which connects the Madhumati and Atharobanki rivers, is a significant man-made waterway in Gopalganj that has improved local navigation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

B) Jute

B) Samatata
C) Idilpur
D) Vanga

B) 1,174 sq km
C) 1,350 sq km
D) 1,520 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Faraizi Movement declared the region a 'Dar al-Harb' (House of War) because it was:
A) Prone to frequent conflicts
B) Ruled by non-Muslims (the British)

D) Under attack from Burmese invaders
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ruled by non-Muslims (the British)

A) The Tagores
B) The Roys of Bhawal
C) The Nawabs of Dhaka

A) Sylhet
B) Rangpur
C) Greater Faridpur (including Shariatpur)
D) Chittagong
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Greater Faridpur (including Shariatpur)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Shariatpur is primarily part of the Ganges Meander Floodplain, characterized by complex patterns of ridges and basins.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] In which upazila is the Shariatpur branch of the 'Chandpur Irrigation Project' located, helping to control floods?
A) Zanjira
B) Bhedarganj
C) Gosairhat
D) Damudya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bhedarganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district of Shariatpur has no railway connectivity.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== RAJBARI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Rajbari is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dhaka Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The town of Rajbari is situated on the southern bank of the Padma River.

Q3. [MCQ] The district's name "Rajbari" translates to what in English?
A) King's Boat
B) King's Market
C) King's Palace
D) King's Road
CORRECT ANSWER: C) King's Palace

Q4. [MCQ] Which famous river port, once one of the most important in Bengal, is located in Rajbari?
A) Paturia Ghat
B) Mawa Ghat
C) Aricha Ghat
D) Goalundo Ghat
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Goalundo Ghat

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a separate district, Rajbari was a part of the greater Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural crop of Rajbari?

B) Jute
C) Coffee
D) Rubber
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute

Q7. [MCQ] The Lalon Shah Bridge connects Rajbari with which neighboring district?
A) Faridpur
B) Pabna
C) Manikganj
D) Kushtia
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pabna

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajbari is a major industrial district with numerous heavy industries.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The famous novelist Mir Mosharraf Hossain spent a part of his life and is buried in which upazila of Rajbari?
A) Rajbari Sadar
B) Pangsha
C) Baliakandi
D) Goalundo
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Baliakandi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Rajbari has a direct road and rail connection to the capital, Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Rajbari officially established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic importance of Goalundo Ghat was primarily due to its role as a major trans-shipment point between broad-gauge and meter-gauge railways.

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Rajbari district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Rajbari Government College' was originally established in the name of which zamindar?
A) Raja Sitaram Ray
B) Raja Surya Kumar
C) Raja Pramatha Nath Roy
D) Raja Pratapaditya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Raja Surya Kumar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous Hilsa fish is found in abundance in the Padma River near Goalundo.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The tomb of which famous Muslim saint is located at the shrine in Pangsha?
A) Shah Ali Baghdadi
B) Shah Fariduddin Masud
C) Shah Pahloan
D) Shah Madar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Pahloan

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is another major river that flows through Rajbari?
A) Gorai River
B) Jamuna River
C) Meghna River
D) Teesta River
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Gorai River

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The renowned artist Rokeya Sultana, known for her printmaking and paintings, was born in Rajbari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic 'Nawab Bari' or palace of the Nawab of Dhaka is located in Rajbari.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Rajbari district is higher than the national average, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Eastern Bengal Railway extended its line to Goalundo Ghat in which year, cementing its importance?
A) 1857
B) 1871
C) 1895
D) 1905
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1871

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Rajbari district is less than 1.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Rajbari District in square kilometers?
A) 950 sq km
B) 1,118 sq km
C) 1,320 sq km
D) 1,510 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,118 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Mir Mosharraf Hossain's famous novel 'Bishad Sindhu' was first published while he was working in which estate?
A) The Puthia Estate
B) The Dighapatia Estate
C) The Delduar Estate
D) The Bhawal Estate
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Delduar Estate

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British Raj, the original district headquarters of this region was in Pangsha, not Rajbari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Dhol-Samudra Dighi' is a large, ancient pond excavated by which king of the Sena Dynasty?
A) Ballal Sen
B) Lakshman Sen
C) Hemanta Sen
D) It was excavated before the Sena Dynasty.
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Ballal Sen

Q7. [MCQ] The geography of Rajbari is prone to the formation of temporary islands in the Padma river, which are known as:
A) Beels
B) Haors
C) Chars
D) Tillas
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chars

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, Rajbari was liberated from Pakistani forces in the first week of December.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was liberated later in December).

Q9. [MCQ] The ancient name of the region that includes modern-day Rajbari was:
A) Bikrampur
B) Banga (Vanga)
C) Pundravardhana
D) Harikela
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Banga (Vanga)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil composition in Rajbari is primarily non-calcareous grey floodplain soil, which is distinct from the soil in the neighboring Kushtia district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== MAGURA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Magura is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Shakib Al Hasan, one of the world's most famous cricket all-rounders, was born in Magura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main river flowing through Magura town?
A) Padma
B) Jamuna
C) Nabaganga
D) Meghna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nabaganga

Q4. [MCQ] What is a major agricultural product of Magura district?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Coffee
D) Apples
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a separate district, Magura was a subdivision of the Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The district is located to the north-east of which major divisional city?
A) Khulna
B) Barisal
C) Rajshahi
D) Jessore
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jessore

Q7. [MCQ] The famous 'Ghazi Kalu-Champabati' folk tale and shrine are associated with which upazila of Magura?
A) Magura Sadar
B) Sreepur
C) Mohammadpur
D) Shalikha
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Shalikha

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Magura has a large international airport.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district headquarters is a town also named Magura.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Gorai River, a major distributary of the Padma, flows through Magura district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Magura officially established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Raja Sitaram Ray's Palace' is a famous archaeological site in the Mohammadpur upazila of Magura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Magura district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 4

Q4. [MCQ] Poet and literary critic Syed Ali Ahsan was born in which upazila of Magura?
A) Magura Sadar
B) Mohammadpur
C) Sreepur
D) Shalikha
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Magura Sadar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The region of Magura was a significant area of resistance during the British-led Indigo Revolt.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the historic temple located in Sreepur that is a notable pilgrimage site?
A) Kantajew Temple
B) Puthia Temple
C) Sreepur Temple
D) Siddheshwari Math
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Siddheshwari Math

Q7. [MCQ] The district of Magura has direct road connectivity with Dhaka via which bridge?
A) Padma Bridge
B) Bangabandhu Bridge
C) Lalon Shah Bridge
D) Rupsha Bridge
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Padma Bridge

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Magura district is lower than the national average, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Khatial' is a traditional form of rural folk opera or theatre native to which greater region?
A) Sylhet
B) Chittagong
C) Jessore-Magura
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jessore-Magura

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Magura has no railway line passing through it.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Raja Sitaram Ray established his capital in Mohammadpur and ruled in defiance of which empire in the early 18th century?
A) The British Empire
B) The Sena Empire
C) The Mughal Empire
D) The Pala Empire
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Mughal Empire

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Magura district is less than one million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Magura District in square kilometers?
A) 850 sq km
B) 1,039 sq km
C) 1,210 sq km
D) 1,420 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,039 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The historic battle between the rebellious zamindar Raja Sitaram Ray and the Mughal forces was led by which Subahdar's general?
A) Shaista Khan's forces
B) Mir Jumla's forces
C) Murshid Quli Khan's forces
D) Islam Khan's forces
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Murshid Quli Khan's forces

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil composition in Magura is primarily part of the 'Ganges River Floodplain', which is very fertile for cropping.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Magura subdivision, under Jessore district, established?
A) 1845
B) 1883
C) 1901
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1845

Q7. [MCQ] Bir Shrestha Lutfur Rahman, a hero of the Liberation War, was born in Magura.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: B) False (There is no Bir Shrestha by this name).

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War, the Battle of Alfapur was a significant engagement where freedom fighters ambushed a Pakistani army convoy in Magura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The archaeological site of 'Chandraketugarh' is located in Magura.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: B) False (It is in West Bengal, India).

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Nabaganga River, which flows through Magura, has its origins in the Mathabhanga River in Chuadanga district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== JHENAIDAH ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Jhenaidah is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Bir Shrestha Hamidur Rahman, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, was born in a village that is now part of Jhenaidah district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the main river that flows through Jhenaidah town?
A) Padma
B) Nabaganga
C) Gorai
D) Kumar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nabaganga

Q4. [MCQ] The district is well-known for producing which agricultural crop?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Cotton
D) Apples
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Jhenaidah shares a direct land border with the country of India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The famous 'Naldanga Temple Complex' is a major archaeological site in which district?
A) Magura
B) Kushtia
C) Jhenaidah
D) Jessore
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jhenaidah

Q7. [MCQ] What is a famous traditional sweet from Jhenaidah?
A) Roshmalai
B) Monda
C) Sweet Curd (Doi) and Ghee
D) Chomchom
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sweet Curd (Doi) and Ghee

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Jhenaidah was a subdivision under the greater Kushtia district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The revolutionary freedom fighter Bagha Jatin (Jatindranath Mukherjee) was born in which district?
A) Jessore
B) Kushtia
C) Jhenaidah
D) Magura
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jhenaidah

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Jhenaidah has direct railway connectivity.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Jhenaidah officially established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1990
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The area of Jhenaidah was a significant center of the 19th-century Indigo Revolt against British planters.

A) 4
B) 6
C) 8
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

A) Buddhist Viharas

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sultanate-era Mosques

A) Jhenaidah Sadar
B) Kaliganj
C) Shailkupa
D) Harinakunda
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shailkupa

A) Kaliganj
B) Kotchandpur
C) Jhenaidah Sadar
D) Moheshpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jhenaidah Sadar

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Jhenaidah district is lower than the national average, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Shailkupa
B) Kaliganj

CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kaliganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous Baul singer Lalon Shah spent his early life in Harinakunda upazila of Jhenaidah.

A) Marble
B) Sandstone

=== CHUADANGA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Chuadanga is a district in the southwestern part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Chuadanga holds the distinction of being the first temporary capital of independent Bangladesh in 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main river that flows through Chuadanga district?
A) Nabaganga
B) Gorai
C) Kumar
D) Mathabhanga
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Mathabhanga

Q4. [MCQ] The district is a major producer of which sweet winter product?
A) Honey
B) Date Jaggery (Khejur Gur)
C) Sugarcane Molasses
D) Maple Syrup
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Date Jaggery (Khejur Gur)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Chuadanga shares a long international border with the Indian state of West Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Darshana land port is a major border crossing located in which district?
A) Jessore
B) Meherpur
C) Satkhira
D) Chuadanga
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chuadanga

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major cash crop cultivated in Chuadanga?
A) Tea
B) Betel Leaf (Paan)
C) Rubber
D) Coffee
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Betel Leaf (Paan)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The first railway line in what is now Bangladesh was established through Chuadanga.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The climate of Chuadanga is known for experiencing some of the highest temperatures in Bangladesh during summer.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Chuadanga was a part of the greater Pabna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Chuadanga officially established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1978
C) 1984
D) 1989
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The provisional government of Bangladesh was formally proclaimed in Chuadanga on 10 April 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Chuadanga district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 4

Q4. [MCQ] The historic 'Keru & Co. Distillery' in Darshana, the only one in Bangladesh, was established in which year?
A) 1897
B) 1911
C) 1938
D) 1952
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1938

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bhairab River, which flows through Meherpur and Jessore, originates from the Mathabhanga River in Chuadanga.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Begum Rokeya Sakhawat Hossain, the pioneer of female education, was born in Chuadanga.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: B) False (She was born in Rangpur).

Q7. [MCQ] The Gholdari Mosque, a notable single-domed Sultanate-era mosque, is located in which upazila?
A) Chuadanga Sadar
B) Alamdanga
C) Damurhuda
D) Jibannagar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Alamdanga

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Chuadanga is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The first commemorative postage stamps of independent Bangladesh were issued from where?
A) A post office in London
B) Mujibnagar, Meherpur
C) Chuadanga Post Office
D) Kolkata GPO
CORRECT ANSWER: A) A post office in London

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The economy of Chuadanga is primarily based on agriculture and cross-border trade.

B) 1862

D) 1885

D) 1,510 sq km

=== MEHERPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Meherpur is the smallest district in Bangladesh and is part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Khulna Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic Proclamation of Independence of Bangladesh was formally made in Meherpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The place where the first government of Bangladesh was formed is known as:
A) Tungipara
B) Baidyanathtala
C) Ramgarh
D) Chuadanga
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Baidyanathtala

Q4. [MCQ] The historic site of Baidyanathtala was later renamed what?
A) Shanti Nagar
B) Nazrul Nagar
C) Mujibnagar
D) Swadhin Nagar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mujibnagar

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Meherpur shares an international border with the Indian state of West Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main river flowing through Meherpur district?
A) Padma
B) Mathabhanga
C) Bhairab
D) Kumar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bhairab

Q7. [MCQ] The Mujibnagar Memorial Complex is built to commemorate which event?
A) The 1952 Language Movement
B) The 1971 Liberation War oath-taking ceremony
C) The end of the British Raj
D) The historic 7th March speech
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The 1971 Liberation War oath-taking ceremony

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Meherpur is a leading producer of tea in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product of Meherpur?
A) Jute
B) Tobacco
C) Vegetables and Mangoes
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Vegetables and Mangoes

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Before 1947, Meherpur was a part of the Nadia district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Meherpur established as a district, the last in Bangladesh to receive this status?
A) 1984
B) 1991
C) 1996
D) 2000
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 2000

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The oath-taking ceremony of the first government of Bangladesh took place on April 17, 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Meherpur district?
A) 3
B) 4
C) 5
D) 6
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 3

Q4. [MCQ] Who was sworn in as the acting President of Bangladesh at the Mujibnagar ceremony?
A) Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
B) Tajuddin Ahmad
C) Syed Nazrul Islam
D) A. H. M. Qamaruzzaman
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Syed Nazrul Islam

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The architect of the main Mujibnagar Memorial monument is Louis I. Kahn.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The historic 'Amjhupi Nilkuthi' is a relic from which period of colonial exploitation?
A) Dutch spice trade
B) Portuguese piracy
C) British indigo plantation
D) French textile manufacturing
CORRECT ANSWER: C) British indigo plantation

Q7. [MCQ] The Mujibnagar government's oath-taking ceremony took place in a mango grove, which is locally known as:
A) Baidyanathtala Amrakanan
B) Mujib Udyan
C) Shadhinota Bithi
D) Amra Bagan
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Baidyanathtala Amrakanan

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Meherpur district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Meherpur was a subdivision of which greater district?
A) Jessore
B) Pabna
C) Kushtia
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kushtia

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] There is no railway line that passes through Meherpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Who administered the oath of office to the acting President and Prime Minister at Mujibnagar?
A) M. A. G. Osmani
B) Yusuf Ali
C) Abdul Mannan
D) Amir-ul Islam
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Yusuf Ali

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Meherpur is believed to have originated from a 16th-century Sufi saint named Meher Ali Shah.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Meherpur District in square kilometers, making it the smallest in the country?
A) 751 sq km
B) 815 sq km
C) 920 sq km
D) 1,010 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 751 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The original name of the village 'Baidyanathtala' was renamed 'Mujibnagar' by whom?
A) Sheikh Mujibur Rahman
B) Syed Nazrul Islam
C) Tajuddin Ahmad
D) M. A. G. Osmani
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tajuddin Ahmad

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, Meherpur has the lowest population of any district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (Bandarban has the lowest).

Q6. [MCQ] The architect of the Mujibnagar Memorial Complex, including the map of Bangladesh and the monument, is:
A) Mazharul Islam
B) Fazlur Rahman Khan
C) Kashef Mahboob Chowdhury
D) Tanveer Masood
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Tanveer Masood

Q7. [MCQ] During the Liberation War, Meherpur was the headquarters of which Sector of the Mukti Bahini?
A) Sector 1
B) Sector 2
C) Sector 8
D) Sector 9
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sector 8

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] General M. A. G. Osmani was present at the Mujibnagar oath-taking ceremony and was appointed the Commander-in-Chief of the Bangladesh Forces.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Ballavpur Mission, an old Christian mission with a historic church, is located near which upazila?
A) Meherpur Sadar
B) Gangni
C) Mujibnagar
D) It is in a different district.
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Gangni

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Meherpur is part of the 'Moribund Ganges Delta', characterized by heavy clay soils which are excellent for vegetable cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== NARAIL ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Narail is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous avant-garde artist S. M. Sultan, known for his paintings of muscular peasants, was born in Narail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Mashrafe Bin Mortaza, the celebrated cricketer and former captain of the Bangladesh national team, hails from which district?
A) Jessore
B) Magura
C) Narail
D) Khulna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Narail

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows through Narail town?
A) Padma
B) Madhumati
C) Chitra
D) Bhairab
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chitra

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Narail was a subdivision under the greater Khulna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural crop in Narail?
A) Tea
B) Rice and Jute
C) Cotton
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rice and Jute

Q7. [MCQ] The "Sultan Mela" is an annual fair held in Narail to celebrate the birth anniversary of which artist?
A) Zainul Abedin
B) S. M. Sultan
C) Quamrul Hassan
D) Jamini Roy
CORRECT ANSWER: B) S. M. Sultan

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Narail has a direct land border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district headquarters is a town also named Narail.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The traditional boat race is a very popular cultural event on the rivers of Narail.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Narail officially established as a district?
A) 1978
B) 1981
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Bir Shrestha Nur Mohammad Sheikh, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, was born in a village in Narail district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Narail district?
A) 3
B) 4
C) 5
D) 6
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 3

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Narail Victorian College', one of the oldest educational institutions in the region, was founded by the local:
A) British administration
B) Christian missionaries
C) Zamindars
D) Merchant community
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Zamindars

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Shishu Swarga' (Children's Paradise) was an art school and park established by S. M. Sultan for underprivileged children.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The historic 'Bandha Ghat' on the Chitra river is a famous landmark in which upazila?
A) Narail Sadar
B) Kalia
C) Lohagara
D) It is not in Narail.
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Narail Sadar

Q7. [MCQ] The economy of Narail is primarily based on:
A) Industry and manufacturing
B) Agriculture and fisheries
C) Tourism
D) Information Technology
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Agriculture and fisheries

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a separate subdivision, the area of Narail was part of the Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The great flutist, Pandit Hariprasad Chaurasia, has family roots in Narail.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: B) False

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Narail is higher than the national average, as per the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The name 'Narail' is believed to have originated from the local zamindars who were known by what title?
A) Bhuiyan
B) Chowdhury
C) Nariyal (meaning 'of the boat')
D) Laskar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nariyal (meaning 'of the boat')

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Narail district is less than 1 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Narail District in square kilometers?
A) 780 sq km
B) 990 sq km
C) 1,150 sq km
D) 1,320 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 990 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Neelkuthi' (indigo factory) at Goalerghat is a remnant of the oppressive indigo cultivation forced upon peasants in the 19th century by which group?
A) Portuguese traders
B) Dutch merchants
C) French planters
D) British planters
CORRECT ANSWER: D) British planters

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] S. M. Sultan's artistic philosophy was unique because he intentionally depicted Bengali peasants and laborers with heroic, muscular bodies, symbolizing their strength and productivity.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Narail subdivision established?
A) 1861
B) 1882
C) 1905
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1861

Q7. [MCQ] The historic 'Nishinath Tola' in Lohagara is known for being a:
A) Royal cremation ground
B) Buddhist monastery
C) Sultanate-era mosque
D) British-era courthouse
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Royal cremation ground

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chitra River, which flows through Narail, is a distributary of the Nabaganga River.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] During the Liberation War, the Battle of Lohagara was a significant victory for the Mukti Bahini, leading to the liberation of the area.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Narail is primarily part of the 'Ganges Tidal Floodplain', which is characterized by non-calcareous grey soils.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== SATKHIRA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Satkhira is a district in the southwestern corner of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] A large portion of the Sundarbans, the world's largest mangrove forest, is located in Satkhira district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is a famous natural product collected from the Sundarbans in Satkhira?
A) Tea
B) Silk
C) Honey
D) Rubber
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Honey

Q4. [MCQ] Satkhira shares a long international land and riverine border with which country?
A) Myanmar
B) Nepal
C) Bhutan
D) India
CORRECT ANSWER: D) India

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Satkhira is famous for its large-scale cultivation of apples and oranges.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main river that forms the international border in the Satkhira region?
A) Padma
B) Jamuna
C) Ichamati-Kalindi
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ichamati-Kalindi

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major industry in Satkhira, contributing significantly to Bangladesh's exports?
A) Ready-made garments
B) Leather processing
C) Shrimp and crab farming
D) Jute mills
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shrimp and crab farming

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bhomra Land Port is an important trade point between Bangladesh and India, located in Satkhira.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The famous cricketer Soumya Sarkar hails from which district?
A) Khulna
B) Jessore
C) Satkhira
D) Bagerhat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Satkhira

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Satkhira was a part of the greater Jessore district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Satkhira established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Pran Nath Roy Chowdhury Zamindar Bari' (also known as Kothabari) is a major architectural landmark in Satkhira.

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Satkhira district?
A) 5
B) 7

D) 11

A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kopotakkho River, immortalized in a poem by Michael Madhusudan Dutt, flows through Satkhira.

A) Pala Buddhist
B) British Colonial
C) Modern
D) Mughal and Sultanate

Q7. [MCQ] Before becoming a separate subdivision, Satkhira was administered under which greater district?
A) Jessore
B) Khulna
C) Barisal
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khulna

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Satkhira district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

A) Satkhira Sadar
B) Kaliganj
C) Assasuni
D) Debhata
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kaliganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is highly vulnerable to climate change impacts like sea-level rise and cyclones.

A) 2,980 sq km
B) 3,450 sq km
C) 3,817 sq km

A) 1852
B) 1861
C) 1882
D) 1905
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1861

B) Kaliganj

CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shyamnagar

=== PIROJPUR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Pirojpur is a district in the southern part of which division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Barisal Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is often called the "Venice of Bengal" due to its intricate network of rivers and canals.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous floating market in Pirojpur, especially known for guavas?
A) Banaripara Market
B) Bhimruli Floating Market
C) Nesarabad Market
D) Kawkhali Market
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Bhimruli Floating Market

Q4. [MCQ] Pirojpur is a leading producer of which of the following fruits?
A) Litchi
B) Mango
C) Guava and Hog Plum (Amra)
D) Pineapple
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Guava and Hog Plum (Amra)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Baleshwar River is the main river that flows by Pirojpur town.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major local industry in Pirojpur?
A) Shipbuilding
B) Coir (coconut fiber) industry
C) Tea processing
D) Leather tanning
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Coir (coconut fiber) industry

Q7. [MCQ] Delwar Hossain Sayeedi, a politician and Islamic scholar, hailed from which district?
A) Bagerhat
B) Barguna
C) Pirojpur
D) Jhalokati
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pirojpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Pirojpur was part of the greater Faridpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district headquarters is a town also named Pirojpur.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Pirojpur shares a direct border with the Bay of Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Pirojpur established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Rayerkathi Zamindar Bari' and its numerous Shiva temples are located in Pirojpur.

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Pirojpur district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9

CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

A) Khulna
B) Faridpur
C) Jessore
D) Barisal (Bakerganj)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Barisal (Bakerganj)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Ahsan Habib, a renowned modern poet and journalist, was born in Pirojpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Kumarkhali River' is a major waterway in which upazila, famous for its boat-building industry?
A) Pirojpur Sadar
B) Nesarabad (Swarupkathi)
C) Mathbaria
D) Bhandaria
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nesarabad (Swarupkathi)

A) Banaripara
B) Kaukhali
C) Swarupkathi
D) Indurkani
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Swarupkathi

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Pirojpur is one of the highest in Bangladesh, according to the 2022 census.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) Bhandaria
B) Zianagar
C) Pirojpur Sadar
D) Nesarabad
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pirojpur Sadar

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district has direct railway connectivity to Dhaka.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q1. [MCQ] The name 'Pirojpur' is widely believed to be derived from the name of the daughter of which Mughal prince?

D) Aurangzeb
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Shuja

A) 1,050 sq km
B) 1,277 sq km
C) 1,490 sq km
D) 1,650 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,277 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] During the Liberation War of 1971, the massacre at the 'Pirojpur C&B Ghat' was a brutal event where many civilians were killed by Pakistani forces.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

A) 1859
B) 1885
C) 1901
D) 1921
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1859

A) Titumir
B) Haji Shariatullah
C) Golam Masum
D) It is not famous for a major revolt.
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Golam Masum

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The British established their administrative center at Pirojpur due to its strategic location on the Baleshwar River, which provided access to the Sundarbans for timber.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) Madhupur Forest
B) Lawachara Forest
C) Bhawal Forest
D) The Sundarbans
CORRECT ANSWER: D) The Sundarbans

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Pirojpur was liberated from Pakistani occupation forces on December 8, 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== JHALOKATI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Jhalokati is a small district located in which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Chittagong Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barisal Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famous for its large guava orchards and floating guava markets.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows through Jhalokati town?
A) Padma
B) Sugandha
C) Meghna
D) Baleshwar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sugandha

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major product of Jhalokati's cottage industry?
A) Silk sarees
B) Cane and bamboo crafts
C) Terracotta pottery
D) Brassware
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Cane and bamboo crafts

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Sher-e-Bangla A. K. Fazlul Huq, a prominent political leader, was born in Jhalokati.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The district headquarters is a town also named Jhalokati.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] What is a common mode of transport within the district due to its many rivers and canals?
A) Cable car
B) Tram
C) Boat
D) Subway
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Boat

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Jhalokati was a part of the greater Faridpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional boat race, or 'Nouka Baich', is a popular cultural event in Jhalokati.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Jhalokati is a major industrial hub with many steel and cement factories.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Jhalokati officially established as a district?
A) 1972
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1991
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Gabkhan Canal, often called the "Suez Canal of Bengal," connects the Sugandha and Bishkhali rivers, significantly shortening the waterway to Mongla port.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Jhalokati district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 4

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Jhalokati was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Khulna
B) Faridpur
C) Barisal (Bakerganj)
D) Patuakhali
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barisal (Bakerganj)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Kamini Roy, the first woman to graduate with honours in British India, was born in a village that is now in Jhalokati district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (She was born in Basanda, now in Barisal district).

Q6. [MCQ] The historic 'Sujabad Kella' (fort) was built by the Mughals to defend against whom?
A) The British East India Company
B) Arakanese and Portuguese pirates
C) The Tripura Kingdom
D) Local zamindar rebels
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Arakanese and Portuguese pirates

Q7. [MCQ] What is the old name of Jhalokati town?
A) Chandradwip
B) Maharajganj
C) Bakla
D) Fatehabad
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Maharajganj

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil and climate of Jhalokati are highly suitable for hog plum (Amra) cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Civil Surgeon's Building' in Jhalokati is a notable example of which architectural style?
A) Mughal
B) Sultanate
C) Indo-Saracenic
D) European colonial
CORRECT ANSWER: D) European colonial

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Jhalokati is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Gabkhan Canal was excavated in which year during the British period?
A) 1890
B) 1905
C) 1918
D) 1932
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1918

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, Jhalokati has the lowest population of all districts in the Barisal Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Jhalokati District in square kilometers?
A) 550 sq km
B) 707 sq km
C) 920 sq km
D) 1,100 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 707 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] During the Liberation War of 1971, the massacre at the Jhalokati Sadar Hospital was a brutal event where Pakistani forces killed numerous doctors, patients, and civilians.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Jhalokati is part of the 'Active Ganges Deltaic Plain', characterized by silty clay loams that are poorly drained.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Jhalokati subdivision established?
A) 1875
B) 1895
C) 1915
D) 1945
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1875

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Kirtipasha Zamindar Bari' is historically significant for the role of its female zamindars in promoting what?
A) Military training
B) Female education
C) Religious reform
D) Indigo cultivation
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Female education

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Jhalokati is believed to have originated from 'Jelera Kathi' (Fishermen's settlement) or from the abundance of Jhal trees.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Saat Dastan' manuscript, a historical Persian text, mentions the area of Jhalokati as a major center for what?
A) Salt production
B) Muslin weaving
C) Boat building
D) Spice trade
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Boat building

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Jhalokati was liberated from Pakistani forces on December 8, 1971, through the efforts of the Mukti Bahini without a major frontal battle in the town itself.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== PATUAKHALI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Patuakhali is a coastal district in which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Dhaka Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Barisal Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Patuakhali is popularly known as "Sagar Kanya," which means "Daughter of the Sea."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Kuakata, a famous sea beach known for offering views of both sunrise and sunset, is located in which district?
A) Cox's Bazar
B) Chittagong
C) Patuakhali
D) Barguna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Patuakhali

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major river flowing into the Bay of Bengal through Patuakhali?
A) Jamuna
B) Teesta
C) Andharmanik
D) Surma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Andharmanik

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The economy of Patuakhali is primarily based on heavy industries like steel and cement.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main agricultural crop of Patuakhali?
A) Jute
B) Tea
C) Rice
D) Wheat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rice

Q7. [MCQ] The Payra Sea Port, one of Bangladesh's major seaports, is being developed in which district?
A) Chittagong
B) Khulna
C) Barguna
D) Patuakhali
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Patuakhali

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Patuakhali was a part of the greater Khulna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which ethnic minority group, known for their Buddhist faith and unique culture, has a significant presence in Patuakhali?
A) Garo
B) Santal
C) Rakhine
D) Marma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rakhine

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Patuakhali is directly connected to Dhaka by railway.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Patuakhali established as a district?
A) 1969
B) 1972
C) 1980
D) 1984
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1969

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Sreerampur Miah Bari Mosque' is a well-preserved example of Mughal architecture in Patuakhali.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Patuakhali district?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q4. [MCQ] The name 'Patuakhali' is believed to have originated from a popular folk song about a 'Patua' or painter.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Bir Shrestha Mohiuddin Jahangir, a hero of the Liberation War, is buried in Patuakhali.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (He is buried in Chapainawabganj).

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Kuakata Buddhist Vihara' contains a large statue of Gautama Buddha, which is one of the largest in the country.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Patuakhali was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Faridpur
B) Barisal (Bakerganj)
C) Khulna
D) Noakhali
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Barisal (Bakerganj)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is highly vulnerable to natural disasters like cyclones and tidal surges.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the science and technology university located in Patuakhali?
A) Kuakata University
B) Barisal Science and Technology University
C) Patuakhali Science and Technology University (PSTU)
D) Sagar Kanya University
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Patuakhali Science and Technology University (PSTU)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Patuakhali is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The 'Lebur Char' and 'Fatrar Char' are eco-tourism spots near Kuakata that are part of which forest?
A) Lawachara Forest
B) Bhawal Forest
C) The Sundarbans mangrove forest
D) Madhupur Forest
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Sundarbans mangrove forest

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Patuakhali district is more than 2 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Patuakhali District in square kilometers?
A) 2,550 sq km
B) 3,221 sq km
C) 3,890 sq km
D) 4,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 3,221 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The historic 'Masjid-e-Sirajuddowla' in Bauphal upazila was built in which century?
A) 16th Century
B) 17th Century
C) 18th Century
D) 19th Century
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 18th Century

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rakhine community first settled in the coastal areas of Patuakhali and Barguna after fleeing persecution in their native Arakan in the late 18th century.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Patuakhali subdivision established?
A) 1859
B) 1871
C) 1892
D) 1905
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1871

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Potheghata' massacre during the 1971 Liberation War took place in which upazila of Patuakhali?
A) Kalapara
B) Galachipa
C) Dumki
D) Bauphal
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bauphal

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Patuakhali district is part of the 'Meghna Estuarine Floodplain', characterized by a network of tidal rivers and low-lying chars.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The first Bachelor-level government college in the district, 'Patuakhali Government College', was established in which year?
A) 1947
B) 1957
C) 1967
D) 1972
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1957

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Payra Thermal Power Plant, a major energy project, is a joint venture between Bangladesh and South Korea.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It's a joint venture with China).
=== BARGUNA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Barguna is the southernmost district of which administrative division?
A) Khulna Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Barisal Division
D) Dhaka Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Barisal Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] A part of the Sundarbans mangrove forest is located within Barguna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the main economic activity for the people living in the coastal areas of Barguna?
A) Tea cultivation
B) Garment manufacturing
C) Salt production
D) Sea fishing
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sea fishing

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major river flowing through Barguna?
A) Jamuna
B) Teesta
C) Karnaphuli
D) Bishkhali
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bishkhali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Barguna is a district that is highly vulnerable to natural disasters like cyclones and tidal surges.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Shubho Shondha' sea beach is a popular local tourist spot in which upazila?
A) Barguna Sadar
B) Amtali
C) Taltali
D) Patharghata
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Taltali

Q7. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Barguna was a part of which greater district?
A) Khulna
B) Faridpur
C) Barisal
D) Patuakhali
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Patuakhali

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Barguna has direct railway connectivity with the rest of the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Taltali Eco-Park' is known for its scenic beauty and mangrove forests.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famous for producing high-quality mangoes.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Barguna established as a district?
A) 1969
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1990
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rakhine ethnic community has several settlements and historic pagodas in Barguna.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Barguna district?
A) 5
B) 6
C) 7
D) 8
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

Q4. [MCQ] The name 'Barguna' is believed to have originated from the name of a prominent timber merchant named 'Baragun'.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Baleshwar River forms the eastern boundary of Barguna district, separating it from Pirojpur.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Bibichini Shahi Mosque' is a historic Sultanate-era mosque located in which upazila?
A) Taltali
B) Betagi
C) Patharghata
D) Amtali
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Betagi

Q7. [MCQ] What is 'Hilsa,' a major product of Barguna, famous for?
A) Being the national bird of Bangladesh
B) Being the national fish of Bangladesh
C) Being a rare type of wood
D) Being a local handicraft
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Being the national fish of Bangladesh

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Barguna is one of the lowest in the Barisal division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Fatrar Char' is a large island and part of the Sundarbans located in which upazila?
A) Barguna Sadar
B) Patharghata
C) Taltali
D) Amtali
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Patharghata

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] There are no public universities or medical colleges located in Barguna district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic Bibichini Mosque is locally believed to have been built by a Persian princess. What was her name?
A) Pari Bibi
B) Jahanara Begum
C) Iran Dukht Rahmat Bibi (Bibichini)
D) Roshanara Begum
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Iran Dukht Rahmat Bibi (Bibichini)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Barguna district is less than 1 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Barguna District in square kilometers?
A) 1,520 sq km
B) 1,831 sq km
C) 2,150 sq km
D) 2,480 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,831 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The 1971 Liberation War massacre at Patharghata, where hundreds of civilians were killed by the Pakistani army, took place near the bank of which river?
A) Andharmanik
B) Payra
C) Bishkhali
D) Agunmukha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bishkhali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Barguna subdivision was created in 1969, at the same time Patuakhali was upgraded to a district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which upazila is the main fishing port of Barguna, one of the largest in the country, located?
A) Amtali
B) Taltali
C) Betagi
D) Patharghata
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Patharghata

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Charkhali-Tushkhali' ferry is a major crossing point over the Baleshwar river, connecting Barguna with which district?
A) Patuakhali
B) Jhalokati
C) Bagerhat
D) Pirojpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Pirojpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Barguna is part of the 'Tidal Mangrove Floodplain', which is characterized by very high salinity and is unsuitable for most crops without special management.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Sonakata Eco-Park' is located in which upazila?
A) Barguna Sadar
B) Patharghata
C) Taltali
D) Amtali
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Taltali

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The first elected chairman of the Barguna Zila Parishad was appointed before the year 2010.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The first election was held in 2016).

=== PANCHAGARH ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Panchagarh is famously known as the district located at which extreme point of Bangladesh?
A) Southernmost
B) Easternmost
C) Westernmost
D) Northernmost
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Northernmost

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Banglabandha Land Port, a major trade route with India, is located in Panchagarh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] In recent years, Panchagarh has become famous for the large-scale cultivation of what crop, previously uncommon in the region?
A) Jute
B) Tea
C) Cotton
D) Coffee
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Tea

Q4. [MCQ] Which major river flows through Panchagarh?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Jamuna
D) Karatoya
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Karatoya

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] From Tetulia in Panchagarh, it is possible to see the Kanchenjunga mountain range on a clear day.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Panchagarh is a district in which administrative division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Mymensingh Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rangpur Division

Q7. [MCQ] The "Zero Point" at the Banglabandha border signifies the starting point of the highway distance within Bangladesh.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Panchagarh is a coastal district bordering the Bay of Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district's name "Panchagarh" means what in Bengali?
A) Five Rivers
B) Five Villages
C) Five Forts
D) Five Markets
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Five Forts

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Panchagarh was part of the greater Rangpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Panchagarh officially established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1987
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Mirzapur Shahi Mosque' in Panchagarh is a well-preserved example of Mughal architecture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Panchagarh district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Panchagarh was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Rangpur
B) Bogra
C) Dinajpur
D) Thakurgaon
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dinajpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Banglabandha Land Port provides direct trade connectivity to Nepal and Bhutan through Indian territory.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The historic 'Maharaja's Dighi' (King's Pond) is located in which upazila of Panchagarh?
A) Panchagarh Sadar
B) Boda
C) Tetulia
D) Atwari
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Panchagarh Sadar

Q7. [MCQ] The soil and climate of Panchagarh are suitable for tea cultivation because they are similar to those of which Indian region?
A) Darjeeling
B) Assam
C) Kerala
D) Punjab
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Darjeeling

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Panchagarh is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Rocks Museum' at Panchagarh Government Women's College is unique for its collection of:
A) Ancient pottery
B) Fossils and ancient rocks
C) Terracotta plaques
D) Sultanate-era coins
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Fossils and ancient rocks

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Panchagarh is the only district in Bangladesh that is bordered by India on three sides.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The five 'garhs' (forts) after which Panchagarh is named are Bhitargarh, Hosaingarh, Mirgarh, Rajangarh, and which other?
A) Devengarh
B) Patangarh
C) Sitagarh
D) Kotagarh
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Devengarh

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Panchagarh district is more than 1.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Panchagarh District in square kilometers?
A) 1,150 sq km
B) 1,404 sq km
C) 1,680 sq km
D) 1,890 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,404 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The region of Panchagarh was historically part of which ancient kingdom?
A) Gauda
B) Vanga
C) Samatata
D) Kamarupa
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kamarupa

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Mahananda River, which forms a part of the border with India, originates in the Himalayas and flows through Panchagarh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Panchagarh subdivision established?
A) 1947
B) 1965
C) 1971
D) 1980
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 1980

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Kartowa Valley' geological formation in Panchagarh is known for its deposits of:
A) Coal
B) Limestone
C) Peat and gravel
D) Iron ore
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Peat and gravel

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, Panchagarh was the first area in the country to be declared a "free zone" by the Mukti Bahini.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic 'Golokdham Temple' in Panchagarh is dedicated to which Hindu deities?
A) Shiva
B) Kali
C) Durga
D) Radha-Krishna
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Radha-Krishna

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The tea industry in Panchagarh is dominated by large government-owned estates.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is primarily led by private small-scale and large-scale growers).
=== THAKURGAON ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Thakurgaon is a district located in the northwestern part of which division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Thakurgaon shares a border with the Indian state of West Bengal.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the main agricultural crop for which Thakurgaon is known?
A) Jute
B) Tea
C) Rice
D) Cotton
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rice

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Tangon' is a major river that flows through which district?
A) Panchagarh
B) Thakurgaon
C) Nilphamari
D) Lalmonirhat
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Thakurgaon

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Thakurgaon Sugar Mill is one of the largest and oldest in the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The traditional folk music genre 'Bhawaiya' is popular in which region of Bangladesh?
A) Chittagong
B) Sylhet
C) Greater Rangpur (including Thakurgaon)
D) Barisal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Greater Rangpur (including Thakurgaon)

Q7. [MCQ] The district was named after a respected local figure with the title 'Thakur'.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Thakurgaon was part of the greater Bogra district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous historical landmark in Thakurgaon?
A) Kantajew Temple
B) Ranishankail Zamindar Bari
C) Tajhat Palace
D) Puthia Palace
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ranishankail Zamindar Bari

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Thakurgaon is directly connected to Dhaka by air.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The nearest airport is in Saidpur).
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Thakurgaon established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1989
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Mirza Fakhrul Islam Alamgir, a prominent politician and secretary-general of the BNP, hails from Thakurgaon.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Thakurgaon district?
A) 5
B) 6
C) 7
D) 8
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 5

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Thakurgaon was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Rangpur
B) Pabna
C) Dinajpur
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dinajpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Jamalpur Zamindar Bari Mosque' in Thakurgaon is a well-preserved example of Mughal architecture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The famous 'Nek Mardan' fair and shrine is located in which upazila?
A) Thakurgaon Sadar
B) Baliadangi
C) Ranishankail
D) Pirganj
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ranishankail

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the ancient, massive Banyan tree, a popular tourist spot in Baliadangi upazila?
A) Shahjalal's Banyan Tree
B) Suryapuri Aamgach (Mango Tree)
C) Jorpakhuri Banyan Tree
D) It is not a Banyan tree.
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jorpakhuri Banyan Tree

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Thakurgaon district is significantly higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The district has a significant population of which ethnic minority group?
A) Chakma
B) Garo
C) Santal and Oraon
D) Marma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Santal and Oraon

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Thakurgaon has direct railway connectivity.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The original name of the Thakurgaon subdivision, when it was established, was:
A) Nishchintapur
B) Gobindanagar
C) Ranishankail
D) It was always Thakurgaon.
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Gobindanagar

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Thakurgaon is less than that of the neighboring Panchagarh district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Thakurgaon District in square kilometers?
A) 1,550 sq km
B) 1,809 sq km
C) 2,130 sq km
D) 2,450 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,809 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The historic 'Gorokshonath Temple and Well' is an archaeological site believed to be from which period?
A) Pre-Mughal Sultanate
B) Pala or Sena Dynasty
C) British Period
D) Gupta Period
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Pala or Sena Dynasty

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Thakurgaon is part of the 'Himalayan Piedmont Plain', which is characterized by sandy loams and is excellent for rice cultivation.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Thakurgaon subdivision established?
A) 1860
B) 1883
C) 1905
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1860

Q7. [MCQ] The freedom fighter and one of the accused in the Agartala Conspiracy Case, Sergeant Zahurul Haq, was born in which district?
A) Thakurgaon
B) Noakhali
C) Barisal
D) Comilla
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Noakhali

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, Thakurgaon was liberated from Pakistani forces in the last week of November.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was liberated in early December).

Q9. [MCQ] The Ranishankail Zamindar family, who built the palace, belonged to which religion?
A) Islam
B) Buddhism
C) Christianity
D) Hinduism
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Hinduism

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Thakurgaon is one of the leading wheat-producing districts in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== NILPHAMARI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Nilphamari is a district in the northern part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Nilphamari' is associated with the historical cultivation of indigo (Nil).
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Saidpur Railway Workshop, the largest in Bangladesh, is located in which district?
A) Lalmonirhat
B) Dinajpur
C) Nilphamari
D) Gaibandha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nilphamari

Q4. [MCQ] Which major river flows along the eastern border of Nilphamari?
A) Jamuna
B) Teesta
C) Padma
D) Karatoya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Teesta

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Uttara Export Processing Zone (EPZ) is a major industrial area located in Nilphamari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Nilsagar' is a large, historic water tank (dighi) located in which district?
A) Rangpur
B) Nilphamari
C) Dinajpur
D) Panchagarh
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nilphamari

Q7. [MCQ] Saidpur is a town in Nilphamari known for its significant population of which community?
A) Garo
B) Santal
C) Chakma
D) Urdu-speaking community (Biharis)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Urdu-speaking community (Biharis)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Nilphamari shares a direct land border with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Asaduzzaman Noor, a famous actor and politician, hails from which district?
A) Thakurgaon
B) Kurigram
C) Nilphamari
D) Mymensingh
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nilphamari

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The main airport serving the region, Saidpur Airport, is located in Nilphamari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Nilphamari established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Chini Mosque' in Saidpur is famous for its unique construction using pieces of chinaware.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Nilphamari district?
A) 4
B) 6
C) 8
D) 10
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 6

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Nilphamari was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Dinajpur
B) Bogra
C) Cooch Behar
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rangpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Teesta Barrage, a major irrigation project, is located within Nilphamari district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is in Lalmonirhat).

Q6. [MCQ] The historic name of Nilsagar was 'Birat Dighi' and it is associated with which mythological king?
A) King Harishchandra
B) King Sitaram
C) Raja Birat
D) Raja Lakshman Sen
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Raja Birat

Q7. [MCQ] Saidpur town was established and grew around which major industry in the 19th century?
A) Jute processing
B) Indigo plantation
C) Railway engineering
D) Tea packaging
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Railway engineering

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Nilphamari is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Dharmapal Garh' is an archaeological site associated with which ancient ruling dynasty?
A) The Sena Dynasty
B) The Pala Dynasty
C) The Gupta Dynasty
D) The Maurya Dynasty
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Pala Dynasty

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Nilphamari is part of the Teesta Meander Floodplain, which is very fertile for agriculture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Saidpur Railway Workshop was established by the Assam Bengal Railway in which year?
A) 1857
B) 1870
C) 1895
D) 1901
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1870

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Nilphamari is over 2 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Nilphamari District in square kilometers?
A) 1,250 sq km
B) 1,547 sq km
C) 1,780 sq km
D) 1,990 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,547 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Indigo Revolt of 1859-60, a major peasant uprising against British planters, had a significant impact on which upazila of Nilphamari?
A) Jaldhaka
B) Dimla
C) Kishoreganj
D) Domar
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Jaldhaka

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The construction of the Chini Mosque in Saidpur was initiated by a local landlord who was inspired by the architecture of Kolkata's Nakhoda Mosque.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (He was inspired by the Star Mosque in Dhaka and used broken crockery).

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Nilphamari subdivision established?
A) 1857
B) 1875
C) 1895
D) 1921
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1875

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Kunda Pukur Mazar' is a historic shrine in Nilphamari Sadar dedicated to a Sufi saint from which country?
A) Iran
B) Turkey
C) Yemen
D) Iraq
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Iraq

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War, the killing of Golam Gafur, the station master of Saidpur, was one of the first major acts of violence by the Pakistani army in the region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Jamuneshwari River, which flows through Nilphamari, is a distributary of which larger river?
A) Brahmaputra
B) Karatoya
C) Teesta
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Teesta

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Uttara EPZ in Nilphamari is particularly known for producing wigs and other hair products for export.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== LALMONIRHAT ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Lalmonirhat is a district in the northern part of which division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Teesta Barrage, the largest irrigation project in Bangladesh, is located in Lalmonirhat.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the major river that flows through Lalmonirhat, on which the Teesta Barrage is built?
A) Jamuna
B) Dharla
C) Teesta
D) Padma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Teesta

Q4. [MCQ] The Burimari Land Port provides a major trade link between Bangladesh and which country?
A) Nepal
B) Bhutan
C) Myanmar
D) India
CORRECT ANSWER: D) India

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Lalmonirhat is a major tea-producing district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The town of Lalmonirhat is known for its history as a major:
A) River port
B) University town
C) Railway town
D) Textile center
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Railway town

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product of Lalmonirhat?
A) Cotton
B) Tobacco and Maize
C) Sugarcane
D) Coffee
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Tobacco and Maize

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Lalmonirhat was a part of the greater Dinajpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Tin Bigha Corridor' is an strip of Indian land that connects a Bangladeshi enclave. This corridor is located near which land port?
A) Hili
B) Benapole
C) Tamabil
D) Patgram (near Burimari)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Patgram (near Burimari)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters of Lalmonirhat is a town named Patgram.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Lalmonirhat established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Kakina Zamindar Bari' is a well-known landmark in the Kaliganj upazila of Lalmonirhat.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Lalmonirhat district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Lalmonirhat was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Dinajpur
B) Bogra
C) Cooch Behar
D) Rangpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rangpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During World War II, a military airfield was built by the British in Lalmonirhat, which is still in use by the Bangladesh Air Force.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Tebhaga Movement', a significant peasant uprising demanding a two-thirds share of the harvest, had a strong presence in which upazila of Lalmonirhat?
A) Lalmonirhat Sadar
B) Hatibandha
C) Kaliganj
D) Aditmari
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Hatibandha

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Dahagram-Angarpota' are famous Bangladeshi enclaves that were connected to the mainland via which corridor?
A) Tin Bigha Corridor
B) Fulbari Corridor
C) Siliguri Corridor
D) Tetulia Corridor
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Tin Bigha Corridor

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Lalmonirhat district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Sheikh Reazuddin Ahmed, a notable writer and journalist of the Bengal Renaissance, hailed from which upazila?
A) Patgram
B) Kaliganj
C) Lalmonirhat Sadar
D) Aditmari
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Kaliganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Lalmonirhat is part of the Teesta Meander Floodplain, which is highly fertile due to silt deposits.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The name 'Lalmonirhat' is believed to have originated from a woman named Lalmoni who sold her land to the railway, combined with 'hat' (market).
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Lalmonirhat is greater than the population of the neighboring Nilphamari district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Lalmonirhat District in square kilometers?
A) 1,020 sq km
B) 1,247 sq km
C) 1,450 sq km
D) 1,680 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,247 sq km

A) Hatibandha
B) Aditmari
C) Patgram
D) Kaliganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kaliganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Lalmonirhat subdivision was established in the year 1979.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Saniajan' is another major river that flows through which upazila, often causing floods?
A) Lalmonirhat Sadar
B) Kaliganj
C) Hatibandha
D) Patgram
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Hatibandha

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Nidaria Mosque' in Aditmari is a historic mosque built in which century?
A) 16th century
B) 17th century
C) 18th century
D) 19th century
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 18th century

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Teesta Barrage project was primarily funded by the World Bank and the Asian Development Bank.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was primarily funded by the Government of Bangladesh).

Q9. [MCQ] Historically, the region of Lalmonirhat was part of which ancient kingdom's territory?
A) Pundra
B) Vanga
C) Kamarupa
D) Samatata
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kamarupa

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Lalmonirhat was liberated from Pakistani forces on December 6, 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== KURIGRAM ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Kurigram is a district in the northernmost part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Rajshahi Division
C) Sylhet Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is known for having a very large number of 'chars' or river islands.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which major river enters Bangladesh from India through Kurigram district?
A) Padma
B) Meghna
C) Brahmaputra (Jamuna)
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Brahmaputra (Jamuna)

Q4. [MCQ] The Chilmari River Port, a historically important port, is located in which district?
A) Gaibandha
B) Lalmonirhat
C) Kurigram
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kurigram

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Kurigram is one of the wealthiest districts in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main livelihood for the people living on the 'chars' of Kurigram?
A) Tourism
B) Heavy industry
C) Agriculture and fishing
D) Tea cultivation
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Agriculture and fishing

Q7. [MCQ] The district shares a border with which two states of India?
A) West Bengal and Meghalaya
B) West Bengal and Assam
C) Tripura and Mizoram
D) Assam and Meghalaya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) West Bengal and Assam

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous folk singer Abbasuddin Ahmed was born in Kurigram.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (He was born in Cooch Behar).

Q9. [MCQ] Besides the Brahmaputra, which other major river flows through Kurigram?
A) Karnaphuli
B) Surma
C) Dharla
D) Rupsha
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dharla

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters is a town also named Kurigram.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Kurigram established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, the Rowmari area of Kurigram remained a liberated zone throughout the war.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Kurigram district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Kurigram was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Dinajpur
B) Bogra
C) Rangpur
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous writer Syed Shamsul Haq had his ancestral home in Kurigram.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Chandamari Mosque' is a historic mosque located in which upazila of Kurigram?
A) Kurigram Sadar
B) Rajarhat
C) Nageshwari
D) Bhurungamari
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rajarhat

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Bangasonaihat Bridge' is a newly constructed bridge over which river, improving connectivity in the region?
A) Teesta
B) Brahmaputra
C) Jamuna
D) Dudhkumar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Dudhkumar

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Kurigram is one of the lowest in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The "Bhawaiya Academy" in Kurigram was established to promote what?
A) Modern art
B) Local folk music
C) Ethnic minority languages
D) The weaving industry
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Local folk music

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Kurigram' is believed to have come from the 'Kuri' (twenty) families of the 'Mali' (gardener) caste who first settled there.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q1. [MCQ] The historic Chilmari River Port was once a major hub for exporting which commodity to Calcutta?

B) 1875

D) Tripura
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Assam
