=== GAIBANDHA ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Gaibandha is a district in the northern part of Bangladesh, belonging to which division?
A) Rajshahi Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Rangpur Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangpur Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Jamuna (Brahmaputra) River flows along the eastern border of Gaibandha.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The district is known for having many river islands, which are locally called what?
A) Haors
B) Beels
C) Tillas
D) Chars
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chars

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural crop in Gaibandha?
A) Tea
B) Jute and Paddy
C) Coffee
D) Cotton
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jute and Paddy

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Gobindaganj' upazila is an important commercial center located on the Dhaka-Rangpur highway.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the name of the historic palace located in Gobindaganj?
A) Tajhat Palace
B) Baliati Palace
C) Bardhan Kuthi
D) Puthia Palace
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Bardhan Kuthi

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Balashi Ghat' is a major river terminal that connects Gaibandha with which other district by ferry?
A) Sirajganj
B) Pabna
C) Jamalpur
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jamalpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Gaibandha was part of the greater Dinajpur district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Gaibandha has a significant population of which ethnic minority group?
A) Chakma
B) Garo
C) Santal
D) Marma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Santal

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famous for its large-scale salt production.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Gaibandha established as a district?
A) 1972
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1987
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Santal Rebellion' of 1855 against the British and zamindars took place partly in areas that are now in Gaibandha.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Gaibandha district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Gaibandha was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Bogra
B) Rangpur
C) Dinajpur
D) Pabna
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Rangpur

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Masta Mosque' in Gobindaganj is a well-preserved example of Sultanate-era architecture.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Trimohini Ghat' is the confluence of which three rivers?
A) Teesta, Dharla, Dudhkumar
B) Jamuna, Teesta, Karatoya
C) Padma, Meghna, Dakatia
D) It is not a river confluence.
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jamuna, Teesta, Karatoya

Q7. [MCQ] Shah Abdul Hamid, the first Speaker of the Pakistan National Assembly, hailed from which upazila of Gaibandha?
A) Gaibandha Sadar
B) Gobindaganj
C) Palashbari
D) Sundarganj
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Gobindaganj

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Gaibandha district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The Bonarpara Railway Junction is an important communication hub in which upazila?
A) Saghata
B) Fulchhari
C) Gobindaganj
D) Palashbari
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Saghata

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Gaibandha' is believed to have originated from a place where the royal cows ('Gai') of the Raja of Virat were tied up ('Bandha').
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The 'Bardhan Kuthi', the seat of the Raja of Bardhan, dates back to which historical period?
A) Mughal Period
B) British Period
C) Pre-Mughal, Hindu Kingdom Period
D) Pala Period
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pre-Mughal, Hindu Kingdom Period

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Gaibandha is over 2.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Gaibandha District in square kilometers?
A) 1,850 sq km
B) 2,179 sq km
C) 2,450 sq km
D) 2,780 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,179 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Purno Chandra Sing, a leader of the Santal community, played a vital role in organizing the 'Hul' (rebellion) in which part of Gaibandha?
A) Sundarganj
B) Palashbari
C) Gobindaganj
D) Saghata
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Gobindaganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Gaibandha is part of both the Teesta Meander Floodplain and the Karatoya-Bangali Floodplain, making it extremely fertile but prone to flooding.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Gaibandha subdivision established?
A) 1857
B) 1875
C) 1895
D) 1910
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1875

Q7. [MCQ] During the Liberation War, the 'Battle of Rangamati' was a major operation carried out by freedom fighters in which upazila?
A) Gobindaganj
B) Phulchhari
C) Palashbari
D) Saghata
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Phulchhari

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Gaibandha has one of the highest rates of riverbank erosion in Bangladesh, leading to significant displacement of people annually.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Tulushighat, a village in Gaibandha, became a notable center for which anti-British movement in the 1920s and 30s?
A) The Swadeshi Movement
B) The Khilafat Movement
C) The Non-cooperation Movement
D) The Tebhaga Movement
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Non-cooperation Movement

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Jamuna Char Integrated Development Project' is a government initiative specifically targeting the socio-economic improvement of the river-island communities in Gaibandha.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== JOYPURHAT ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Joypurhat is a district located in which administrative division?
A) Rangpur Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Joypurhat is well-known for being one of the major sugar-producing zones in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the main mineral resource found in large deposits deep underground in Joypurhat?
A) Iron Ore
B) Gold
C) Limestone and Coal
D) Natural Gas
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Limestone and Coal

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Joypurhat Sugar Mill' is one of the largest in the country.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Joypurhat shares a long international border with the country of Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main river flowing through Joypurhat district?
A) Padma
B) Jamuna
C) Little Jamuna (Chhoto Jamuna)
D) Teesta
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Little Jamuna (Chhoto Jamuna)

Q7. [MCQ] The district is located in which geographical part of Bangladesh?
A) Southeast
B) Southwest
C) Northeast
D) Northwest
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Northwest

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Joypurhat was a part of the greater Rajshahi district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The historic 'Lokma Rajbari' is a well-known landmark in which upazila?
A) Joypurhat Sadar
B) Panchbibi
C) Kalai
D) Khetlal
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Panchbibi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters is a town also named Joypurhat.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Joypurhat established as a district?
A) 1978
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1986
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Tebhaga Movement', a significant peasant uprising, had a strong presence in the Joypurhat region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Joypurhat district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Joypurhat was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Rangpur
B) Dinajpur
C) Naogaon
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bogra

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Hinda-Kasba Shahi Mosque' is a historic mosque from the Sultanate period located in Khetlal upazila.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The coal and limestone deposits in Jamalganj are notable for being:
A) The largest open-pit mines in Asia
B) Easily accessible near the surface
C) Located at a very great depth, making extraction difficult
D) Already fully extracted
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Located at a very great depth, making extraction difficult

Q7. [MCQ] The economy of Joypurhat is primarily based on:
A) Tourism
B) Heavy industry
C) Agriculture and agro-based industries
D) Information Technology
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Agriculture and agro-based industries

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Joypurhat' is believed to have originated from a victory ('Joy') of a Pala dynasty king.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Aas-Ranga Dighi' is a large historic water tank located in which upazila?
A) Akkelpur
B) Kalai
C) Panchbibi
D) Khetlal
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Panchbibi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Joypurhat district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The famous Tebhaga movement leader in the Joypurhat region was a female activist named:
A) Pritilata Waddedar
B) Ila Mitra
C) Moni Singh
D) Jasoda Rani Sarkar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jasoda Rani Sarkar

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Joypurhat is less than one million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

A) 750 sq km
B) 965 sq km
C) 1,120 sq km

CORRECT ANSWER: B) 965 sq km

A) 1884
B) 1905
C) 1920
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1920

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Joypurhat is part of the Barind Tract, which is an elevated Pleistocene terrace characterized by reddish and yellowish clay soils.

A) Panchbibi
B) Joypurhat Sadar

D) Kalai
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Joypurhat Sadar

A) Maurya and Gupta periods
B) Mughal period
C) British period
D) Sultanate period

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Joypurhat has the highest per capita potato production in Bangladesh.

A) Khetlal

D) Akkelpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Panchbibi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Joypurhat was the last district to be established within the Rajshahi Division in 1984.

=== NAOGAON ===

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Naogaon shares a direct land border with the country of India.

Q9. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Naogaon was a part of which greater district?
A) Pabna
B) Bogra
C) Dinajpur
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters is a town also named Naogaon.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Naogaon established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Somapura Mahavihara at Paharpur was built by the Pala king Dharmapala in the 8th century.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Naogaon district?
A) 9
B) 11
C) 13
D) 15
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 11

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Patisar Kuthibari', a zamindari estate office of Rabindranath Tagore, is located in which upazila of Naogaon?
A) Manda
B) Niamatpur
C) Atrai
D) Raninagar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Atrai

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kusumba Mosque was built during the reign of the Mughal emperor Akbar.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was built during the Suri period).

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Jagaddal Vihara', another significant Buddhist monastery, was founded by which Pala king?
A) Dharmapala
B) Devapala
C) Mahipala
D) Ramapala
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Ramapala

Q7. [MCQ] The district has a large population of which ethnic minority groups?
A) Garo and Hajong
B) Chakma and Marma
C) Santal, Oraon, and Munda
D) Khasi and Manipuri
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Santal, Oraon, and Munda

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Naogaon district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Mohammad Baitullah, the first Deputy Speaker of the Jatiya Sangsad of Bangladesh, hailed from which district?
A) Rajshahi
B) Natore
C) Naogaon
D) Bogra
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Naogaon

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Naogaon' is said to have originated from the combination of 'Nau' (nine) and 'Gaon' (village).
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was the Somapura Mahavihara at Paharpur inscribed as a UNESCO World Heritage Site?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1985
D) 1990
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1985

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, Naogaon has a larger population than the neighboring Rajshahi district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Naogaon District in square kilometers?
A) 2,980 sq km
B) 3,150 sq km
C) 3,435 sq km
D) 3,890 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3,435 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Kusumba Mosque was built by a high-ranking official named Sulaiman during the reign of which Suri sultan?
A) Sher Shah Suri
B) Islam Shah Suri
C) Adil Shah Suri
D) Ghiyasuddin Bahadur Shah
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Ghiyasuddin Bahadur Shah

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in the western part of Naogaon is part of the Barind Tract, making it less fertile and more drought-prone than the eastern alluvial plains of the Atrai river.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Naogaon subdivision established?
A) 1860
B) 1877
C) 1905
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1877

Q7. [MCQ] Rabindranath Tagore received the Nobel Prize for Literature while he was managing his family estates, including Patisar. A significant portion of the prize money was used to establish what in the area?
A) A school
B) A hospital
C) An agricultural cooperative bank
D) A library
CORRECT ANSWER: C) An agricultural cooperative bank

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War, the Pakistani army established their largest camp in the district at the Patisar Kuthibari.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (Their camp was at the Naogaon Government College).

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Dibya pillar', a black stone pillar, is associated with the victory of which Kaivarta chief over the Pala rulers?
A) Bhima
B) Divya
C) Rudraka
D) It is not in Naogaon.
CORRECT ANSWER: D) It is not in Naogaon (It is in Dinajpur).

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Naogaon is the largest rice-producing district in the Rajshahi Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== NATORE ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Natore is a district in the northern part of which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Khulna Division
C) Rajshahi Division
D) Rangpur Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Natore is famous for its historic palace, the Natore Rajbari, the residence of Rani Bhabani.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] A famous sweet delicacy made from chhena (cottage cheese), for which Natore is renowned, is called:
A) Roshmalai
B) Monda
C) Chomchom
D) Kachagolla
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kachagolla

Q4. [MCQ] The vast wetland area known as Chalan Beel, the largest in Bangladesh, covers a large part of which district?
A) Bogra
B) Naogaon
C) Pabna and Natore
D) Sirajganj
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Pabna and Natore

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Dighapatia Rajbari, which now serves as the Uttara Ganabhaban, is located in Natore.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Who was the famous queen of the Natore zamindari estate, known for her philanthropy and efficient administration?
A) Rani Lakshmibai
B) Rani Padmini
C) Rani Bhabani
D) Rani Durgavati
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rani Bhabani

Q7. [MCQ] The Uttara Ganabhaban serves as the official northern residence for which head of state?
A) The Prime Minister of Bangladesh
B) The President of Bangladesh
C) The Chief Justice of Bangladesh
D) The Speaker of the Parliament
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The President of Bangladesh

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Natore was a part of the greater Bogra district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] What is the main river that flows through Natore?
A) Jamuna
B) Padma
C) Teesta
D) Atrai
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Atrai

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Natore has a direct railway connection.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Natore established as a district?
A) 1972
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1987
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Rani Bhabani was a contemporary of Nawab Siraj ud-Daulah and was known for her support of the British.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (She was known for her shrewdness and managed her estate after the Battle of Plassey).

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Natore district?
A) 6
B) 7
C) 8
D) 9
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Natore was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Pabna
B) Bogra
C) Kushtia
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Chalan Beel Museum' is dedicated to preserving the history and biodiversity of the region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Sir Jadunath Sarkar, one of the most eminent historians of Mughal India, was born in which upazila of Natore?
A) Natore Sadar
B) Singra
C) Gurudaspur
D) Baraigram
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Singra

Q7. [MCQ] What is the primary ingredient of Natore's famous Kachagolla?
A) Flour and sugar
B) Only chhena (cottage cheese)
C) Semolina and coconut
D) Milk solids (kheer)
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Only chhena (cottage cheese)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Natore district is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Halti Beel' is another large wetland located primarily in which upazila of Natore?
A) Lalpur
B) Gurudaspur
C) Bagatipara
D) Naldanga
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Naldanga

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Natore Sugar Mill is the first and oldest sugar mill in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It's not the first).
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year did Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman officially declare the Dighapatia Rajbari as the 'Uttara Ganabhaban'?
A) 1969
B) 1971
C) 1972
D) 1975
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1972

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to legend, the sweet 'Kachagolla' was invented accidentally when a confectioner's chhena couldn't be processed into sandesh, and he sold the raw sweetened chhena instead.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Natore District in square kilometers?
A) 1,550 sq km
B) 1,900 sq km
C) 2,130 sq km
D) 2,450 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,900 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Rani Bhabani became the zamindar of the vast Rajshahi estate after her husband, Raja Ramkanta Roy, died shortly after which historic event?
A) The Great Bengal Famine of 1770
B) The Battle of Plassey (1757)
C) The arrival of the British
D) The Maratha invasions
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Battle of Plassey (1757)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Natore' is believed to have originated from a combination of the words 'Nao' (boat) and 'Thar' (stop), meaning a place where boats stopped.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Natore subdivision established?
A) 1845
B) 1869
C) 1882
D) 1905
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1845

Q7. [MCQ] During the Liberation War of 1971, the massacre at the North Bengal Sugar Mill was a tragic event that took place in which upazila?
A) Singra
B) Natore Sadar
C) Lalpur
D) Baraigram
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Lalpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The architecture of the Dighapatia Rajbari (Uttara Ganabhaban) is heavily influenced by the Neoclassical style of European palaces.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Shahid Sagar' is a memorial pond in Natore Sadar commemorating the freedom fighters who were killed by the Pakistani army and thrown into it.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, Natore district has a higher population density than the neighboring Naogaon district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

=== CHAPAINAWABGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Chapainawabganj is a district in which administrative division of Bangladesh?
A) Rangpur Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Rajshahi Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famously known as the "Mango Capital" of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The historic Choto Sona Mosque (Small Golden Mosque) is a major tourist attraction in which district?
A) Bogra
B) Naogaon
C) Chapainawabganj
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chapainawabganj

Q4. [MCQ] Which major river, known as the Ganges in India, flows through Chapainawabganj?
A) Jamuna
B) Teesta
C) Meghna
D) Padma
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Padma

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The folk music and drama form known as "Gombhira" is a famous cultural tradition of this district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Sona Masjid Land Port is a major trade point between Bangladesh and which country?
A) Myanmar
B) Nepal
C) India
D) Bhutan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) India

Q7. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Chapainawabganj was a subdivision of which greater district?
A) Pabna
B) Bogra
C) Rajshahi
D) Dinajpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rajshahi

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bir Shrestha Mohiuddin Jahangir, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, is buried in Chapainawabganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is another major river flowing through the district?
A) Karatoya
B) Atrai
C) Mahananda
D) Tulsiganga
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Mahananda

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters was previously known as Nawabganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Chapainawabganj established as a district?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic 'Nachole Uprising' of 1949 was a peasant movement of the Santal community against the zamindari system.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Chapainawabganj district?
A) 4
B) 5
C) 6
D) 7
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 5

Q4. [MCQ] Ila Mitra, a communist leader and a key figure in the Nachole Uprising, is famously known by what title?
A) Agnikanya (Daughter of Fire)
B) Rani Maa (Queen Mother)
C) Nacholer Rani (Queen of Nachole)
D) Desh Konna (Daughter of the Nation)
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Nacholer Rani (Queen of Nachole)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Darasbari Mosque' is another historic mosque built during the Sultanate period, located near the Choto Sona Mosque.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which of these is a famous variety of mango for which Chapainawabganj is renowned?
A) Amrapali
B) Langra and Fazli
C) Rupali
D) Himsagar
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Langra and Fazli

Q7. [MCQ] Bir Shrestha Mohiuddin Jahangir was killed in action during which battle of the 1971 Liberation War?
A) Battle of Kamalpur
B) Battle of Belonia
C) Battle of Chapainawabganj
D) Battle of Hilli
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Battle of Chapainawabganj

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The ancient city of Gauda, a capital of Bengal, was located in an area that is now partly in Chapainawabganj and partly in India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Tahkhana Complex', containing a mosque and a tomb, was built by which Mughal governor?
A) Shaista Khan
B) Mir Jumla
C) Shah Shuja
D) Islam Khan
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Shah Shuja

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Chapainawabganj is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Choto Sona Mosque was built during the reign of which Sultan of Bengal?
A) Ghiyasuddin Azam Shah
B) Shamsuddin Ilyas Shah
C) Alauddin Husain Shah
D) Nasiruddin Nasrat Shah
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Alauddin Husain Shah

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Chapainawabganj is over 2 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Chapainawabganj District in square kilometers?
A) 1,350 sq km
B) 1,702 sq km
C) 1,980 sq km
D) 2,140 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1,702 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Gombhira' performance traditionally involves two main characters, a grandfather and his grandson, who discuss social and political issues through song and dialogue. What are these characters called?
A) Nana-Nati
B) Dada-Nati
C) Bura-Chhokra
D) Ustad-Shagred
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Nana-Nati

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Chapainawabganj is primarily part of the Barind Tract, a Pleistocene-era terrace, which is ideal for mango cultivation due to its well-drained, slightly acidic nature.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The original name of the Chapainawabganj subdivision, when it was established under Malda district in 1899, was:
A) Shibganj
B) Gauda
C) Ramchandrapur
D) Nawabganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Nawabganj

Q7. [MCQ] During the British period, the main administrative and commercial center of the region was:
A) Shibganj
B) Malda (now in India)
C) Godagari
D) Rajshahi
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Malda (now in India)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Kansat' mango market in Shibganj upazila is the largest wholesale mango market in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The historic 'Rajbibi Mosque' is architecturally similar to which other famous mosque in the Gauda region?
A) Kusumba Mosque
B) Bagha Mosque
C) Darasbari Mosque
D) Shait Gumbad Mosque
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Darasbari Mosque

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district was renamed from Nawabganj to Chapainawabganj to avoid confusion with another Nawabganj district (now Dinajpur).
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was to avoid confusion with Nawabganj upazila near Dhaka).
=== HABIGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Habiganj is a district in the northeastern part of Bangladesh, belonging to which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Mymensingh Division
D) Sylhet Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sylhet Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is very famous for its large number of tea gardens.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows through Habiganj town?
A) Surma
B) Kushiara
C) Khowai
D) Manu
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khowai

Q4. [MCQ] The Habiganj Gas Field is one of the largest natural gas fields in Bangladesh.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Habiganj shares a border with the Indian state of Meghalaya.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] The Rema-Kalenga Wildlife Sanctuary is a protected forest area located in which district?
A) Moulvibazar
B) Habiganj
C) Sunamganj
D) Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Habiganj

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural crop of Habiganj, besides tea?
A) Jute
B) Cotton
C) Rice
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rice

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Habiganj was a subdivision under the greater Comilla district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The historic village of Baniyachong in Habiganj is famous for being what?
A) The smallest village in Asia
B) The largest village in Asia
C) The oldest village in Bangladesh
D) The highest village in Bangladesh
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The largest village in Asia

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters is a town also named Habiganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Habiganj established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1989
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Habiganj was a subdivision of the greater Sylhet district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Habiganj district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q4. [MCQ] During the 1971 Liberation War, the historic meeting of the sector commanders of the Mukti Bahini, where the command structure was formalized, took place at which tea garden in Habiganj?
A) Rashidpur Tea Garden
B) Teliapara Tea Garden
C) Laskarpur Tea Garden
D) Surma Tea Garden
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Teliapara Tea Garden

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Rema-Kalenga Wildlife Sanctuary is a tropical evergreen forest, distinct from the mangrove forests of the Sundarbans.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The great medieval poet Syed Sultan, author of "Nabibangsha," was born in which upazila of Habiganj?
A) Habiganj Sadar
B) Lakhai
C) Madhabpur
D) Nabiganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Nabiganj

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Shankor Pasha Shahi Mosque' is a well-preserved example of which architectural style?
A) Mughal
B) British Colonial
C) Sultanate
D) Modern
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sultanate

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Habiganj is one of the lowest in the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Bibiyana' gas field, one of the largest in the country, is partly located in which upazila of Habiganj?
A) Chunarughat
B) Nabiganj
C) Bahubal
D) Baniachang
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Nabiganj

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name Habiganj was derived from a market ('ganj') established by a zamindar named Habib Ullah.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic village of Baniyachong was the capital of which ancient kingdom?
A) Kamarupa Kingdom
B) Gaur Kingdom
C) Samatata Kingdom
D) Laud Kingdom
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Laud Kingdom

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Habiganj is less than 2.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Habiganj District in square kilometers?
A) 2,150 sq km
B) 2,636 sq km
C) 2,980 sq km
D) 3,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,636 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The memorial at Teliapara Tea Garden was built to commemorate the meeting of Mukti Bahini officers that took place on which date in 1971?
A) March 26
B) April 4
C) April 17
D) May 10
CORRECT ANSWER: B) April 4

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Habiganj district shares its international border with the Indian state of Tripura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Hemango Biswas, a famous Bengali folk singer and composer associated with the Indian People's Theatre Association (IPTA), was born in which upazila?
A) Habiganj Sadar
B) Chunarughat
C) Nabiganj
D) Baniachang
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Habiganj Sadar

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Satchari National Park', another protected forest area, is located in which upazila of Habiganj?
A) Madhabpur
B) Bahubal
C) Nabiganj
D) Chunarughat
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chunarughat

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Habiganj subdivision was established during the British Raj in 1874.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a prominent ethnic minority group residing in the hilly areas of Habiganj?
A) Santal
B) Marma
C) Tripura
D) Rakhine
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tripura

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Rashidpur' gas field in Habiganj was the first gas field to be discovered in the then East Pakistan.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (The first was at Haripur, Sylhet).
=== MOULVIBAZAR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Moulvibazar is a district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Chittagong Division
C) Sylhet Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sylhet Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famously known as the "Tea Capital" of Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Lawachara National Park, a famous tropical forest, is located in which upazila of Moulvibazar?
A) Sreemangal
B) Kulaura
C) Kamalganj
D) Juri
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Kamalganj

Q4. [MCQ] The town of Sreemangal is famous for being the center of what industry in Bangladesh?
A) Jute
B) Leather
C) Tea
D) Sugar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Tea

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Madhabkunda waterfall, a major tourist attraction, is located in Moulvibazar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which ethnic minority group, known for its unique culture and handloom weaving, has a large presence in Moulvibazar?
A) Chakma
B) Santal
C) Manipuri
D) Marma
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Manipuri

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main river flowing through Moulvibazar district?
A) Surma
B) Kushiara
C) Khowai
D) Manu
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Manu

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Moulvibazar was a part of the greater Comilla district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Hakaluki Haor, one of the largest wetlands in Bangladesh, is partly located in which district?
A) Sunamganj
B) Habiganj
C) Kishoreganj
D) Moulvibazar
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Moulvibazar

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district shares a border with the Indian state of Tripura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Moulvibazar established as a district?
A) 1972
B) 1980
C) 1984
D) 1990
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Bangladesh Tea Research Institute (BTRI), the main hub for tea-related research, is located in Sreemangal.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Moulvibazar district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Moulvibazar was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Comilla
B) Noakhali
C) Habiganj
D) Sylhet
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sylhet

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Ham Ham waterfall is another popular tourist destination located deep inside the forests of Moulvibazar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which of the following is another significant ethnic minority group living in the tea garden areas?
A) Munda
B) Oraon
C) Khasi
D) Bhil
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khasi

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Baikka Beel' is a famous wetland sanctuary, particularly known for what?
A) Migratory birds
B) Crocodiles
C) Royal Bengal Tigers
D) Elephants
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Migratory birds

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Moulvibazar is lower than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Manipuri Raas Leela' is a famous cultural festival celebrated by which community in Moulvibazar?
A) The Khasi community
B) The Tripura community
C) The Manipuri community
D) The Garo community
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Manipuri community

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district was named after a local zamindar named Moulvi Muhammad Bazar.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Lawachara National Park is particularly famous for its population of which endangered primate species?
A) Capped Langur
B) Slow Loris
C) Rhesus Macaque
D) Western Hoolock Gibbon
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Western Hoolock Gibbon

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Moulvibazar is over 2.5 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Moulvibazar District in square kilometers?
A) 2,150 sq km
B) 2,799 sq km
C) 3,120 sq km
D) 3,450 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,799 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The name of the district, Moulvibazar, originated from a local preacher and merchant who established a market ('bazar'). What was his name?
A) Moulvi Syed Qudratullah
B) Moulvi Ibrahim
C) Shah Mustafa
D) Hazrat Syed Ahmed
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Moulvi Syed Qudratullah

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] During the 1971 Liberation War, the 'Battle of Gazipur' in Kulaura upazila was a significant confrontation where the Pakistani army suffered heavy losses.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the South Sylhet (Dakshin Sylhet) subdivision renamed to Moulvibazar?
A) 1947
B) 1960
C) 1971
D) 1984
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1960

Q7. [MCQ] Sreemangal holds the record for the lowest temperature ever recorded in Bangladesh.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Manipuri people primarily migrated to the greater Sylhet region following a Burmese invasion of their kingdom in the 18th century.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Gour Govinda Fort' is an ancient archaeological site that dates back to the pre-Sultanate period.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district has the highest number of tea gardens of any district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== SUNAMGANJ ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Sunamganj is a district in the northeastern part of Bangladesh, belonging to which division?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Mymensingh Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Sylhet Division
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sylhet Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is famous for its vast wetlands, which are locally known as "haors."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The Tanguar Haor, a major wetland and Ramsar site, is located in which district?
A) Kishoreganj
B) Habiganj
C) Sunamganj
D) Moulvibazar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sunamganj

Q4. [MCQ] The mystic poet and Baul singer Hason Raja, known for his philosophical songs, was born in which district?
A) Sylhet
B) Kushtia
C) Kishoreganj
D) Sunamganj
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sunamganj

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Sunamganj shares a long border with the Indian state of Meghalaya.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] What is the main river that flows through Sunamganj town?
A) Kushiara
B) Khowai
C) Surma
D) Manu
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Surma

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main agricultural crop of the haor region?
A) Jute
B) Boro Rice
C) Wheat
D) Sugarcane
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Boro Rice

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous folk singer Shah Abdul Karim, known as the "Baul Samrat," was born in Sunamganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The district headquarters is a town also named Sunamganj.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Sunamganj is a major industrial district with many large factories.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Sunamganj established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Before becoming a district, Sunamganj was a subdivision under the greater Sylhet district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Sunamganj district?
A) 9
B) 11
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 12

Q4. [MCQ] The shrine of which famous companion of Hazrat Shah Jalal (R) is located at Shaharpara in Sunamganj?
A) Shah Paran
B) Shah Malum
C) Shah Kamal
D) It is not in Sunamganj.
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shah Malum

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The Tanguar Haor is designated as a "Ramsar Site," which means it is a wetland of international importance.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The limestone required for the Lafarge Surma Cement Plant is transported via a long conveyor belt from which Indian state?
A) Assam
B) Tripura
C) West Bengal
D) Meghalaya
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Meghalaya

Q7. [MCQ] Abdus Samad Azad, one of the key organizers of the Liberation War and a former foreign minister, was from which upazila of Sunamganj?
A) Sunamganj Sadar
B) Derai
C) Jagannathpur
D) Chhatak
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jagannathpur

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Dhamail' is a traditional form of folk music and dance, particularly popular during weddings in the Sunamganj region.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Tekergat' limestone quarry is located in which upazila?
A) Bishwambarpur
B) Tahirpur
C) Dowarabazar
D) Jamalganj
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Tahirpur

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Sunamganj is one of the lowest in the Sylhet Division.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The historic 'Nankar Rebellion' of 1948-49 was a peasant movement against an oppressive land tenure system prevalent in which region?
A) North Bengal
B) The Chittagong Hill Tracts
C) Greater Sylhet
D) The Barind Tract
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Greater Sylhet

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Sunamganj is over 3 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Sunamganj District in square kilometers?
A) 2,980 sq km
B) 3,350 sq km
C) 3,747 sq km
D) 4,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3,747 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Hason Raja Museum, dedicated to the mystic poet, is located on the bank of which river in Sunamganj town?
A) Kushiara
B) Surma
C) Kalni
D) Jadukata
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Surma

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The geology of the haor basin is primarily a saucer-shaped depression that is a part of the Indo-Gangetic Plain's tectonic foredeep.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The famous folk singer and composer Radharaman Dutta was born in which upazila?
A) Sunamganj Sadar
B) Chhatak
C) Derai
D) Jagannathpur
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Jagannathpur

Q7. [MCQ] During the Liberation War of 1971, the 'Battle of Sreepur-Gobindapur' was a major engagement that took place in which upazila?
A) Tahirpur
B) Dowarabazar
C) Dharmapasha
D) Bishwambarpur
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dowarabazar

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Sunamganj was the first subdivision to be established in the Sylhet region by the British.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Jadukata River, known for its clear water and the collection of stones and sand, originates from which hills in India?
A) Garo Hills
B) Khasi Hills
C) Lushai Hills
D) Jaintia Hills
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khasi Hills

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Sunamganj was liberated from Pakistani forces on December 6, 1971.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== BANDARBAN ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Bandarban is a hilly district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Sylhet Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Bandarban is home to some of the highest mountain peaks in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the famous lake, known for its natural beauty, located in Bandarban?
A) Kaptai Lake
B) Foy's Lake
C) Boga Lake
D) Dighinala Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Boga Lake

Q4. [MCQ] Which of the following is the main river that flows through Bandarban?
A) Karnaphuli
B) Sangu (Shankha)
C) Matamuhuri
D) Feni
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sangu (Shankha)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] A large number of different ethnic minority groups, often referred to as 'Pahari', live in Bandarban.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Nilgiri' is a famous tourist resort known for its panoramic views of hills and clouds.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural practice in the hills of Bandarban?
A) Tea cultivation
B) Jhum cultivation (slash-and-burn)
C) Wheat farming
D) Sugarcane plantation
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Jhum cultivation (slash-and-burn)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bandarban shares a border with both India and Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Buddha Dhatu Jadi, a large Buddhist temple also known as the "Golden Temple," is a major landmark in which district?
A) Cox's Bazar
B) Rangamati
C) Khagrachari
D) Bandarban
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bandarban

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The name 'Bandarban' means "dam of the monkeys."
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The grave of which Bir Shrestha, a hero of the 1971 Liberation War, is located in the Chittagong Hill Tracts?
A) Hamidur Rahman
B) Mohiuddin Jahangir
C) Mostafa Kamal
D) Munshi Abdur Rouf
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Munshi Abdur Rouf

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Tazing Dong is officially recognized as the highest peak in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Bandarban district?
A) 5
B) 7
C) 9
D) 11
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 7

Q4. [MCQ] Which is the largest ethnic group residing in Bandarban?
A) Chakma
B) Tripura
C) Tanchangya
D) Marma
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Marma

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The administrative head of the traditional governance system in Bandarban is the Bohmong Circle Chief.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Sangrai' festival, featuring water splashing events, is the main traditional celebration of which community?
A) The Mro community
B) The Bawm community
C) The Marma community
D) The Chakma community
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Marma community

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Nafakhum' waterfall is a popular tourist destination on which river?
A) Sangu
B) Remakri (a tributary of Sangu)
C) Matamuhuri
D) Bakkhali
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Remakri (a tributary of Sangu)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Before 1981, Bandarban was a part of the greater Rangamati district.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was a subdivision of the Chittagong Hill Tracts district).

Q9. [MCQ] What is the name of the highest roadway in Bangladesh, which connects Thanchi and Alikadam?
A) Nilgiri Road
B) Dim Pahar Road
C) Chimbuk Road
D) Ruma-Boga Lake Road
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Dim Pahar Road

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Bandarban is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] According to official measurements, what is the approximate height of Tazing Dong peak?
A) 829 meters
B) 986 meters
C) 1,052 meters
D) 1,280 meters
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 1,280 meters

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chittagong Hill Tracts Peace Accord, aimed at ending the decades-long insurgency, was signed in 1997.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Bandarban District in square kilometers, making it one of the largest districts by area?
A) 3,120 sq km
B) 3,890 sq km
C) 4,479 sq km
D) 5,150 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 4,479 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Mro' ethnic group in Bandarban is unique for having their own:
A) Monarchy
B) Written script and alphabet
C) Naval fleet
D) Currency
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Written script and alphabet

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, Bandarban has the lowest population of any district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Buddha Dhatu Jadi (Golden Temple) contains a sacred relic believed to be from which disciple of Gautama Buddha?
A) Ananda
B) Sariputta
C) Moggallana
D) Kassapa
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Sariputta

Q7. [MCQ] During the British Raj, the Chittagong Hill Tracts were administered under a special regulation known as the:
A) CHT Regulation of 1900
B) Hill Tracts Act of 1881
C) Bengal Tenancy Act of 1885
D) Forest Act of 1927
CORRECT ANSWER: A) CHT Regulation of 1900

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sangu Matamuhuri Reserve Forest in Bandarban is one of the last remaining habitats for the Asian elephant in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Keokradong' peak is located on the border of which two upazilas?
A) Thanchi and Alikadam
B) Ruma and Thanchi
C) Lama and Ruma
D) Bandarban Sadar and Rowangchhari
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ruma and Thanchi

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Bandarban was established as a separate district in 1981.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== KHAGRACHARI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Khagrachari is a hilly district that is part of which administrative division?
A) Sylhet Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The district is known for its many valleys and the Chengi river that flows through it.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous natural cave and tourist spot in Khagrachari?
A) Boga Lake
B) Ali's Tunnel (Alutila)
C) Nafakhum Waterfall
D) Rema-Kalenga
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Ali's Tunnel (Alutila)

Q4. [MCQ] Which is the largest ethnic minority group in Khagrachari district?
A) Marma
B) Chakma
C) Tripura
D) Tanchangya
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Chakma

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Khagrachari shares a border with the country of Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q6. [MCQ] What does the name 'Khagrachari' mean?
A) Golden Hills
B) River of Reeds
C) Field of Reeds
D) Three Streams
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Field of Reeds

Q7. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major agricultural product of Khagrachari?
A) Tea
B) Jute
C) Jackfruit and Pineapple
D) Wheat
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Jackfruit and Pineapple

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Biju' festival is the main traditional celebration of the Chakma people.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Hajachora-Toiduchora' are famous waterfalls located in which upazila?
A) Khagrachari Sadar
B) Panchhari
C) Dighinala
D) Matiranga
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dighinala

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The district headquarters is a town also named Khagrachari.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Khagrachari established as a separate district?
A) 1981
B) 1983
C) 1985
D) 1987
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1983

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The traditional administrative system in Khagrachari is headed by the Mong Circle Chief.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It is the Chakma Circle Chief).

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Khagrachari district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Khagrachari was a subdivision under which administrative unit?
A) The greater Comilla district
B) The greater Chittagong district
C) The Chittagong Hill Tracts district
D) The Noakhali district
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Chittagong Hill Tracts district

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'New Zealand Para' is a scenic area in Khagrachari known for its lush green, organized landscape.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Ramgarh subdivision, now an upazila of Khagrachari, was historically the first headquarters of which district?
A) Chittagong
B) Chittagong Hill Tracts
C) Feni
D) Rangamati
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Chittagong Hill Tracts

Q7. [MCQ] Which of these is a major river valley that defines the geography of Khagrachari?
A) Sangu Valley
B) Karnaphuli Valley
C) Chengi Valley
D) Matamuhuri Valley
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chengi Valley

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Khagrachari is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Baisabi' festival is a collective term for the New Year celebrations of which three major ethnic groups?
A) Chakma, Marma, Garo
B) Chakma, Marma, Tripura
C) Santal, Oraon, Munda
D) Marma, Mro, Bawm
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Chakma, Marma, Tripura

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Khagrachari shares its international border with the Indian state of Tripura.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The traditional head of the Chakma people, who holds administrative and social authority in the Chakma Circle, is known as the:
A) Bohmong Chief
B) Mong Chief
C) Chakma Raja (King)
D) Headman
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chakma Raja (King)

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Chittagong Hill Tracts Regulation of 1900 granted a special administrative status to the region, restricting land ownership by non-tribal people.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Khagrachari District in square kilometers?
A) 2,150 sq km
B) 2,749 sq km
C) 3,010 sq km
D) 3,450 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,749 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Khagrachari Cantonment' was established as a key military installation in the region after which major event?
A) The end of British rule in 1947
B) The start of the insurgency in the 1970s
C) The 1971 Liberation War
D) The Chittagong Hill Tracts Peace Accord
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The start of the insurgency in the 1970s

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, the ethnic minority population constitutes the majority of the total population in Khagrachari district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Sajek Valley', a very popular tourist destination, is administratively in Rangamati but is primarily accessed through which upazila of Khagrachari?
A) Khagrachari Sadar
B) Mahalchhari
C) Dighinala
D) Lakshmichhari
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Dighinala

Q7. [MCQ] During the Liberation War of 1971, the Ramgarh area was the site of the first training camp for the freedom fighters of the Hill Tracts.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The soil in Khagrachari's valleys is primarily composed of sandy loam and is suitable for growing ginger and turmeric.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Khagrachari subdivision was formed in which year?
A) 1947
B) 1960
C) 1971
D) 1976
CORRECT ANSWER: D) 1976

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'System of Three Chiefs' (Chakma, Bohmong, and Mong) was formally recognized and empowered by the British administration.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

=== BAGERHAT ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Bagerhat is a district in which administrative division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Barisal Division
C) Khulna Division
D) Rajshahi Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic Sixty Dome Mosque (Shat Gombuj Masjid) is located in Bagerhat.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] The historic Mosque City of Bagerhat was founded by which Turkish general and saint in the 15th century?
A) Shah Jalal
B) Khan Jahan Ali
C) Shah Makhdum
D) Bayazid Bostami
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Khan Jahan Ali

Q4. [MCQ] A large portion of which famous UNESCO World Heritage Site is located in Bagerhat district?
A) The ruins of Paharpur
B) The Sundarbans
C) The historic city of Gauda
D) The Mainamati ruins
CORRECT ANSWER: B) The Sundarbans

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] Mongla, the second-largest seaport of Bangladesh, is located in Bagerhat district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The mausoleum (shrine) of Khan Jahan Ali is a major pilgrimage site in which district?
A) Khulna
B) Satkhira
C) Jessore
D) Bagerhat
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bagerhat

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the large, historic water tank located in front of Khan Jahan Ali's tomb?
A) Ramsagar Dighi
B) Dharmasagar Dighi
C) Ghora Dighi
D) Kamlasagar Dighi
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Ghora Dighi

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Bagerhat is famous for its large tea plantations.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] Which of the following is a major industry in Bagerhat, besides activities related to the port?
A) Ready-made garments
B) Shrimp farming and processing
C) Leather tanning
D) Steel manufacturing
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Shrimp farming and processing

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The Pasur River is one of the main rivers flowing through Bagerhat district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was the Mosque City of Bagerhat inscribed as a UNESCO World Heritage Site?
A) 1979
B) 1982
C) 1985
D) 1997
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1985

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The Sixty Dome Mosque actually has 77 domes in total, not 60.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Bagerhat district?
A) 7
B) 9
C) 11
D) 13
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 9

Q4. [MCQ] What was the historical name of the city founded by Khan Jahan Ali?
A) Fatehabad
B) Jahangirnagar
C) Khalifatabad
D) Shujabad
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khalifatabad

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The crocodiles in the pond at Khan Jahan Ali's shrine are believed by devotees to be sacred.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Nine Dome Mosque' is another historic architectural monument located near which other famous site?
A) The Sundarbans
B) Mongla Port
C) The Sixty Dome Mosque
D) Bagerhat Town
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The Sixty Dome Mosque

Q7. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Bagerhat was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Jessore
B) Barisal
C) Khulna
D) Faridpur
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Khulna

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The architectural style of the Sixty Dome Mosque shows influences of Tughlaq architecture from Delhi.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The Rampal Power Station, a major energy project, is a joint venture between Bangladesh and which country?
A) China
B) Russia
C) Japan
D) India
CORRECT ANSWER: D) India

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Bagerhat district is higher than the national average.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Bagerhat officially established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, the population of Bagerhat district is over 2 million.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Bagerhat District in square kilometers?
A) 2,980 sq km
B) 3,550 sq km
C) 3,959 sq km
D) 4,320 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 3,959 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The tomb of which associate of Khan Jahan Ali is located in the 'Nine Dome Mosque' complex?
A) Zinda Pir
B) Bakhtiyar Khan
C) Burhan Khan
D) There is no known tomb in the complex.
CORRECT ANSWER: D) There is no known tomb in the complex.

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The walls of the Sixty Dome Mosque are unusually thick, tapering upwards, which is a feature designed to support the weight of the numerous domes.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The Bagerhat subdivision was established in which year?
A) 1842
B) 1863
C) 1882
D) 1905
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1863

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Kodla Math' in Bagerhat Sadar upazila is a towering Hindu temple noted for its unique:
A) Terracotta ornamentation
B) Single-spired ('rekha deul') design
C) Use of white marble
D) Numerous domes
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Single-spired ('rekha deul') design

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War of 1971, the battle at the Bagerhat Circuit House was a significant engagement between the Mukti Bahini and the Pakistani army.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The soil in the southern part of Bagerhat, bordering the Sundarbans, is part of which geological tract, characterized by high salinity?
A) Ganges Tidal Floodplain
B) Barind Tract
C) Madhupur Tract
D) Himalayan Piedmont Plain
CORRECT ANSWER: A) Ganges Tidal Floodplain

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The UNESCO inscription for the Mosque City of Bagerhat specifically mentions around 50 monuments from the Sultanate period.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== COX'S BAZAR ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Cox's Bazar is a district located in which division of Bangladesh?
A) Dhaka Division
B) Sylhet Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Barisal Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar is famous for having the longest natural sea beach in the world.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] Which of the following is a famous coral island and major tourist destination in Bangladesh, accessible from Cox's Bazar?
A) Hatiya Island
B) Sandwip Island
C) Bhola Island
D) St. Martin's Island
CORRECT ANSWER: D) St. Martin's Island

Q4. [MCQ] What is the name of the main river that flows into the sea at Cox's Bazar town?
A) Karnaphuli
B) Sangu
C) Matamuhuri
D) Bakkhali
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Bakkhali

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The district was named after Hiram Cox, an officer of the British East India Company.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Besides tourism, what is another major economic activity in Cox's Bazar?
A) Tea production
B) Jute processing
C) Sea fishing and salt production
D) Leather tanning
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Sea fishing and salt production

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Himchari National Park' is a popular eco-tourism spot known for its hills and waterfalls, located near which beach?
A) Patenga Beach
B) Kuakata Beach
C) Cox's Bazar Beach
D) Parki Beach
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Cox's Bazar Beach

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar shares a border with the country of India.
CORRECT ANSWER: False

Q9. [MCQ] What is the local name for the dried fish (shutki) which is a famous product of Cox's Bazar?
A) Ilish
B) Puti
C) Loitta
D) Chingri
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Loitta

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] Inani Beach is famous for its golden sand and calm waters.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It's famous for its rocky corals).
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] In which year was Cox's Bazar established as a district?
A) 1971
B) 1979
C) 1984
D) 1988
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1984

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The historic name of Cox's Bazar was "Palongkee."
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Cox's Bazar district?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 8

Q4. [MCQ] Before becoming a district, Cox's Bazar was a subdivision under which greater district?
A) Noakhali
B) Comilla
C) Chittagong
D) Rangamati
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The large Rohingya refugee camps, some of the biggest in the world, are located in the Ukhiya and Teknaf upazilas of Cox's Bazar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] The 'Aggmeda Khyang' in Cox's Bazar town is a large monastery belonging to which religious community?
A) Hindu
B) Christian
C) Buddhist
D) Animist
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Buddhist

Q7. [MCQ] What is the name of the southernmost point of mainland Bangladesh, located in Cox's Bazar?
A) Kuakata
B) St. Martin's Island
C) Teknaf
D) Shah Porir Dwip
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Shah Porir Dwip

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Cox's Bazar is one of the lowest in the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The 'Dulahazara Safari Park', the first of its kind in Bangladesh, is located in which upazila?
A) Cox's Bazar Sadar
B) Ramu
C) Chakaria
D) Pekua
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chakaria

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The marine drive road from Cox's Bazar to Teknaf is considered one of the most scenic drives in the country.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] What is the approximate length of the main uninterrupted sandy beach in Cox's Bazar?
A) 80 km
B) 100 km
C) 120 km
D) 150 km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 120 km

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 Census, Cox's Bazar district has a higher population density than the neighboring Bandarban district.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Cox's Bazar District in square kilometers?
A) 1,980 sq km
B) 2,491 sq km
C) 2,850 sq km
D) 3,120 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 2,491 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] Captain Hiram Cox was sent to the region in the late 18th century to deal with a conflict between Arakanese refugees and which local community?
A) The Mughals
B) The British
C) The local Rakhine people
D) The Chakma people
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The local Rakhine people

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The 'Sonadia Island' near Cox's Bazar is a critical habitat for migratory birds and is designated as an Ecologically Critical Area.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was the Cox's Bazar subdivision established?
A) 1854
B) 1874
C) 1901
D) 1959
CORRECT ANSWER: A) 1854

Q7. [MCQ] The historic 'Adinath Temple' is located on top of a hill on which island near Cox's Bazar?
A) St. Martin's Island
B) Sonadia Island
C) Kutubdia Island
D) Moheshkhali Island
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Moheshkhali Island

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Cox's Bazar is the only district in Bangladesh that has a border with Myanmar but not with India.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The first international chain hotel to open in Cox's Bazar was:
A) The Westin
B) Radisson Blu
C) The Marriott
D) Sayeman Beach Resort (rebuilt as international standard)
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Sayeman Beach Resort (rebuilt as international standard)

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] During the Liberation War, the Pakistani navy used the Cox's Bazar airport as a major base, which was targeted by the Indian Air Force.
CORRECT ANSWER: True
=== RANGAMATI ===
EASY LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] Rangamati is a hilly district in which administrative division?
A) Sylhet Division
B) Dhaka Division
C) Chittagong Division
D) Mymensingh Division
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chittagong Division

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] By area, Rangamati is the largest district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the name of the large, man-made lake that is the most prominent feature of Rangamati?
A) Boga Lake
B) Foy's Lake
C) Mahamaya Lake
D) Kaptai Lake
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Kaptai Lake

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Jhum' cultivation (slash-and-burn agriculture) is a traditional practice of the indigenous people of Rangamati.
A) True
B) False
CORRECT ANSWER: A) True

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The famous 'Shuvolong' waterfall is a popular tourist attraction in Rangamati.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] Which is the largest ethnic minority group residing in Rangamati?
A) Marma
B) Tripura
C) Tanchangya
D) Chakma
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Chakma

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Hanging Bridge' (Jhulonto Shetu) is an iconic landmark of which district?
A) Bandarban
B) Khagrachari
C) Rangamati
D) Cox's Bazar
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Rangamati

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Kaptai Hydroelectric Power Plant, the only one of its kind in Bangladesh, is located in Rangamati.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the main river that was dammed to create Kaptai Lake?
A) Sangu
B) Chengi
C) Feni
D) Karnaphuli
CORRECT ANSWER: D) Karnaphuli

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The traditional head of the Chakma people is known as the Chakma Raja (King).
CORRECT ANSWER: True
MEDIUM LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The Kaptai Dam was constructed in which decade, leading to the creation of Kaptai Lake?
A) 1940s
B) 1950s
C) 1960s
D) 1970s
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 1960s

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The creation of Kaptai Lake submerged a vast area of arable land and displaced a large number of the Chakma population.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] How many upazilas are there in the Rangamati district?
A) 8
B) 10
C) 12
D) 14
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 10

Q4. [MCQ] The 'Rajban Vihara' is a large and famous monastery in Rangamati belonging to which religion?
A) Hinduism
B) Christianity
C) Buddhism
D) Animism
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Buddhism

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] The grave of Bir Shrestha Lance Naik Munshi Abdur Rouf is located on an island in Kaptai Lake.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] 'Biju', 'Sangrai', and 'Baisu' are the names of the New Year festivals celebrated by which communities, respectively?
A) Marma, Chakma, Tripura
B) Chakma, Marma, Garo
C) Chakma, Marma, Tripura
D) Santal, Oraon, Munda
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Chakma, Marma, Tripura

Q7. [MCQ] The 'Sajek Valley', a famous tourist destination, is administratively under which upazila of Rangamati?
A) Rangamati Sadar
B) Kaptai
C) Baghaichhari
D) Belaichhari
CORRECT ANSWER: C) Baghaichhari

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] Rangamati shares a border with both India and Myanmar.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] What is the main product of the 'Karnaphuli Paper Mills', located near Kaptai?
A) Newsprint
B) High-quality writing paper
C) Cardboard
D) Tissue paper
CORRECT ANSWER: B) High-quality writing paper

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] The literacy rate of Rangamati is higher than that of the other two hill districts (Bandarban and Khagrachari).
CORRECT ANSWER: True
HARD LEVEL (10 Questions)

Q1. [MCQ] The construction of the Kaptai Dam was completed in which year?
A) 1958
B) 1962
C) 1965
D) 1968
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1962

Q2. [TRUE/FALSE] The original palace of the Chakma King was submerged by the waters of Kaptai Lake.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q3. [MCQ] What is the approximate total area of Rangamati District in square kilometers?
A) 4,120 sq km
B) 5,450 sq km
C) 6,116 sq km
D) 6,890 sq km
CORRECT ANSWER: C) 6,116 sq km

Q4. [MCQ] The Chittagong Hill Tracts Peace Accord was signed between the government of Bangladesh and which political group representing the indigenous people?
A) United People's Democratic Front (UPDF)
B) Parbatya Chattagram Jana Samhati Samiti (PCJSS)
C) Hill Students' Council
D) Chakma Circle Council
CORRECT ANSWER: B) Parbatya Chattagram Jana Samhati Samiti (PCJSS)

Q5. [TRUE/FALSE] According to the 2022 census, Rangamati has the lowest population density of any district in Bangladesh.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q6. [MCQ] In which year was Rangamati established as a separate district?
A) 1981
B) 1983
C) 1985
D) 1987
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1983

Q7. [MCQ] The Kaptai Dam project was primarily funded and technically supported by which country's development agency?
A) The Soviet Union
B) The United Kingdom
C) The United States (USAID)
D) Japan (JICA)
CORRECT ANSWER: C) The United States (USAID)

Q8. [TRUE/FALSE] The Pablakhali Wildlife Sanctuary is a protected forest area located in the northern part of Rangamati.
CORRECT ANSWER: True

Q9. [MCQ] The traditional administrative system of the three Hill districts is based on the CHT Regulation of which year?
A) 1881
B) 1900
C) 1927
D) 1947
CORRECT ANSWER: B) 1900

Q10. [TRUE/FALSE] During the British Raj, the headquarters of the Chittagong Hill Tracts was first established in Rangamati before being moved to Chittagong.
CORRECT ANSWER: False (It was first at Chandraghona, then moved to Rangamati).
